## Rate Limits

Every write endpoint that calls `checkRateLimit` returns HTTP `429` (or a tool-level error with `code: "RATE_LIMITED"` inside the MCP JSON-RPC envelope) with:
- `retryAfterSeconds` — seconds until the window resets
- `limit` — the ceiling for the window
- `windowSeconds` — length of the window
- `Retry-After` header on HTTP responses (per RFC 9110)

Clients (including AI agents) should parse `retryAfterSeconds` and back off. Do NOT sleep a fixed 30s — use the returned value.

| Endpoint / bucket | Limit | Window |
|---|---|---|
| `/api/mcp` (per API key / OAuth token) | 100 | 1 hr |
| `/api/mcp/oauth/token` (per client_id) | 60 | 1 hr |
| `/api/mcp/oauth/register` (per IP) | 10 | 1 hr |
| `send_bulk_email` MCP tool (per event) | 10 | 1 hr |
| `research_sponsor` MCP tool (per user+event) | 30 | 1 hr |
| `speaker-agreement-template` upload (per user) | 10 | 1 hr |
| Public register — burst (per IP) | 15 | 60 s |
| Public register — sustained (per IP) | 100 | 15 min |
| Public register — per email address | 10 | 15 min |
| Public checkout (per IP) | 15 | 60 s |
| Public register preflight `check-email` (per IP) | 200 | 1 hr |
| Public `zoom-join` (per IP) | 60 | 1 hr |
| Mobile login/refresh (per IP) | 10 | 5 min |

Thresholds are best-effort; in-memory store means limits reset on EC2/Docker restart. For stricter SLAs migrate to Redis (Vercel KV / Upstash) — the `checkRateLimit` interface is store-agnostic.

## Role-Based Access Control (RBAC)

### Roles
- **SUPER_ADMIN / ADMIN** - Full access to all features (org-bound)
- **ORGANIZER** - Full access to assigned events (org-bound)
- **MEMBER** - Org-bound **read-only viewer**. Same event scope as ORGANIZER (sees all org events) but **every** write is blocked (`denyReviewer()` includes MEMBER → all non-abstract POST/PUT/DELETE return 403) — EXCEPT the registration-desk opt-ins (`REGISTRATION_DESK_ALLOW` includes MEMBER: add registration, check-in, badge, record payment). **⚠ Doc-drift corrected July 10, 2026 (payments review L3): MEMBER has been finance-CAPABLE since the June 17 'desk staff record payments' decision** — `FINANCE_ROLES` in [src/lib/finance-visibility.ts](src/lib/finance-visibility.ts) is `SUPER_ADMIN/ADMIN/ORGANIZER/MEMBER/ONSITE` (fails closed for unknown roles), so MEMBER SEES money and `redactFinancialFields()`/`denyFinance()` no longer fire for it. The historical description below reflects the pre-June-17 model: `denyFinance()` 403s MEMBER on invoice list/detail/PDF + quote PDF GET routes; the registration-detail / tickets / event GET APIs run `redactFinancialFields()` for MEMBER (strips amounts, invoices, billing, bank/tax, prices — **keeps `paymentStatus`**, which is operational not financial); the agent refuses `FINANCE_ONLY_AGENT_TOOLS` (`list_invoices`, `list_unpaid_registrations`) for MEMBER and redacts financial fields from mixed tool results; the registration detail-sheet hides the Billing & Payments tab and the Tickets page renders `—` for masked prices. **Can use the AI Agent in read-only mode** — the route allows MEMBER but `isReadOnlyTool()` refuses anything not matching `list_`/`get_`/`search_` (fails closed). Intended for leadership / auditors / sponsor-side stakeholders who need operational visibility without edit rights or money. Invited via Settings → Users like ADMIN/ORGANIZER. Amber badge in the UI.
- **REVIEWER** - Abstracts-only access to assigned events (org-independent, scoped by `event.settings.reviewerUserIds`)
- **SUBMITTER** - Abstracts-only access to own submissions (org-independent, scoped by `Speaker.userId`)
- **REGISTRANT** - Self-service access to own registrations only (org-independent **unless internal-domain — see below**, scoped by `Registration.userId`); can edit personal details, view payment status, make payments via Stripe; no dashboard/events access
- **CRM_USER** - Org-bound **sales-team role, CONFINED to the CRM** (sponsorship pipeline). Added July 15, 2026 (additive enum migration `20260715070000_add_crm_user_role`). Can **fully work the CRM** — own deals, companies, CRM contacts, tasks, notes, reports, CSV export — and **sees deal values** (`canViewDealValues` includes it), but is walled off from everything else: no events, registrations, speakers, invoices, or settings. **NOT in `FINANCE_ROLES`** — it sees CRM *deal* money, not event invoices/registration payments (different money; the CRM has its own visibility predicates in [src/crm/lib/crm-roles.ts](src/crm/lib/crm-roles.ts) — `canViewCrm`/`canOwnDeals`/`canViewDealValues`). Enforced in depth: (1) **Event access** — [buildEventAccessWhere](src/lib/event-access.ts) returns `{ id: { in: [] } }` (zero events); the CRM's deal/report event picker uses the name-only `GET /api/crm/events-lite` instead. (2) **API** — in `denyReviewer`'s restricted set (blocked from all non-CRM writes); the `/api/crm/*` routes gate via their own `requireCrmWrite` → `canOwnDeals`. It IS in `canViewContacts` (owner decision) so it can search the event contact store to link a rep to their registration. (3) **Middleware** ([src/proxy.ts](src/proxy.ts)) — redirects it to `/crm` from every non-CRM dashboard path. (4) **UI** — sidebar shows only the CRM entry; header "CRM User" badge (green). Org-bound team member (`TEAM_ROLES`), invited from **Settings → Users**.
- **ONSITE** - Org-bound **registration-desk staff**, scoped **PER EVENT** (per-event model July 7, 2026; role added June 16, 2026). A temp desk worker is assigned to specific events and sees/acts on **only those events** — NOT every event in the org. Assignment lives in **`Event.settings.onsiteUserIds`** (JSON array, mirroring `reviewerUserIds`), managed from the **Settings → Onsite Staff** tab (create a temp account + assign to event(s), remove-from-event, delete account; one temp can span multiple events). Can ONLY: **add a registration**, **check attendees in**, **view the registrations list**, and **print badges** — for assigned events. **Undo (July 11, 2026, `706ba17`):** the desk can reverse a mistaken check-in via `DELETE .../check-in` → `undoCheckIn()` in [check-in.ts](src/lib/check-in.ts), which clears status + `checkedInAt` together (audited `CHECK_IN_UNDO`, no seat change). An 'Undo Check-in' button appears on the registration detail sheet when CHECKED_IN. **NB — do NOT 'undo' by hand-flipping status:** that leaves `checkedInAt` set and `checkInGate` then refuses the attendee forever with ALREADY_CHECKED_IN. **ONSITE is finance-CAPABLE** (`canViewFinance("ONSITE")` is true — `FINANCE_ROLES` includes it since the June 17 "desk staff record payments" decision), so it sees payment amounts for its assigned events (this is why the cross-event gap below also leaked payment data). Everything else is blocked. Enforced in depth: (1) **Event visibility** — [buildEventAccessWhere](src/lib/event-access.ts) ONSITE branch scopes to `settings.onsiteUserIds` (org-bound AND assigned); unassigned ⇒ zero events. (2) **API** — ONSITE is in `denyReviewer`'s restricted set; the create-registration, check-in (POST+PUT), badge-print, and payments routes opt it back in via `denyReviewer(session, { allow: REGISTRATION_DESK_ALLOW })` **AND** route their event lookup through `buildEventAccessWhere`, so an ONSITE user assigned to Event A gets a **404** on Event B's list/create/edit/check-in/badge. This is the [security fix](__tests__/api/onsite-cross-event-isolation.test.ts) for the adversarial-review BLOCKER — before it, those 5 desk routes org-scoped only, so ONSITE could operate on any event in the org. The other 27 write routes block ONSITE entirely. (3) **Middleware** ([src/proxy.ts](src/proxy.ts)) — confines ONSITE to `/events` (list, now assignment-scoped) + an event's `/registrations*` + `/check-in*` paths; the API layer is the authoritative cross-event gate (middleware can't read settings at the Edge). (4) **UI** — sidebar = Events + the event's Registrations + Check-In; header "Onsite Staff" badge; registrations list keeps Add/Print Badge/Export, hides bulk/import/share; detail sheet keeps Check In + Print Badge, hides Edit/Delete/Send Email/Download Quote. Invited from **Settings → Onsite Staff** (org admins); cyan badge. Migration `20260616120000_add_onsite_role` (additive enum). Per-event scoping is settings-JSON only (no migration).

### Architecture: Org-bound vs. Org-independent Users
- **Team members** (ADMIN, ORGANIZER, MEMBER, **ONSITE**) have a required `organizationId` and are scoped to their organization. MEMBER is the read-only variant; ONSITE is the registration-desk variant. The "team members" set is `TEAM_ROLES` in [src/lib/auth-guards.ts](src/lib/auth-guards.ts) (`isTeamRole()`); the Settings → Users list filters to it, so org-bound registrants (below) don't appear as staff.
- **Reviewers**, **Submitters**, and **Registrants** have `organizationId: null` — they are independent entities scoped only by event assignment
- This allows one reviewer to review events across multiple organizations; submitters self-register per event; registrants create accounts during public registration
- `User.organizationId` is nullable in the schema; non-null assertion (`!`) is used in admin-only code paths
- **Internal-domain rule (June 16, 2026):** registering with an **internal-domain** email ([src/lib/internal-domains.ts](src/lib/internal-domains.ts)) gets the org attached, even as a REGISTRANT. **Two tiers:** **(a) VERIFIED** — `meetingmindsdubai.com` (real mailboxes): created **org-null** at registration + sent a **verify-email link** ([src/lib/email-verification.ts](src/lib/email-verification.ts) → [/verify-email](src/app/verify-email/page.tsx) → `POST /api/auth/verify-email`); clicking it sets `User.emailVerified` **and** attaches the org. Until then they're a normal external registrant (registration works; verification only unlocks internal/org status). **(b) TRUSTED** — `meetingmindsexperts.com` / `meetingmindsgroup.com` (temp accounts, addresses may not be real mailboxes): org attached **immediately, no verification**; admins delete them from Settings → Users when done. An admin **invite/promote** is a trusted human action and works regardless of verification — the gate only governs the *automatic* org-attach at registration. So an internal person is org-bound from the start and can later be **promoted** to a team role (`POST /api/organization/users` updates an existing org-independent — or org-bound non-team — account's org + role in place, keeping its password + registrations) instead of being blocked by the global email-uniqueness check. A *different* org's user is still refused. `/my-registration` is session-scoped (not role-gated), so a promoted staff member keeps access to their own registrations.

### Restricted Role Enforcement (3-layer, applies to REVIEWER, SUBMITTER, and REGISTRANT)
1. **API Layer:** `denyReviewer(session)` guard on all POST/PUT/DELETE handlers (except abstract operations and `/api/registrant/registrations` self-edit) returns 403 for REVIEWER, SUBMITTER, and REGISTRANT
2. **Middleware Layer:** `src/proxy.ts` (Next.js middleware; renamed from `middleware.ts` in Next 16.1) redirects REVIEWER/SUBMITTER from non-abstract event routes; REGISTRANT is redirected to `/my-registration` from all dashboard routes
3. **UI Layer:** Write-action buttons hidden; sidebar hidden for REGISTRANT; header shows "Reviewer Portal", "Submitter Portal", or "Registration Portal"

### Event Scoping
- `buildEventAccessWhere(session.user)` from `src/lib/event-access.ts` scopes event queries by role
- Admins/Organizers see all org events
- Reviewers see only events where their userId is in `event.settings.reviewerUserIds` (no org filter)
- **ONSITE** sees only events where their userId is in `event.settings.onsiteUserIds` (org-bound AND assigned — the per-event registration-desk model). Every ONSITE-reachable desk route (registrations list/create, detail PUT, check-in, badge, payments) routes its event lookup through `buildEventAccessWhere`, so it's assignment-gated, not just org-gated.
- Submitters see only events where they have a linked Speaker record (`speakers.some.userId`)
- Registrants see only events where they have a linked Registration record (`registrations.some.userId`)

### Reviewer Assignment
- Reviewers are assigned per-event via `Event.settings.reviewerUserIds` (JSON array of User IDs)
- `Speaker.userId` (nullable FK) links speakers to User accounts
- The Reviewers page lets admins add reviewers via two methods: pick from speakers, or invite by email
- New reviewer accounts are created with `organizationId: null` and sent an invitation email

### Submitter Registration
- Submitters self-register via `/e/[slug]/register` (public page, no auth)
- Registration creates User (role=SUBMITTER, organizationId=null) + finds-or-creates Speaker linked to event
- After login, submitters see only the event they registered for, with access to Abstracts only
- Submitters can submit abstracts (auto-linked to their speaker record), edit own abstracts (DRAFT/SUBMITTED/REVISION_REQUESTED), and view review feedback

### Registrant Registration
- Registrants create an account during public registration at `/e/[slug]/register/[category]` (2-step form: email+password → personal details)
- Registration creates User (role=REGISTRANT, organizationId=null) and links Registration via `Registration.userId`
- Existing unlinked registrations by the same email are auto-linked to the new user account
- After login, registrants see only `/my-registration` portal with their registration details, edit form, and payment status
- If a registrant later registers as a submitter, their role can upgrade from REGISTRANT to SUBMITTER
- Self-edit API at `/api/registrant/registrations` (GET for list, PUT for attendee detail updates with ownership verification)

## Code Conventions

0. **After every code change:** Run `npm run lint` and `npx tsc --noEmit`. Fix ALL errors and warnings before considering a task complete. Do not skip this step.

1. **API Routes:** Use Promise.all for parallel queries, validate with Zod
2. **Error Handling:** Use try/catch with apiLogger for errors
3. **Auth:** All dashboard routes require authentication via `auth()`
4. **Auth Guards:** All write API routes must call `denyReviewer(session)` from `@/lib/auth-guards`
5. **Forms:** Use react-hook-form with Zod validation
6. **Toasts:** Use sonner for notifications
7. **State:** Use React Query for server state, local useState for UI state
8. **Data Fetching:** Use hooks from `src/hooks/use-api.ts` for client-side data
9. **Guard clauses, not nested `if`s:** Prefer early returns — flatten `if (cond) { …body… }` into `if (!cond) return; …body…` so the happy path reads un-indented. Keep to ~one level of nesting; when a branch grows its own sub-branches, extract it into its own function (e.g. the cert worker's reissue branch → `processReissueRun`). Prefer a small guard-clause helper over a nested ternary (e.g. `cohortTagFilter`). JSX conditional rendering (`cond ? <A/> : <B/>`) is exempt.
10. **Log every failure path:** No silent `400/403/404/409/429/500`s or `.catch(()=>{})`. Every `safeParse`→400 logs the field errors; every rejection returned as an error-value is logged at the route boundary with its code. Errors log at `error`, business rejections at `warn`, successes at `info`. Logging is a hard requirement.

## Performance Optimization

### API Routes
- **Parallel queries:** Use `Promise.all()` for independent database calls
  ```typescript
  const [session, event, tickets] = await Promise.all([
    auth(),
    db.event.findFirst({ where: { id } }),
    db.ticketType.findMany({ where: { eventId: id } })
  ]);
  ```
- **Select only needed fields:** Use Prisma `select` instead of returning full objects
  ```typescript
  db.event.findFirst({
    where: { id },
    select: { id: true, name: true, status: true }  // Not the entire record
  });
  ```
- **Cache headers:** Add appropriate cache headers for public endpoints
  ```typescript
  response.headers.set("Cache-Control", "private, max-age=0, stale-while-revalidate=30");
  ```

### Database
- Use indexes for frequently queried fields (already defined in schema)
- Composite indexes on `Registration` for common query patterns: `[eventId, status]` and `[eventId, ticketTypeId]`
- Avoid N+1 queries - use `include` for related data in single query
- Use `findFirst` instead of `findUnique` when filtering by non-unique fields
- Don't add explicit `@@index` on fields that already have `@unique` (unique creates an implicit index)
- **Event existence checks:** Always use `select: { id: true }` when the event lookup only validates access (don't fetch full event objects)
- **Parallelize independent queries:** Event lookup + entity lookup should use `Promise.all()` when they don't depend on each other

### Server Pages
- **Parallelize `params` + `auth()`:** Always use `Promise.all([params, auth()])` in server page functions
- **Parallelize independent DB queries:** When a page needs both an event and related data (e.g., speakers), fetch them in parallel with `Promise.all` after auth
- **Use `select` over `include`:** Server pages should use Prisma `select` to fetch only columns rendered in the template, not full objects

### Frontend
- Use `Suspense` boundaries for loading states
- Lazy load heavy components with `dynamic()` imports
- Minimize client-side state; prefer server components where possible

### Build & Module Optimization

The project uses several optimizations to reduce module load times:

**Next.js Config** (`next.config.ts`):
- `optimizePackageImports` - Tree-shakes large packages like `lucide-react` (44MB), Radix UI, and `@tiptap/*`
- `serverExternalPackages` - Excludes `pdfkit` from bundling (Turbopack rewrites `__dirname` to `/ROOT/`, breaking font file resolution)
- `transpilePackages` - Better tree-shaking for `@getbrevo/brevo`
- `turbopack` - Faster builds with Next.js 16's default bundler

**Lazy Initialization Patterns**:
- **Brevo SDK** (`src/lib/email.ts`): Uses named imports instead of wildcard (`import * as brevo`), API client lazy-initialized on first use
  ```typescript
  // Good - named imports, lazy init
  import { TransactionalEmailsApi, SendSmtpEmail } from "@getbrevo/brevo";
  let apiInstance: TransactionalEmailsApi | null = null;
  function getApiInstance() { /* create on first call */ }

  // Bad - loads entire SDK at module load
  import * as brevo from "@getbrevo/brevo";
  const apiInstance = new brevo.TransactionalEmailsApi();
  ```
- **Logger** (`src/lib/logger.ts`): No synchronous file system operations at module load; pino transports handle directory creation

**Prisma Client** (`src/lib/db.ts`):
- Singleton pattern with `globalThis` caching in development only (prevents HMR connection leaks)
- In production (Vercel), each serverless function gets its own instance — no global caching needed

**Middleware** (`src/proxy.ts`, renamed from `middleware.ts` in Next 16.1):
- Matcher scoped to only dashboard routes (`/events/*`, `/dashboard/*`, `/settings/*`)
- Redirects REVIEWER and SUBMITTER from non-abstract event routes to `/events/[eventId]/abstracts`
- Public routes (`/e/*`), API routes (`/api/*`), auth pages, `/uploads/*`, and static assets skip middleware entirely

**Header Component** (`src/components/layout/header.tsx`):
- Uses React Query hooks (`useEvents`, `useEvent`) instead of manual `useEffect` fetching
- Data cached across navigation, preventing duplicate API calls

### React Query (Client-Side Caching)
Dashboard pages use React Query for client-side data caching. This provides:
- **Instant navigation:** Cached data displays immediately when returning to pages
- **Background refresh:** Data updates silently while showing cached content
- **Optimistic UI:** Mutations update cache immediately for responsive feel

**Configuration** (`src/components/providers.tsx`):
- `staleTime: 5 minutes` - Data considered fresh for 5 minutes
- `gcTime: 30 minutes` - Unused cache kept for 30 minutes
- `refetchOnWindowFocus: true` - Refresh when tab becomes active

**Using React Query hooks** (`src/hooks/use-api.ts`):
```typescript
// Fetching data (useTickets fetches registration types)
const { data: regTypes = [], isLoading, isFetching } = useTickets(eventId);

// Mutations with cache invalidation
const createRegType = useCreateTicket(eventId);
await createRegType.mutateAsync(formData);

// Manual cache invalidation
const queryClient = useQueryClient();
queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: queryKeys.tickets(eventId) });
```

**Available hooks:**
- `useTickets`, `useCreateTicket`, `useUpdateTicket`, `useDeleteTicket` (for registration types)
- `useRegistrations`, `useSpeakers`, `useImportRegistrationsToSpeakers`, `useSessions`, `useTracks`
- `useAbstracts`, `useHotels`, `useAccommodations`
- `useEventMedia`, `useUploadEventMedia`, `useDeleteEventMedia` (event-scoped media library)
- `useReviewers`, `useAddReviewer`, `useRemoveReviewer`
- `useEvents`, `useEvent`
- `useMedia`, `useUploadMedia`, `useDeleteMedia` (media library)
- `useSendCompletionEmails` (bulk send completion tokens to CSV-imported registrants)

## Recent Features

- **Incremental-sync date filters on the speakers + registrations lists — REST + MCP (July 21, 2026, integrator request, commit `70f8cded`, pkg 0.4.23→0.4.24)** — The API-key list endpoints integrations pull from (the n8n→Webflow people sync had to full-pull the roster every run) are now filterable by **created/updated date**: four optional params — `createdAfter` / `createdBefore` / `updatedAfter` / `updatedBefore` (ISO 8601, bounds **inclusive**; `updatedAfter` is the incremental-sync checkpoint) — on REST `GET /api/events/[eventId]/speakers` (previously status-only) + `GET .../registrations` (alongside status/paymentStatus/ticketTypeId/tags) AND MCP `list_speakers` / `list_registrations` (executors + tool defs + the register-mcp-tools Zod mirrors — **MCP clients reconnect**; pkg bumped + lockfile). ONE shared parser, [src/lib/date-range-filter.ts](src/lib/date-range-filter.ts) `parseDateRangeFilters()` (no cross-caller duplication): an unparsable value is an **error** (REST 400 + warn log, MCP tool error, both `code: "INVALID_DATE_FILTER"`), never a silently-dropped filter — the bad-filter-widens class the July 13 bulk-email `INVALID_FILTER` fix closed. **Internal surfaces unaffected by construction**: the dashboard hooks hit the same GETs but never send the params, and with no params the parser returns an empty `where` that spreads to a no-op (pinned by test); the 400 path is unreachable without opting in. Both responses already carry `createdAt`/`updatedAt` per row for checkpointing (no select changes needed). The public OpenAPI spec (`/api-docs`) documents the four params on both endpoints. +15 tests (10 parser: inclusive gte/lte mapping, single-bound checkpoint shape, absent/empty=inactive, per-param error cases, all-or-nothing, date-only values; 5 MCP wiring: where-shape threading, INVALID_DATE_FILTER short-circuits before any query, no-params no-op) — suite 3566 → 3581. tsc/eslint/vitest/build green. Docs: MCP_REFERENCE.md (new dated section + table rows) + the OpenAPI spec. **Follow-up candidates (not built):** `?tags=` + `?sessionRole=` on the speakers GET (would let the Webflow committee pull filter server-side + fix the tag case-sensitivity gotcha at the same time), and the `?segment=internal` union filter from docs/COMMITTEE_MEMBERS.md.

- **Cross-caller duplication audit — 3 drifted clusters consolidated + verified backlog (July 21, 2026, commits `814224aa`/`6b66649a`/`858a50cd` + review-fix follow-up)** — A repo-wide duplication audit surfaced 11 cross-caller findings; each was **verified against source by independent agents BEFORE any fix** (2 of 11 characterizations were wrong, and verification found 2 real bugs the audit missed). The three ALREADY-DRIFTED clusters shipped as gated commits. **(1) `814224aa` — seat+promo accounting consolidated** ([registration-seat-db.ts](src/lib/registration-seat-db.ts) gains `releasePromoUsage` (guarded, relative clamp — never negative), `claimPromoUsage`, `claimSeats` (guarded all-or-nothing bulk claim; `claimSeat` delegates), `claimSeatsOverselling` (the bulk-reactivation allow-and-log policy)); the MCP `bulk_update_registration_status` executor, the REST bulk-type route, and the REST delete route now route through them — fixing the **unguarded `promoCode.update({ decrement })`** on the MCP-bulk + delete paths (usedCount could go negative → a maxUses-capped code admitted extra redemptions) and adding the **H6 promo re-claim on bulk reactivation** (bulk cancel → reactivate → cancel used to double-release). The audit's "three oversell rules" framing was verified WRONG — bulk-type already hard-blocked 409; real drift was two-way. **(2) `6b66649a` — `promo-code-service.createPromoCode`** — REST POST + MCP `create_promo_code` were two drifting inline creates: **MCP wrote NO audit log**, REST never event-validated `ticketTypeIds` (silently linked foreign ticket types), MCP never enforced FIXED_AMOUNT-requires-currency. One service path now owns all of it (6 error codes incl. the P2002 race → DUPLICATE_CODE); REST status codes unchanged, MCP shape preserved. **(3) `858a50cd` — `abstract-service.assignReviewer/unassignReviewer`** — the twice-drifted (H6/H8) ~130-line REST+MCP reviewer-assignment pair is ONE implementation (org-scoped lookups, NOT_REVIEWABLE gate, upsert role/COI semantics, source-tagged audits now with before-values on both surfaces, create-only notification); response bodies byte-compatible, all 15 pre-existing route/COI tests pass unchanged. **Post-ship adversarial review of the batches: 0 BLOCKER / 0 HIGH / 3 MED / 5 LOW** — fixed in-band: M1 (the promo clamp fallback became a RELATIVE guarded decrement — an absolute `set 0` could have erased a concurrent redemption committed between the two statements), M2 (REST reviewers 500 bodies restored to the stable `ASSIGN/UNASSIGN_REVIEWER_FAILED` contract instead of leaking raw error text; service UNKNOWN messages are static), L2 (promo audit-failure log restored warn→error per the never-downgrade-alerts rule). Deferred (ROADMAP §"Cross-caller duplication audit"): findings 4–7 (setSessionSpeakers consolidation, MCP invoice-status through `cancelInvoice` + REST invoice audit gap, a canonical `rateLimited()` 429 helper — exactly 4 of 105 sites miss `Retry-After`, folding MCP single add/remove-speaker into session-service), M3 (bulk-status promo-re-claim TOCTOU), L4 (releaseExistingRedemption still hand-rolled), and the frontend cluster A4 (detail-sheet edits missing state/zip only — the audit's tags/photo/website claims were wrong) / A6 (speaker-status colour map ×5 with agenda drift → needs `speaker-enums.ts`) / A8 (dialog-vs-page free/paid tier-resolution divergence). Full report: [docs/CODE_REVIEW_DUPLICATION_JULY21.html](docs/CODE_REVIEW_DUPLICATION_JULY21.html). +34 tests across the batches (suite 3517 → 3548 + review-fix pins); tsc/eslint/vitest/build green per batch. **Stale-doc note fixed in passing:** the "MCP `update_invoice_status` REFUNDED is DB-only" claim in this file's tool list is outdated — the June 10 M6 fix narrowed the tool to CANCELLED/OVERDUE. **Tranche 2 — findings 4–7 shipped same day (owner go-ahead):** `56dcad12` **session roster ops → session-service** — `setSessionSpeakersTx` is the ONE atomic swap + L1 topic-cleanup applier (shared by `updateSession` step 2 + the new `replaceSessionRoster`), and `addSessionSpeaker`/`removeSessionSpeaker`/`replaceSessionRoster` own the H1 break-item truth table + source-tagged audits, with the three MCP roster executors reduced to thin wrappers (byte-compatible shapes; 3 production `as never` casts removed); `14540e81` **invoice status transitions** — shared `transitionInvoiceStatus` (idempotency guard + optional source-tagged audit) behind `cancelInvoice(id, ctx?)` + the new `markInvoiceOverdue`; **REST invoice status changes are audited for the first time** and MCP delegates instead of bare-updating; `9e9f2ed0` **canonical `rateLimited()` 429 helper** in [src/lib/api-errors.ts](src/lib/api-errors.ts) (RFC-9110 `Retry-After` + `code: "RATE_LIMITED"` + `retryAfterSeconds`, always logs) applied to all 7 call sites in the 4 files that omitted the header (agent execute, public complete-registration, both agreement routes); the ~100 compliant sites migrate opportunistically — **new code must use the helper**. Post-ship review of tranche 2: 0 BLOCKER / 0 HIGH / 2 MED / 7 LOW — **its M1 ("mcp-remote audit FK fails") was REFUTED by hand-verification** (migration `20260418000000_seed_mcp_system_user` seeds the User row; the tranche-1 reviewer had it right — when two reviews contradict, read the migration); M2 (no source-state gate on invoice transitions — a PAID invoice can still be marked OVERDUE/CANCELLED, pre-existing) is an **owner decision** in ROADMAP; L2/L3/L5 riders fixed in-band. +18 more tests (suite → 3566). MCP tool schemas unchanged (no pkg bump).

- **Agenda break items — Registration / Coffee Break / Lunch / Networking as first-class time blocks (July 21, 2026, organizer request, commit `fcd86151`, pkg 0.4.22→0.4.23)** — The agenda now distinguishes real program sessions from **break items**: plain time blocks with no speakers, topics, abstract, track, or Zoom. New `SessionType` enum + `EventSession.type` (default SESSION; additive+idempotent migration `20260721140000_add_session_type`). **Invariant lives in ONE place** — [session-service.ts](src/services/session-service.ts) `validate()` checks the RESULTING state (`BREAK_ITEM_HAS_PROGRAM`, 400): converting a session requires the payload to explicitly clear its roster (the dashboard form does this by submitting empty lists — we never auto-delete on the caller's behalf); an attached **Zoom meeting blocks conversion** (the edit dialog hides the Zoom section for break items, so conversion would strand a live billable meeting), and the **webinar anchor session can never be converted** (409 `WEBINAR_ANCHOR_SESSION`, mirroring the DELETE guard). The per-roster MCP executors (`add_speaker_to_session` / `add_topic_to_session` / `replace_session_speakers`) bypass the service and therefore enforce the gate themselves (adversarial-review H1). Shared display constants + the `isBreakSessionType()` hinge live in [session-enums.ts](src/lib/session-enums.ts) — **fails OPEN** on absent/unknown type (a pre-migration cached row can never be hidden; pinned by tests both ways after the suite caught the original fail-closed 404 guard). Wired through every surface: REST POST/PUT Zod (`z.nativeEnum(SessionType)`), MCP `create_session`/`update_session` `type` param (**MCP clients reconnect**; pkg bumped), the dashboard agenda (Type picker as the first form field — break types hide track/capacity/roles/topics/Zoom sections; muted dashed cards with per-type icons; the save toast now surfaces the server's actual error instead of a generic failure), the public agenda (slim muted bands with coffee/lunch icons), and the public session detail route (404 for break items). **Counts:** break items are excluded from the agenda "Sessions"/"Scheduled" tiles, `list_live_sessions_now`, `get_event_dashboard`/`get_event_stats`, and the cached `EventStats.sessionCount`. Adversarial review: 0 BLOCKER / 1 HIGH / 4 MED / 6 LOW — H1+M2+M3+M4+L1+L2 shipped in-band; deferred (ROADMAP §"Agenda break items review"): M1 check-then-act race on the invariant (narrow, self-healing), L3 HTTP-MCP can't convert topic-bearing sessions (extends the known `update_session`-omits-topics gap), L4 registration-page preview renders breaks plainly, and the multi-track known limitation (a break renders in the "No Track" column, not spanning all tracks). **Same-day follow-up (owner ask):** the agenda **CSV import** gained an optional `type` column (aliases: "Coffee Break"→BREAK, "Lunch Break"→LUNCH; unknown value = a ROW error, never a silent SESSION default; break rows ignore track/capacity — documented in the dialog — while speakers on a break row surface the service's rejection as a row error), and the **in-app AI Agent** can create break items via the shared `create_session` tool (an opening ceremony is a normal SESSION with speakers). +30 tests total (suite 3505); user-guide §3 "Break items" sub-section added (picked up by the help chatbot). tsc/eslint/vitest/build green. **Multi-day-programme review round (same day, owner ask):** verified the CSV import handles a 3-day programme structurally, and fixed the two things that would have bitten it — **(a) timezone-naive CSV datetimes were parsed in the SERVER's timezone** (UTC in prod), silently shifting an Excel-authored Dubai "09:00" to 1 PM; they are now read as **event wall-clock** via `wallTimeInTzToDate` (explicit `Z`/`±HH:MM` offsets still honored — matches the dashboard form's semantics); **(b) re-importing a corrected file duplicated the whole agenda** — rows matching an existing (name, startTime) are now **skipped** and reported (`skipped` count; in-file duplicate rows too). Also killed the residual agenda-domain duplication: ONE `HTTP_STATUS_FOR_SESSION_ERROR` map ([src/lib/session-http.ts](src/lib/session-http.ts), exhaustive over the service's error union — both routes used to carry hand-synced copies), the `[sessionId]` route + list GET now use the service's exported `SESSION_SELECT` (the list GET additionally gained `updatedAt`, additive), and every status/role/type literal list (route Zod, MCP whitelists, CSV whitelist) is now **derived from the Prisma enums** so a new enum value fails the build instead of drifting. +12 tests (suite 3517).

- **Speaker / Faculty reimbursement form — web replacement for the paper wire-transfer PDF (July 20, 2026, owner request)** — Speakers claim their speaker fee / flights / hotel / ground transport online instead of the emailed DOCX ("MMG Speaker Reimbursement Form"). **Owner decisions locked:** v1 is **submission-only** (PENDING → SUBMITTED; approval/payment tracking stays outside the system), dashboard visibility is **SUPER_ADMIN/ADMIN/ORGANIZER only**, currencies are **USD/AED/SAR** (as on the paper form). **Model** (additive+idempotent migration `20260720120500_add_speaker_reimbursement` — **applies on next deploy via deploy.sh, not yet on prod**): `SpeakerReimbursement` (one per speaker per event — `speakerId @unique`; unguessable plaintext token like RsvpInvite; Section B snapshot fields + `claimLines` JSON + `bankDetails` JSON + typed-name signature/`submittedAt`/`submittedIp`) + `SpeakerReimbursementDocument` (kind PASSPORT/FLIGHT_RECEIPT/HOTEL_INVOICE/TRANSPORT_RECEIPT/OTHER). **Flow:** organizer console at [/events/[eventId]/reimbursements](src/app/%28dashboard%29/events/%5BeventId%5D/reimbursements/page.tsx) (Setup-hub card, like Dinner RSVP) — add speakers (mints tokens), email personalized links via the new editable **`speaker-reimbursement-invitation`** template (single/all/pending; EmailLog-based 10-min batch retry-safety; logged against the SPEAKER entity so it shows on the speaker's Email History), copy link, review submissions (claim + bank + docs), CSV export for finance (audited PII extraction), **"Reopen for edits"** (conditional SUBMITTED→PENDING claim, audited) and delete. Speaker fills [/e/[slug]/reimbursement/[token]](src/app/e/%5Bslug%5D/reimbursement/%5Btoken%5D/page.tsx) — sections A–F mirroring the paper form, prefilled from the Speaker record, per-currency live totals (never summed across currencies), uploads (PDF/JPG/PNG magic-byte validated, 10MB, max 15), declaration + typed-name e-signature; submit is a **conditional claim on PENDING** (double-submit race commits once), audited with IP (agreement-acceptance shape), fires `notifyEventAdmins` + an automated **`speaker-reimbursement-received`** confirmation email (both failure-isolated). **The paper form's receipt rule is server-enforced**: passport copy always + the matching receipt per claimed expense (`requiredDocumentKinds` in [src/lib/reimbursement/constants.ts](src/lib/reimbursement/constants.ts)); speaker fee needs no receipt. **PII/security:** passport + bank details are wire-transfer data — every dashboard route (reads included) is `denyReviewer(session)`-gated (its restricted set is exactly the excluded population; `canManageReimbursements()` is the named UI predicate, fails closed); uploaded files live under `public/uploads/reimbursements/` (persistent volume + hourly DR sync) but the public `/uploads` catch-all **BLOCKS that prefix** — files stream only via the authed `GET .../reimbursements/[id]/documents/[documentId]` (event-bound + traversal-guarded + re-rooted). Public routes rate-limited per IP + per token; every rejection logs. Client-safe lib split ([constants.ts](src/lib/reimbursement/constants.ts) zod+pure helpers / [server.ts](src/lib/reimbursement/server.ts) token+loader) so the form page never bundles Node crypto. +33 tests ([reimbursement.test.ts](__tests__/lib/reimbursement.test.ts) totals/receipt-rule/predicate/schema + [reimbursement-public-routes.test.ts](__tests__/api/reimbursement-public-routes.test.ts) conditional-claim/lock/missing-docs/uploads-block); suite 3457. tsc/eslint/vitest/build green (e2e: 11 pre-existing failures on clean HEAD, unrelated — verified by stash-rerun). **Follow-up round (same day, owner requests):** send dialog gained **Preview** (renders the real per-event template + typed subject/message via the shared `/email-preview` route, template auto-selected — bulk-email-dialog parity) and an **Edit the template** deep link into the template editor (the templates list GET auto-seeds system defaults as editable rows, so the id always exists); the public form's banner is **width-constrained (`max-w-[1120px]`)** like the other public pages instead of full-bleed; **reimbursement activity now shows on the speaker profile's Activity timeline** (activity-feed.ts resolves the speaker's reimbursement row and folds its `SPEAKER_REIMBURSEMENT` audits in, remapped to `REIMBURSEMENT_SUBMITTED`/`REIMBURSEMENT_REOPENED` etc. so the card reads "Reimbursement form submitted", Banknote icon; the invitation email was already on the timeline via its SPEAKER EmailLog row); and a **Reimbursement card on the speaker profile** ([speaker-reimbursement-card.tsx](src/components/speakers/speaker-reimbursement-card.tsx), self-hides outside the staff boundary) — status + totals, Create & email link, resend, copy link, open console; backed by a `?speakerId=` filter on the list GET. **Docs:** [docs/SPEAKER_REIMBURSEMENT.md](docs/SPEAKER_REIMBURSEMENT.md) (model, boundary, routes, receipt rule) + user-guide "Speaker Reimbursements" section (console + speaker-profile send steps, FAQ — picked up by the help chatbot). **Deferred:** approval/paid tracking (schema leaves room for enum growth), a `speaker-reimbursement` emailType in the BULK-email pipeline (owner: "no need" — the dedicated send route is the one sender), MCP tools.

- **CRM in-app notification service — own bell, own table, separate from event notifications (July 17, 2026, owner request)** — The CRM module now has its own notification service, **deliberately NOT merged with the core `src/lib/notifications.ts`** (owner decision: the event platform's bell never carries pipeline traffic, and core never reads Crm* tables — the module boundary holds). **Model:** new `CrmNotification` (org + recipient `userId` Cascade, string `type`, title/message/link, `isRead`; additive+idempotent migration `20260717120000_add_crm_notification` — **not on prod**, like the rest of the CRM module). **One writer** ([src/crm/lib/crm-notifications.ts](src/crm/lib/crm-notifications.ts) `notifyCrmUser()`, the `recordCrmActivity` one-writer rule): the two cross-cutting rules live in the writer, not at call sites — a user is **never notified about their own action** (actor/recipient compare) and it **never throws** (the mutation it describes already committed; failures log `crm-notification:write-failed` and are swallowed). **Triggers (owner-picked, all four):** deal assigned to you (createDeal + updateDeal re-assign, new owner only, unchanged-ownerId re-sends don't re-nag), your deal stage-moved/**won**/**lost** (moveDealStage announces the OUTCOME when the drag lands in a mapped terminal column; closeDeal too), task assigned to you (create + re-assign), and the reminders worker's **task-due** in-app nudge — minted right after the `remindedAt` conditional claim so it rides the same idempotency as the reminder email and reaches mailbox-less temp accounts. **In-app only** (owner decision: no email — the reminders worker already emails; no push). Messages carry **no deal money**, so FINANCIAL_KEYS redaction never arises for the feed. **API:** `GET/PATCH /api/crm/notifications` (feed + unread count / mark-read `{ids}` or `{all:true}`) — `requireCrmRead`/`requireCrmWrite` gated (passes the source-level gate-drift test), reads+writes scoped to the caller's own `userId`+org in the `where` (no IDOR by construction), API-key callers get 400 `NO_USER_CONTEXT` (notifications are per-user). **UI:** [CrmNotificationBell](src/crm/components/crm-notification-bell.tsx) in the CRM shell header ([crm/layout.tsx](src/app/%28dashboard%29/crm/layout.tsx)) — unread badge, per-type icons, click → mark read + navigate, mark-all-read; `useCrmNotifications` polls 30s ([use-crm-api.ts](src/crm/hooks/use-crm-api.ts)). +21 tests (writer invariants incl. never-throws, effect-level trigger tests asserting the `db.crmNotification.create` payload per the H4 lesson, worker claim-gated nudge) + `crmNotification` mocks added to 4 existing CRM suites; suite 3307 → 3338. Docs: [src/crm/README.md](src/crm/README.md) §3.8 + CRM_STATUS.html. tsc/eslint/vitest/build green.

- **Email previews render ACTUAL data + 8px paragraph rhythm + session time windows (July 17, 2026, owner requests)** — Three related email rounds, shipped in phases (`33c489e1`, `b2f5b1f6`, `40646488`, `edfae54e`, `87ecfe27`). **(1) Paragraph rhythm 16px → 8px.** The Tiptap editor's block spacing (`[&>*]:mb-4` → `mb-2` in [tiptap-editor.tsx](src/components/ui/tiptap-editor.tsx)), the branding wrapper's juice-inlined `p { margin: 0 0 8px 0; }` rule ([email.ts](src/lib/email.ts)), and the CRM cover-email greeting's hardcoded margin all halved **in lockstep** so editor and sent email keep WYSIWYG parity (the July-16 honesty model preserved — the rule exists because email clients otherwise apply their own ~1em defaults). NOTE: the public pages rendering editor-authored HTML (welcome/terms, `[&>*]:mb-4` on `/e/[slug]/*`) were deliberately left at 16px — sweep them if one rhythm everywhere is wanted. **(2) presentationDetails now carries session time windows + durations.** `buildPresentationBlocks` ([speaker-agreement.ts](src/lib/speaker-agreement.ts)) renders one "Date & Time" line **per session** — start–end clock in the event TZ + duration, e.g. "Monday, March 15, 2026, 9:00 AM – 10:30 AM GMT+4 (1h 30m)" (new `formatSessionWindow`/`formatSessionDuration`; topic-session fallback deduped; `endTime` added to the topic select). The **`{sessionDateTime}` docx merge token stays format-stable** (start time only — it lands in the quasi-legal agreement document; pinned by test). **(3) Preview honesty — every token, all three failure classes closed.** Root causes: `renderTemplate` leaves unknown keys as literal `{{token}}`, and the sample-vars set was missing ~21 tokens (so previewing any webinar template, payment-confirmation, presenter-agreement, reviewer notify, or a speaker template showed raw tokens), while `{{organizerSignature}}` showed a canned sample. Now: **(a)** [getSamplePreviewVariables](src/lib/email.ts) covers every token (webinar joinUrl/passcodeBlock/recordingBlock/webinarDate/webinarTime/panelist+session fields, receiptBlock/paymentReference, presenter/reviewer/cert tokens, entryBarcode placeholder box — samples in the real senders' EXACT markup); **(b)** both preview routes ([email-preview](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/email-preview/route.ts) + the [template test-send](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/email-templates/%5BtemplateId%5D/route.ts)) fetch the caller's **real `User.emailSignature`** (empty when they have none — an honest preview never promises a signature the send won't render) and greet `{{speakerName}}`/`{{presenterName}}`/`{{recipientName}}` with the signed-in user; **(c)** new **[src/lib/email-preview-data.ts](src/lib/email-preview-data.ts)** `buildRealPreviewOverrides(eventId)` — the async real-data layer both routes run in parallel: first session (name, start in event TZ, the **gated-session joinUrl**, webinarDate/Time), the **real Zoom passcode** + recording state (absent when no Zoom attached, so samples stand), latest abstract titles + real count, a representative session-linked speaker's REAL presentationDetails block, real login/review links; failure-isolated (enrichment error → warn log + samples render, a preview can never 500 from it). **Deliberately still representative** (documented in the module header): per-recipient minted links (survey/rsvp/agreement — minting real tokens in a preview would rotate live credentials), payment artifacts, un-issued cert serials, entryBarcode (cid-attached PNG), per-abstract decision fields. **(d) Drift guard** ([email-preview-vars.test.ts](__tests__/lib/email-preview-vars.test.ts)): every `{{token}}` in every default template AND every advertised `TEMPLATE_VARIABLES` key must have a preview value — a future template with an unsampled token fails the suite, not an organizer's Preview click. **(4) New `{{moderatorDetails}}`/`{{moderatorDetailsText}}` variable (owner request, same day).** For each session the recipient **MODERATES** (`SessionSpeaker.role === MODERATOR`): session name + location + time window, then the full **topic run-sheet** — Time | Topic | Speaker(s) | Duration table, with each topic's start–end **computed by stacking topic durations from the session start** (SessionTopic stores no start time; an un-timed topic shows "—" and does not advance the clock). Built by `buildModeratorBlocks` in [speaker-agreement.ts](src/lib/speaker-agreement.ts) (dynamic strings HTML-escaped — a malicious topic title can't inject), empty for non-moderators. Rides everywhere the speaker context does: bulk sends + the single-send route (incl. its `renderMessageValue` rawHtmlKeys so the token typed into a compose box resolves), the agreement-page merge map (plain-text policy like presentationDetails), `DEFAULT_RAW_HTML_KEYS`, the TEMPLATE_VARIABLES reference, preview samples, and the real-data preview layer (a representative moderator's actual run-sheet). +40 tests across the day (suite → 3307). Verified per phase: tsc/eslint/vitest/build green.

- **Dinner RSVP ROUND 2 review + full MED remediation (July 16, 2026)** — An independent second pass over the Dinner RSVP module (3 adversarial lenses, deduped against Round 1's [CODE_REVIEW_SURVEY_RSVP.html](docs/CODE_REVIEW_SURVEY_RSVP.html), whose H2/B2/H4/H5 fixes were re-verified to HOLD): **0 BLOCKER / 0 HIGH / 12 MED / 16 LOW**, report at [docs/CODE_REVIEW_DINNER_RSVP_R2.html](docs/CODE_REVIEW_DINNER_RSVP_R2.html). **All 12 MEDs + 7 LOW riders shipped same-day in 4 gated batches** (+15 tests, suite → 3246). **(1) Public-submit correctness (`2716baf7` — M1/M2/M3/M10 + L7/L11/L13):** a dinner with **no `rsvpDeadline` never closed** — the optional-field default meant the roster stayed editable weeks after the gala; the effective close is now `rsvpDeadline ?? dinnerAt` (new `isDinnerOpen`, both GET + POST). An answer for a dinner that closed while the form sat open was **silently dropped behind `ok:true`** — the API now returns `ignoredDinnerIds` and the form warns which answers were NOT recorded. The public submit now writes a **before→after AuditLog row with IP** (`action: RESPOND`, `actor: INVITEE` — the speaker-agreement-acceptance shape), so a disputed "I confirmed with 3 guests" is resolvable. Riders: deadline-after-dinner rejected on POST + partial PUT (effective merged values); venue-NAT-safe public submit limits (per-IP 120/hr + per-token 20/hr); dinner UPDATE/DELETE + invite DELETE audits carry real snapshots (were field-names-only / `{}`). **(2) Access alignment (`3966a6d4` — M4/M5/L9):** `GET /dinners` had **no role guard + hand-rolled `organizationId!`** (CRM_USER / cross-event ONSITE could read any org event's dinner config — the class the roster GET's H2 fix missed); now `denyReviewer` + `buildEventAccessWhere`. **MEMBER could read the full VIP roster (names/emails/dietary) through the in-app agent's `list_dinner_rsvps`** — list_-prefixed, so it tunneled through the read-only gate around the H2 policy; new `ROSTER_PII_AGENT_TOOLS` set in [tools/_shared.ts](src/lib/agent/tools/_shared.ts), refused in the agent execute route with `ROSTER_FORBIDDEN` (the FINANCE_ONLY pattern; API-key MCP callers are admin-equivalent, unchanged). All six organizer handlers now resolve the event via `buildEventAccessWhere` (org-null SUPER_ADMIN no longer 404s). **(3) Send-pipeline parity (`c54addef` — M6/M7/M8 + L1/L15):** batch sends are **retry-safe** — the EmailLog rows the route already writes are the resume state (invitees successfully mailed in the last 10 min are skipped with `skippedRecentlyInvited` reported; single-invitee sends are explicit resends, never skipped), so a mid-loop timeout + retry can't re-blast the VIP list. The shared **email-preview route now renders the typed Subject and feeds the typed Message to BOTH `{{message}}` and `{{personalMessage}}`** (the dinner preview used to show the canned "We're excited to have you!" instead of the organizer's text). The send route got the July-16 **`renderMessageValue`** wiring (tokens typed into the Message box resolve per recipient). Riders: "Sent 0, N failed" toasts red; zero-dinner sends refused (400 `NO_DINNERS`). **(4) Honesty + records (`e41d4692` — M9/M11/M12 + L2/L16):** MCP `inviteesTruncated` no longer hard-codes false under a status filter (compares against the FILTERED total); a failed event fetch on the console no longer lets Copy-link hand out a broken `/e//rsvp/…` URL with a green toast; the import dialog toasts on fetch failure instead of "No people found."; and the **doc drift on a security statement** was corrected — DINNER_RSVP.md's "MEMBER can read the roster" (the OPPOSITE of the enforced model since H2) superseded, this file's "NOT yet independently reviewed" line + DOMAIN_MAP's scoreboard fixed. **Remaining LOWs** (L3 bucket-burn-before-ownership, L4 CRLF, L5 token-in-EmailLog-body, L6 console TZ race, L8 isActive unreachable, L10 CSV name collisions, L12 missing PUT/DELETE rate limits, L14 CSV bare-href) tracked in [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md) §"Dinner RSVP — backlog". - **July-16 review remediation round 1 — H1 + M1/M2/M3 + M9/M10/L7 shipped (July 16, 2026)** — The owner-picked first tranche from [docs/CODE_REVIEW_JULY16_PROGRAM_COMMS.html](docs/CODE_REVIEW_JULY16_PROGRAM_COMMS.html) (the post-ship review of the same-day program/comms/speaker-documents batch), three gated commits. **(1) H1 (`e795e829`) — the M9 date guard no longer locks Settings → General.** The guard keyed on field *presence*, and the General form always echoes startDate/endDate/timezone back — so an event with a legacy out-of-range session couldn't save a rename/venue/tax change. It now fires only on a **computed change** (`getTime()`/timezone diff vs the stored row) and **excludes CANCELLED sessions** (they no longer render on the agenda and must not block a legitimate date change). **(2) Agreement-link semantics (`a9fdabe7`, M1/M2/M3).** `mintSpeakerAgreementLink` gained `{ rotate }`: **strict AGREEMENT sends keep rotate** (latest re-send wins), **agreementBlock-driven sends (invitation/custom, incl. `includeAgreementLink`) mint ADDITIVELY** — sweeping only expired rows — so a bounced invitation or two same-minute scheduled sends can never invalidate a previously-delivered agreement link (tokens are stored hashed, so literal reuse is impossible; additive minting is the equivalent guarantee). Acceptance now `deleteMany`s ALL of the speaker's tokens (no valid sibling survives a signing; a stale link post-acceptance still lands on the friendly `alreadyAccepted` state). **M3 cross-caller parity:** bulk AGREEMENT re-sends to a *signed* speaker used to render a dead `href=""` CTA while single-send minted a working link — bulk strict sends now mint for everyone (landing signed speakers on the already-accepted page; `{{agreementBlock}}` still renders the green note). **M2 disclosure:** the bulk dialog (speaker invitation) + the speaker page's invitation dialog now say the agreement block adds a personal Review & Agree link (previous links stay valid) + attaches the personalized agreement when configured; the strict agreement dialog states re-sending REPLACES the previous link. **(3) Timezone/labels sweep (`f056daab`, M9/M10/L7).** The five surfaces the July-16 agenda unification missed now render in the **event's** timezone with a label: speaker detail page (sessions + topics + its SessionDetailSheet mount), the speakers-list quick-view sheet, **webinar confirmation/reminder emails** (`{{webinarDate}}`/`{{webinarTime}}` rendered the server's UTC clock — a 10:00 Dubai webinar emailed "06:00 AM UTC"), the **`{sessionDateTime}` merge field inside the personalized agreement document** (was Dubai-fixed `formatDateTime`), and **dinner RSVP** (public invitee page + organizer console — the console's datetime-local form also moved onto the event-TZ `localDateTimeInTz`/`wallTimeInTzToDate` inverse pair with the TZ named on the input labels). The speaker page's **fifth hand-rolled SessionRole colour map** (moderator/chairperson colours swapped vs [session-enums](src/lib/session-enums.ts), lowercase labels) replaced with `SESSION_ROLE_COLORS`/`formatSessionRole`; the communications Session Role filter maps over `SESSION_ROLE_OPTIONS` and the bulk-dialog recap prints "Moderator" not raw "MODERATOR". +7 tests (suite → 3157); report pills flipped in place. **Still open from that review:** M4 (same-session abstract-swap false P2002), M5 (SpeakerDocument replace race + orphaned file), M6 (sortOrder tx doesn't serialize under READ COMMITTED), M7 (signed agreements publicly downloadable via `/uploads` — needs an owner call: authed streaming route vs accepted risk), M8 (MCP `update_session` schema omits `topics`), L1–L6, L8.

- **Scheduled-email ownership token + mid-send cancel (comms C1+C5) + contacts honest saves (R2-M3/M4) (July 16, 2026)** — Two deferred clusters from the day's reviews, shipped together. **(1) C1 — ownership, not just liveness:** new `ScheduledEmail.claimToken` (additive+idempotent migration `20260716120000`): the worker's PENDING→PROCESSING claim stamps a per-claim token, and the heartbeat + ALL terminal writes (SENT / SENT-0 / FAILED) now condition on `status = PROCESSING AND claimToken = ours` ([scheduled-emails-worker.ts](src/lib/scheduled-emails-worker.ts)) — before this, `status = PROCESSING` alone also matched a row a Retry had re-claimed, so a zombie sender surviving a DB-write outage could mark the re-claimed row SENT with its own counts while worker B was mid-send. Retry clears the token. **(2) C5 — a mid-flight send can be stopped:** `executeBulkEmail` + `executeCertificateBulkSend` take a `shouldContinue` callback checked between every 25-recipient batch (the worker's check = "still PROCESSING with MY token"); the schedule DELETE now cancels **PROCESSING** rows too — a mistaken 2,000-recipient send stops at the next batch boundary instead of running to completion. An aborted send returns `aborted: true`, writes NO terminal state, fires no audit/notify, and everything already sent stays in `emailedKeys` so a later Retry resumes rather than re-sends; a THROWING check means keep-going (a pooler blip must not kill a live send). MCP `cancel_scheduled_email` deliberately stays PENDING-only. **(3) Contacts honest saves:** `additionalEmail` added to the contacts update schema (it was in NEITHER schema, so the detail sheet's field was a dead write — success toast, value reverted; empty string → null clears), and the [contact detail sheet](src/components/contacts/contact-detail-sheet.tsx) now sends `value || null` for every optional field so an emptied phone/org/bio/notes actually CLEARS (half the fields previously sent `|| undefined` = "unchanged" — and the only other clearing surface, the full-page edit form, was itself broken until this morning's H-B fix). +24 tests (claim-token stamping + same-token completion, zombie/abort no-terminal-write, shouldContinue truth table, 26-recipient batch-boundary abort with resume-keys, throwing-check keep-going, additionalEmail persist/clear/reject + null-clear PUT). tsc/eslint/vitest 3085/build green.

- **CRM: product/service catalog + deal line items (July 15, 2026)** — New CRM domain: the org's **product/service catalog** (a **Products** tab) + **line items on deals**, so a deal is itemized from catalog products. Seeded from Meeting Minds' Jan-2026 service list (**131 products**, baked into [crm-products-seed.ts](src/crm/lib/crm-products-seed.ts)). **Two models** (migration `20260715170000`, additive/idempotent, **not on prod**): `CrmProduct` (org-scoped catalog — `name`/`sku`/`category`/`source`/`price`/`currency`/`priceIncludesTax`/`archivedAt`; `category` is the **functional group** from the SKU/name prefix — Content/Sponsorship/Design/CME/… — chosen over the CSV's In-House/Out-Sourced column, which is kept as the separate `source` flag) and `CrmDealProduct` (a deal line item: `crmProductId` ref + **snapshotted** productName/category/sku so a later catalog edit never rewrites a deal, `unitPrice`, `quantity`). **Owner decisions:** category = functional group; deals get **line items (qty × price)**; the deal **Value stays MANUAL** (the products total is informational, shown alongside); the **line unit price is set on the deal** (pre-filled from the catalog list price, editable per deal); catalog **seeded** (not a CSV-upload UI). New [crm-product-service.ts](src/crm/services/crm-product-service.ts): `ensureCrmProducts` seeds once (idempotent), catalog CRUD (audits to core `AuditLog` like pipeline/templates), + deal line-item ops (`addDealProduct`/`updateDealProduct`/`removeDealProduct`) which bind **both** the deal and the product to the org, reject a duplicate product on a deal (`PRODUCT_ALREADY_ON_DEAL`), and record `PRODUCT_ADDED`/`PRODUCT_REMOVED` on the **deal's** `CrmActivity` History. **Finance-gated:** `price` + `unitPrice` are in `FINANCIAL_KEYS`, so `redactForCaller` strips them for MEMBER — line totals + products total render "—" (never a partial sum), and the inline price inputs don't render. Routes: `GET/POST /api/crm/products`, `PATCH/DELETE /api/crm/products/[productId]` (archive = admin+CRM_USER), `GET/POST/PATCH/DELETE /api/crm/deals/[dealId]/products`. UI: a **Products** page (searchable table + category filter + New/Edit dialog with a category datalist + Show archived) and a **Products card on the deal page** ([crm-deal-products.tsx](src/crm/components/crm-deal-products.tsx) — searchable catalog picker excluding already-added, inline qty/price edit on blur, products total). +11 service tests (seed-once, required fields, org-bound edits, the deal line-item guards: deal+product org-binding, dup, snapshot, activity). Gate green: tsc, eslint, **2983 tests**, build (all routes + page register). **Adversarial review** (no BLOCKER; IDOR/finance-gating/snapshot/RBAC verified solid): **H1** silent business rejections → a `reject()` logging helper; **M1** seed double-seed → `@@unique([organizationId, sku])` (migration `20260715180000`) + `skipDuplicates`; **M2** cross-currency products total → `sumDealProducts` returns null + "— (mixed currencies)"; **M3** product dialog stale state → keyed remount — all shipped; L1–L5 deferred ([ROADMAP](docs/ROADMAP.md) §"CRM products review"). Not deployed — ships with the rest of the CRM module.
- **CRM: editable email templates + management screen (July 15, 2026)** — Promoted the CRM email templates from hardcoded constants to a **per-org, editable store** with a **Templates** tab in the CRM (`/crm/templates`). New `CrmEmailTemplate` model (org-scoped, `name`/`subject`/`body` HTML/`sortOrder`/`archivedAt`/`createdById`; additive+idempotent migration `20260715160000`, **not applied to prod**). New [crm-email-template-service.ts](src/crm/services/crm-email-template-service.ts): `ensureCrmEmailTemplates` **seeds the built-in three** (Sponsorship prospectus / Follow-up / Thank you, from the existing `crm-email-templates.ts` constants) **on first use, once** (idempotent — archiving all never resurrects them, same rule as `ensurePipelineStages`), + list/create/update/archive. Config, not a tracked CRM record, so it audits to the **core `AuditLog`** (entityType `CrmEmailTemplate`) like `pipeline-service`, NOT the entity-typed `CrmActivity`. Routes: `GET/POST /api/crm/email-templates` (GET seeds + lists, `?archived=1`), `PATCH/DELETE /api/crm/email-templates/[templateId]` (edit / restore / archive). **RBAC:** create+edit = `requireCrmWrite` (write access incl. ORGANIZER + CRM_USER); **archive/restore = `requireCrmDelete`** (admin + CRM_USER — an ORGANIZER may edit but not archive, same as every CRM record). **Management page** ([/crm/templates](src/app/(dashboard)/crm/templates/page.tsx)): list with subject + body preview, New/Edit dialog ([crm-email-template-dialog.tsx](src/crm/components/crm-email-template-dialog.tsx) — name + subject + Tiptap body + token reference), "Show archived" toggle + restore. The **compose dialog now fetches DB templates** via `useCrmEmailTemplates()` (was the constant) — so a CRM_User's edits show up in "Start from a template"; the constants remain only as the seed. Tokens (`{{firstName}}`/`{{companyName}}`/`{{eventName}}`) still substituted at send time. +9 service tests (seed-once idempotency, required fields, org-bound update/archive). Gate green: tsc, eslint, 2958 tests, build (both routes + the page register). Supersedes the earlier "built-in, pre-fill only, no CMS" note — CRM_Users/admins now manage their own. - **CRM: a deal must be linked to an event/project (July 15, 2026)** — Owner: "a deal should have event field as a must; adding a deal should select the project from a dropdown." The event picker (the searchable published-events dropdown that already existed) is now **required** on deal create + edit, and moved up to sit right under the deal name (labelled "Event (project) *"). **Enforced in depth:** the `createDeal` service returns `EVENT_REQUIRED` when no `eventId` (its `CreateDealInput.eventId` is now a required `string`), `updateDeal` refuses to CLEAR the event to null (re-pointing to another event is fine — an event-less legacy deal, e.g. one whose event was `SetNull`'d on deletion, must be given one on next edit); the POST `/api/crm/deals` Zod requires `eventId`, the PATCH drops `.nullable()` on it; and both dialogs validate client-side. `EventCombobox` gained `allowClear`/`placeholder` props — the deal dialogs pass `allowClear={false}` (no "No event" option) while the board/report filters keep "All events". **The DB column stays nullable by design** (`eventId String?`, `onDelete: SetNull`) — a hard NOT-NULL constraint would force the FK to Cascade (delete the deal with its event) or Restrict (block deleting a used event); keeping SetNull + enforcing "required" at create/edit is the safer shape, so **no migration**. +2 service tests (create without event → EVENT_REQUIRED; update can't clear the event). Gate green: tsc, eslint, 2942 tests, build. Not deployed — ships with the rest of the CRM module.
- **CRM: record-page layout redesign + contact promoted to a page + reps exclude organizers (July 15, 2026)** — Owner: "layout is not good, use the design skill." The dedicated record pages (deal/account, and now **contact** too) were flat single-column stacks; they're now a proper **two-column SaaS-admin record layout** (via the `ui-ux-pro-max` design guidance): an identity **header** (title + status/company/lifecycle badges + right-aligned actions), then a body split into a **main work area** (deal: close / follow-up / activity / history; account + contact: notes / deals / people / history) and a **sticky sidebar** of key facts. Everything is grouped into bordered `bg-card` sections instead of `<Separator>`-divided runs; money uses `tabular-nums`; hover/focus states + `max-w-6xl`; responsive (facts stack **first** on mobile, then the work area). Shared presentational primitives in [record-layout.tsx](src/crm/components/record-layout.tsx) (`RecordHeader`/`RecordGrid`/`RecordCard`/`Facts`/`Fact`/`Dash`) keep the three pages visually consistent — the two-column shell is defined ONCE. **Contact is now a page** ([contact-detail-body.tsx](src/crm/components/contact-detail-body.tsx) + `/crm/contacts/[crmContactId]`) matching deal/account; its list row navigates there and the old `crm-contact-detail-sheet.tsx` is deleted (so **all three CRM records — deal, account, contact — are pages now; no detail sheets remain**). Cross-links added: an account's deal/people rows link to those records; a contact's deals + company link out; a deal's stage shows in the sidebar (`stage` added optional to `CrmBoardDeal`, returned by the detail GET). **Also (owner ask):** `/api/crm/reps` `REP_ROLES` drops **ORGANIZER** — reps are now SUPER_ADMIN/ADMIN/CRM_USER only (organizers run events, not the pipeline; `canOwnDeals` still permits an organizer to own a deal if assigned by other means). No schema change, no new API. Gate green: tsc, eslint, 2940 tests, build (all three `[id]` page routes register). Not deployed — ships with the rest of the CRM module.
- **CRM: dedicated deal + account pages (replaces the slide-out sheets) (July 15, 2026)** — A deal and a company (account) are now **first-class records with their own URL** — `/crm/deals/[dealId]` and `/crm/companies/[companyId]` — instead of a slide-out over the board/list. Deep-linkable, back-button-friendly, and each renders full-width (owner decision: **replace** the sheet, not keep-both). **Mechanics:** the sheets' entire content was extracted verbatim into reusable body components ([deal-detail-body.tsx](src/crm/components/deal-detail-body.tsx), [company-detail-body.tsx](src/crm/components/company-detail-body.tsx)) — nothing lost: summary, close (won/lost), follow-up tasks, notes/activity, people-on-deal, email, edit, archive/restore, and the History timeline all moved over. New page routes render the body under the existing tabbed CRM layout (the Deals/Companies tab stays active), with a "Back to deals/accounts" link; the deal page fetches via a new `useCrmDeal(id)` hook (the `GET /api/crm/deals/[dealId]` already returned the full shape — contacts+role, event, owner, stage), the account page via the existing `useCrmCompany(id)`. **Navigation rewired:** clicking a board card `router.push`es to the deal page (was: open sheet); clicking a company row → the account page; and the account page's deal list links straight to each deal page. `onClosed`/`onArchived` callbacks navigate back to the board/list after a close or archive.
