No schema change, no new API. Gate green: tsc, eslint, 2940 tests, build (both `[dealId]`/`[companyId]` page routes register). Not deployed — ships with the rest of the CRM module.
- **CRM: per-deal email + built-in email templates (July 15, 2026)** — Two extensions to the sponsor-email work, sharing ONE dialog + ONE send engine (no duplication). **(1) Email a specific deal.** An **Email** button on the deal detail sheet (gated `canWrite`, disabled when the deal has no contacts) opens the compose dialog scoped to that deal's contacts. **(2) 2–3 built-in email templates.** A "Start from a template" picker in the dialog pre-fills subject + body from [src/crm/lib/crm-email-templates.ts](src/crm/lib/crm-email-templates.ts) (Sponsorship prospectus / Follow-up / Thank you) — **pre-fill only** (client-safe constants, not a per-org template CMS; the ask was "2 or 3"); bodies omit the greeting (the pipeline bakes "Dear {{firstName}}" in) and use only the firstName/lastName/companyName/eventName tokens. **Architecture — generalized, not duplicated:** [sponsor-email-service.ts](src/crm/services/sponsor-email-service.ts) grew `resolveDealRecipients()` + `sendDealEmail()` alongside the event pair, both funnelling through a shared private `dispatchCrmEmail()` (validate → **narrow-never-widen** intersection → batch/`Promise.allSettled` with per-recipient failure isolation → per-contact `EmailLog` + CRM history). A single deal is resolved by passing a one-element array to the SAME `collectSponsorRecipients()` the event path uses (so the dedup/skip logic + its tests cover both). Branding comes from the deal's linked event if any, else the org default sender; `{{eventName}}` renders empty for an event-less deal. A deal send also records **one summary `EMAIL_SENT` row on the deal's History** (in addition to the per-contact rows), so "who emailed this deal, when?" is answerable from the sheet. **The routes multiplex** — `GET .../recipients?eventId=|dealId=` and `POST .../send` (Zod `.refine` requires exactly one of eventId/dealId — an ambiguous target is a client bug, not "send to everything"). The hook + dialog generalized to a `CrmEmailTarget = {kind:"event"|"deal", id}` (`useCrmEmailRecipients`/`useSendCrmEmail`; `SponsorEmailDialog` → `CrmEmailDialog`, still write-gated staff-only + the 10/hr `crm-sponsor-email:org` bucket). The Tiptap body remounts via a nonce `key` when a template is applied (`useEditor` reads `content` only on mount). No schema change. +6 tests (deal 404 / deal send records deal-summary + per-contact / narrow-never-widen / event-less deal / no-summary-when-all-fail / template token+shape guard). Gate green: tsc, eslint, **2940 tests**, build. Not deployed — ships with the rest of the CRM module.
- **CRM: new deal pipeline stages + reconcile script (July 15, 2026)** — Owner changed the sponsorship pipeline to **New → Proposal → Negotiation → Contract Signed → Purchase Order → Invoice Sent → Won → Lost** (was Prospect → Contacted → Proposal → Negotiation → Won → Lost). **(1) Seed.** `DEFAULT_PIPELINE_STAGES` in [pipeline-service.ts](src/crm/services/pipeline-service.ts) updated — canonical for any fresh org (and prod when the CRM deploys). **`Won`/`Lost` keep those exact names on purpose** — `closeDeal()` finds the terminal column *by name* and `terminalStatusFor()` maps a terminal stage to WON/LOST only when it's literally named won/lost, so renaming either would silently stop drag-to-close from closing the deal; new columns go BEFORE them (comment added at the seed). **(2) Applying it to an existing org** — `ensurePipelineStages` deliberately never mutates an org that already has a pipeline (so a customized board isn't force-reset on every load), so the seed change alone only affects brand-new orgs. New pure, unit-tested planner [src/crm/lib/pipeline-reconcile.ts](src/crm/lib/pipeline-reconcile.ts) `planPipelineReconciliation(existing, canonical)` matches existing stages to canonical **by case-insensitive name** (each consumed once, so a duplicate column becomes an orphan not a second winner): CREATE the missing columns at their canonical position, fix name/order/terminal on the matches, and everything else is an ORPHAN. **A deal never vanishes** — an orphan column's deals are moved to the fallback (canonical[0] = "New") BEFORE the column is deleted (the FK is Restrict). New [scripts/reconcile-crm-pipeline.ts](scripts/reconcile-crm-pipeline.ts) (dry-run default, `--write`, `--org <id>`) applies the plan in a transaction; **idempotent** (a second run is a clean no-op). So the old board's Prospect/Contacted columns are removed and their deals land in New; Proposal/Negotiation/Won/Lost are re-ordered and kept. **Run the dry-run, eyeball it, then `--write`.** No schema change, no rename API/UI built (deferred — the "API exists, UI doesn't" stage-management item still stands). +6 planner tests (old-seed→canonical create/keep/remove, idempotent no-op, case-insensitive rename, duplicate→orphan). Gate green: tsc, eslint, **2934 tests**, build. Also fixed a latent tsc error in the sponsor-email test fixture (an explicit `null` widened a `{name}|null` field to include `undefined`) that `next build`/vitest don't typecheck and so slipped past the prior commit's gate.
- **CRM: sponsor prospectus email — personalized bulk send + attachments (July 15, 2026)** — Owner ask: "send the sponsorship prospectus to all sponsors of an event." An **Email sponsors** button on the Deals board (honours the current event filter) opens a compose dialog. **(1) Audience — "sponsors of an event", computed in ONE place.** New pure [src/crm/lib/sponsor-recipients.ts](src/crm/lib/sponsor-recipients.ts): `collectSponsorRecipients()` flattens the event's **non-lost, non-archived** deals (`CrmDeal.eventId = X`, `status != LOST`) into their `CrmDealContact` people, **deduped on the contact's canonical `emailKey`** (a person on two of the event's deals is emailed once; `dealCount` records the overlap), dropping archived / email-less contacts and **counting** them for the preview. Owner decisions locked: **all active deals** (prospects + won), **all deal contacts** (every role), **inline per-send PDF** (no schema change), **button on the board**. **(2) Narrow, never widen (the M7 lesson).** The dialog shows the resolved recipients with per-row deselect + Select all/none; the send carries an explicit `contactIds` selection which the server **intersects** with the resolved set via `narrowToSelected()` — an invented/stale contactId can't smuggle a stranger onto the send (a dropped non-sponsor id is logged). **(3) Reuses core send primitives, NOT the event bulk-email pipeline.** New [src/crm/services/sponsor-email-service.ts](src/crm/services/sponsor-email-service.ts) `resolveSponsorRecipients()` + `sendSponsorProspectus()` live in the CRM module and own the audience + token logic, but render + send via **core** `sendEmail` / `renderAndWrap` / `brandingFrom` / `brandingCc` (crm→core is allowed; dragging CRM into `executeBulkEmail`, built around event recipient types, would cross the boundary the wrong way). Batches of 25 via `Promise.allSettled` with **per-recipient failure isolation** (one bad address never sinks the batch); each success writes an `EmailLog` row (Email History, `entityType: OTHER` + the crmContactId — `EmailLogEntityType` has no CRM value, so no schema change) **and** a `PROSPECTUS_SENT` `CrmActivity` row on the contact's History timeline (new free-string action label). **(4) Personalization + attachments.** `{{firstName}} {{lastName}} {{companyName}} {{eventName}}` in the subject + Tiptap body (a greeting is baked in so a tokenless body is still personalized; body-token values HTML-escaped to defuse a `<` in a name); the sender's own `User.emailSignature` is appended; per-event branding/from applies. Attachments: up to **5 files / 10MB** inline base64 (the prospectus PDF), mirroring the dashboard bulk dialog. **(5) Gated.** Both routes ([/api/crm/sponsor-email/recipients](src/app/api/crm/sponsor-email/recipients/route.ts) preview + [/send](src/app/api/crm/sponsor-email/send/route.ts)) are `requireCrmWrite` (staff-only — a read-only MEMBER can't even enumerate the sponsor list), and `send` layers a dedicated `crm-sponsor-email:org` bucket at **10/hr** on top of the generic CRM write limit (a leaked key can't spray the sponsor list). **No migration.** +13 tests (dedup / archived+email-less exclusion / company fallback / **narrow-never-widen** / per-recipient failure isolation / validation), whose key guards assert the **audience math** (the correctness that matters). Full gate green: tsc, eslint, **2928 tests**, build (both routes registered). Status board: [docs/CRM_STATUS.html](docs/CRM_STATUS.html) §5. **Not deployed** — ships with the rest of the CRM module (its migrations are not yet applied to prod; this feature adds none of its own).
- **CRM: edit + soft-delete (archive) + change-log/activity history on deals, accounts, contacts, tasks (July 15, 2026)** — Closed the biggest CRM UI gap ("API exists, UI doesn't") plus the two the owner asked for: **every record can be edited and archived, and a detailed activity log is maintained.** **(1) Change log — one writer, one table.** New `CrmActivity` model (org-scoped, polymorphic `entityType`+`entityId`, `action`, `changes` JSON, `actor`, additive migration `20260715130000`) written by a **single** `recordCrmActivity()` in [src/crm/lib/crm-activity.ts](src/crm/lib/crm-activity.ts) — every service calls it and **nothing else writes the table**, so the trail can't drift between callers (the per-service `writeAudit`→core-`AuditLog` helpers this replaced were the smell; CRM's `AuditLog` rows were never read anyway). It is the CRM's OWN store: org-scoped, **diff-shaped** (edits record field-level before→after via `diffFields`, which normalizes Decimal→number + Date→ISO), and actually READ in the UI. Records CREATE / UPDATE(+diffs) / ARCHIVE / RESTORE / STAGE_MOVE / WON / LOST / CONTACT_ADDED/REMOVED / COMPLETE / REOPEN / link-event-contact. Read via unified `GET /api/crm/activity?entityType=&entityId=`; deal money in a log payload is **redacted for MEMBER** by the same `FINANCIAL_KEYS` machinery the board uses. Rendered as a **History** timeline ([crm-activity-timeline.tsx](src/crm/components/crm-activity-timeline.tsx)) in every detail sheet. **(2) Soft delete only — never a hard delete.** New nullable `archivedAt` on `CrmDeal`/`CrmCompany`/`CrmContact`/`CrmTask` (the old hard `deleteTask` is gone). `setXArchived()` per service is idempotent (a no-op state change records nothing) and snapshots name/value into the ARCHIVE entry so the trail survives. Every list / board / report / CSV excludes `archivedAt != null` (centralized in `buildDealWhere` for deals/reports/export; explicit on the company/contact/task lists via `isArchivedView`); the **reminder worker skips archived tasks**. `DELETE /api/crm/{entity}/[id]` archives; `PATCH {archived:false}` restores; a **"Show archived"** toggle on every list surfaces them (drag disabled on the archived board). **(3) RBAC — a new, narrower predicate.** `canDeleteCrm` ([crm-roles.ts](src/crm/lib/crm-roles.ts)) = **SUPER_ADMIN / ADMIN / CRM_USER** (owner decision) — deliberately narrower than the write predicate, so **ORGANIZER can edit but not archive**, and MEMBER stays read-only. Enforced at the boundary via `denyCrmDelete` / `requireCrmDelete` (the DELETE handlers + the PATCH-restore branch); UI hides the Archive/Restore buttons for anyone without it. **(4) Edit UI (the "API exists, UI doesn't" set).** Edit dialogs for deal ([edit-deal-dialog.tsx](src/crm/components/edit-deal-dialog.tsx) — name/company find-or-create/value/currency/close/event), account, and contact; a **new contact detail sheet** ([crm-contact-detail-sheet.tsx](src/crm/components/crm-contact-detail-sheet.tsx), opened by row click — contacts previously had none) with edit + archive + History. **Adopted going forward: section-by-section CRM work** (deals → companies → contacts → tasks, each gated + tested + pushed on its own); this cohesive change shipped as one exception per owner. +15 archive/activity/diff tests; existing CRM service tests adapted (the new before-snapshot `findFirst`). Full gate green: tsc, eslint, **2911 tests**, build. Status board: [docs/CRM_STATUS.html](docs/CRM_STATUS.html) §4 updated; invariants in [src/crm/README.md](src/crm/README.md) §3.6. **Not deployed** — the migration has not been applied to prod (consistent with the rest of the CRM module).
- **Contacts production review — 3 of 4 HIGHs shipped (July 13–14, 2026, `a0744ef` + `5849962`)** — First independent review of the contacts/CRM domain: **0 BLOCKER / 4 HIGH / 12 MED / 7 LOW**. **(3) H4 — `speaker-service.updateSpeaker()` extraction (`5849962`, cross-caller #6).** MCP `update_speaker` synced only `{email, firstName, lastName}` to the org Contact store while the REST PUT synced ~13 fields — and because **`syncToContact` is enrich-only, a name+email payload against an existing contact is a silent NO-OP** (the call succeeded, logged nothing, changed nothing), so **every agent/n8n speaker edit — phone, affiliation, job title — never reached the CRM**, and since the EU mirror enriches its scalars from Contact, never reached the mirror either. The root cause is the **duplication, not the payload**: only `createSpeaker` had been extracted, so the UPDATE stayed mirrored across two ~full implementations and drifted (the identical class fixed for registrations on July 13). **Fixed by extraction, not a patched payload** — the new service owns the optimistic-locked write, the tag mirror onto the registration facet, the decline cascade, the FULL contact sync, the audit row and the stats refresh; REST keeps auth/`denyReviewer`/`EMAIL_IMMUTABLE`/Zod/event-org-lookup/HTTP mapping, MCP keeps loose-input coercion + JSON-RPC shape. **Extra drift found while extracting:** the MCP audit row recorded *status only* (now full before/after snapshots, so the Activity timeline can diff), the write now binds `{id, eventId}` (a mis-scoped agent call can't touch a sibling event's speaker), stats refresh the speaker's **own** event (was `ctx.eventId`), and `photo` is coerced instead of blind-cast (`input.photo as string | null` let a non-string reach Prisma raw); the REST audit write became fire-and-forget-with-logged-catch (M13 class). **+20 tests whose key guard asserts the EFFECT, not the call** — a test that only checked "`syncToContact` was called" would have **passed against the bug**; all 2666 pre-existing tests (incl. every REST speaker-route test) pass unchanged through the delegation. No MCP schema change → no pkg bump. **(4) M3 — the same bug in the bulk path (`ba69eab`).** `create_registrations_bulk` passed only `{email, firstName, lastName}` to `syncToContact` while the Attendee row got title/organization/jobTitle/phone/country/specialty/registrationType — so a **100-row agent/n8n import produced 100 husk CRM rows** (and husks in the EU mirror, which enriches from Contact). It survived the H4 extraction because **bulk paths are deliberately NOT service-backed** (different mechanics: per-row error capture, `createMany`). Fixed the drift **mechanism**: the row's optional fields were hand-rebuilt in **three** places (Attendee row, confirmation email, contact sync) — now one parsed `attendeeFields` object feeds all three, and the Prisma enum cast stays on the Prisma call rather than leaking `as never` into the shared payload (which would have silently defeated type-checking at the `syncToContact` boundary — the very boundary the finding is about). +3 tests, **verified to fail against the pre-fix code**; one pins Attendee-vs-Contact field equality so they can't drift again. **The enrich-only-sync bug class is now closed on every single-write and bulk path.** **Still open: H3** (the EU mirror never learns about a rename/merge/delete — **plan + owner decisions written** in ROADMAP §"H3 — mirror retraction": tombstone the old email inside the mutation tx, then a worker `PATCH ea_synced = false`; **never hard-delete**, since the table is shared with other sources) and the duplicate-contact backfill. Full report at [docs/CODE_REVIEW_CONTACTS.html](docs/CODE_REVIEW_CONTACTS.html) (browseable at `/admin/docs`; same teaching format as the certificates/accommodation reports — quoted code + failure scenario + a "what to learn" box per finding, plus a §Lessons index). Recorded first as a **document-only** round (stabilization-first posture, [docs/CRM_MODULE_PLAN.md](docs/CRM_MODULE_PLAN.md)); the owner then un-deferred the **two live-impact HIGHs**, shipped July 14. **Everything else is tracked in [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md) §"Contacts review"**. **(1) H1 — the CRM read gate.** The four contacts READ routes (list / detail / export / tags) authorized on `getOrgContext` **alone** — `denyReviewer` guards only the writes — and since the June-16 internal-domain rule **ONSITE (per-event desk temps) and internal-domain REGISTRANTs are org-bound**, so either could call `/api/contacts/export` and download the **entire org CRM** (every contact's email, phone, bio and the organizer's private `notes`) as a CSV, un-audited and un-rate-limited. Same class as check-in H7/H8 (the guard sat on the POST). New **[src/lib/contact-visibility.ts](src/lib/contact-visibility.ts)** — `canViewContacts()` + `denyContactAccess()` (logs its own refusal so no call site can forget; fails closed). **Owner decision: staff (SUPER_ADMIN/ADMIN/ORGANIZER) + MEMBER + API keys may read; ONSITE / REGISTRANT / REVIEWER / SUBMITTER get 403.** It is deliberately **its own boundary** — `denyReviewer` is a write guard that blocks MEMBER (who IS allowed to read the CRM), `FINANCE_ROLES` includes ONSITE (who is not), and `BARCODE_ROLES` is the exact inverse — the same "none of the existing predicates has the right shape" reasoning that produced `barcode-visibility.ts`. The **export** additionally writes an `EXPORT` audit row (who / when / row count / role / IP) and is **rate-limited 10/hr/org**. **(2) H2 — email normalization.** The REST contact-create path was the **only** writer that didn't lowercase the email (`syncToContact`, MCP `create_contact`, both imports and the email PATCH all do) while `@@unique([organizationId, email])` is **case-sensitive** — so an admin adding `John@Hospital.com` plus a later `syncToContact` lowercasing to `john@hospital.com` minted **two contacts for one person**, and the central sync (which dedups by lowercased email, last-write-wins) then **silently mirrored only one of the pair**. Now trim+lowercase via `z.preprocess` **before** validation (so a pasted trailing space is accepted, not 400'd); the create's P2002 race maps to **409** instead of a 500 echoing the raw Prisma message. **⚠ No backfill was run** — duplicate pairs minted before July 14 remain; a merge script is tracked in ROADMAP. +51 tests (suite 2615 → 2666); tsc/eslint/vitest/build green. **Coverage caveat:** 3 of 4 angles completed (RBAC/PII · concurrency/sync-integrity · drift/logging); the lifecycle angle died on an infra error and was not re-run. **Foundations verified clean:** cross-tenant IDOR (every lookup binds `organizationId`), MCP org binding (injected from the API key, never tool input), the May-18 write-guard fix, CSV formula-injection escaping, email-change P2002→409. **The 4 HIGHs, all OPEN:** **H1** — the contacts **read** routes (`GET /api/contacts`, `/export`, `/tags`, detail) authorize on `getOrgContext` alone (`denyReviewer` guards only writes), and ONSITE / MEMBER / internal-domain REGISTRANT are all org-bound ⇒ **a temp desk worker can export the entire org CRM** — every contact's email, phone, bio and private `notes` — un-audited, un-rate-limited (same class as check-in H7/H8). **H2** — the REST contact-create path is the **only** writer that doesn't lowercase the email while the unique index is case-sensitive ⇒ `John@Hospital.com` + a later `syncToContact` mints **two contacts for one person**, and the central sync (which dedups by lowercased email, last-write-wins) then **silently never mirrors one of them**. **H3** — the EU `contacts_centralv1` mirror is **email-keyed and append-only**, so a rename/merge/delete never propagates: fixing a typo'd email leaves the old address in the mirror **forever**, looking like a current EA-maintained person (and that table feeds `mailchimp_*`); the nightly reconcile only upserts, so it cannot heal it. **H4** — **MCP `update_speaker` syncs name+email only** while the REST PUT syncs ~12 fields ⇒ agent/n8n speaker edits never reach the Contact store (and being enrich-only, the payload is a silent no-op) — the exact class already fixed for registrations on July 13, still live for speakers because the speaker **update** was never service-extracted. **Notable MEDs:** `syncToContact` is check-then-act on a unique index and its P2002 loser is swallowed (an `eventId` + all enrich data lost, unhealable by the reconcile); **audit coverage is 2 of 9 mutation paths — `DELETE` writes no audit row**; MCP `create_registrations_bulk` also syncs name+email only; tag normalization is skipped by 2 of 5 writers (agent-created `committee` is invisible to a `Committee` filter — the n8n/Webflow pain at its source); the two "import contacts" features have **opposite** semantics on existing rows; SSRF via `downloadExternalPhoto` (no host allowlist on the EventsAir photo fetch); the central-sync error path can log **attendee emails** (they're in the PostgREST URL); both central-sync jobs are exposed to the **P3 pooler advisory-lock stall** (the mirror can stop silently at debug level). **Flagged for the owner:** the **central sync is org-blind by design** (no `organizationId` filter; its registration join has no `where` at all) — a **hard blocker for white-label**, belongs in MULTI_TENANCY_IMPACT.
- **Accommodation / hotels production review — security + counter-integrity batch shipped in 3 phases (July 13, 2026)** — First full 4-angle review of the accommodation domain (booking lifecycle · RBAC/info-exposure · concurrency/counter integrity · drift/logging): **0 BLOCKER / 8 HIGH / 10 MED / 5 LOW** — the worst of any domain, because these routes predate the IDOR + logging sweeps applied elsewhere. Full report at [docs/CODE_REVIEW_ACCOMMODATION.html](docs/CODE_REVIEW_ACCOMMODATION.html) (browseable at `/admin/docs`), written as a **teaching document**: a "three mistakes" primer (check-then-act on a stale read · unguarded counter moves · trusting a nested id from the URL) then every finding with the buggy code, the failure, the fix, and a "what a junior dev should learn" box. Remaining M/Ls deferred to [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md) §"Accommodation / hotels review". **(1) `7fcb256` — security.** **H1**: all three handlers in [rooms/[roomId]/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/hotels/%5BhotelId%5D/rooms/%5BroomId%5D/route.ts) resolved the room by `{ id: roomId, hotelId }` — the event was org-checked but the **hotel was never bound to the event**, so the authorization chain broke in the middle and a caller could pass ANOTHER org's hotelId+roomId against their own eventId (GET dumped that org's guest PII + barcodes; PUT rewrote their pricing/capacity; DELETE removed the room type). The sibling `rooms/route.ts` always bound `hotel.findFirst({ id: hotelId, eventId })` — pure drift, one file. **H2**: the accommodation detail GET, the PUT response, and the room GET embedded the **full `Registration` row** via `include: { registration: { include: { attendee: true } } }` — carrying `qrCode` + `dtcmBarcode` (physical-access credentials) with **no redaction**, walking straight past the July-11 `barcode-visibility` boundary whose whole point is that MEMBER must not hold a door credential. Replaced with an explicit allow-list `select` (a sensitive column added to Registration later can't leak by default) + composed barcode/finance redaction. **(2) `71ce307` — the counter family, fixed as ONE thing.** `bookedRooms` wasn't conserved because release/claim decisions were made from stale reads and written unguarded. **H3** was deterministic — *no race required*: the PUT moved the counter from **two independent blocks** (room-type change; status change) that didn't know about each other, and the status applier was always handed the OLD roomTypeId — so changing a booking's room type AND cancelling it in one save released the old type **twice** and left a permanent phantom claim on the new one; changing the room type of an already-CANCELLED booking moved counters for a room it didn't hold. Fixed structurally with a pure **`planRoomTransition(prev, next)`** ([accommodation-rooms.ts](src/lib/accommodation-rooms.ts)) that derives the single net movement from the whole before→after pair (same shape as `planSeatTransition`), so double-counting is no longer expressible. **H5**: the status transition was check-then-act — `prevStatus` came from a pre-tx read and the row write's only precondition was the **optional** `expectedUpdatedAt` token, so two tabs both cancelling both released a room (an optional guard is not a guard); the row is now claimed FIRST, conditional on the status the plan was derived from, and the loser touches no counter (same fix on the MCP twin). **H6**: DELETE decided whether to release from a pre-tx status read → a concurrent cancel meant a double release; the DELETE now carries its own precondition. **M1**: every release was a bare `{ decrement: 1 }` with no floor — and negative is worse than wrong, because `available = totalRooms − bookedRooms` then EXCEEDS totalRooms and the `bookedRooms < totalRooms` guard admits more bookings than rooms exist (a counting bug silently becoming **physical overbooking**); `releaseRoom()` is now guarded like `releaseSeat()`. **M4**: lowering `totalRooms` was check-then-act in both REST + MCP → the condition is now part of the write (409 `TOTAL_BELOW_BOOKED`). **(3) `ce7ae60` — the cascade hole + data repair.** **H4**: `Accommodation` has `onDelete: Cascade` from BOTH Registration and Speaker — and **a DB cascade fires no application code**, so deleting a registrant made the booking row vanish while `bookedRooms` kept counting it *forever*; the room type then reports SOLD OUT with an empty room and every future booking fails `NO_ROOMS_AVAILABLE`, with no recovery short of hand-written SQL. The delete transactions already released the ticket seat + promo usage; accommodation was simply missed. New `releaseRoomForDeletedPerson()` called inside the delete tx on **all three** cascade paths (registration delete; speaker delete — which wasn't even in a transaction; the speaker's companion registration). New [scripts/reconcile-bookedrooms.ts](scripts/reconcile-bookedrooms.ts) recomputes counters from row-truth, **reusing the same `holdsRoom()` predicate the runtime uses** so script and runtime can't disagree. **Prod dry-run: 6 room types scanned, 0 drift** — the counters are clean because accommodation is lightly used so far, which is *why* these hadn't bitten yet, not evidence they were harmless. +24 tests (suite 2535 → 2559); each phase verified tsc/eslint/vitest/build green. **Deferred (ROADMAP):** H7 (~30 unlogged failure paths incl. 3 business 400s; the REST create logs none of the service's 10 rejection codes while the MCP twin does), H8+M10 (the dashboard swallows `!res.ok` on hotel/room save + delete — "the button does nothing"), M2 (guest count never re-checked on edit), M3 (no server-side status state machine — MCP can push CANCELLED→CHECKED_OUT, which *re-claims* a room), M5 (P2002 → opaque UNKNOWN), M6/M7/M8/M9 and the LOWs.

- **Certificates production review — BLOCKER + all 5 HIGHs + M1–M5 remediated in 4 phases (July 13, 2026, pkg 0.4.19→0.4.20)** — A 4-angle review (issue lifecycle · security/SSRF/injection · concurrency/idempotency · drift/duplication/logging) of the certificates domain produced **1 BLOCKER / 5 HIGH / 9 MED / 7 LOW**; full report with quoted code + failure scenarios + a per-finding "what a junior dev should learn" box in [docs/CODE_REVIEW_CERTIFICATES.html](docs/CODE_REVIEW_CERTIFICATES.html) (browseable at `/admin/docs`), remaining M/Ls deferred to [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md) §"Certificates review — deferred findings". All shipped same-day, one gated commit per phase. **(1) `2c32d21` — B1 (BLOCKER): the `backgroundPdfUrl` file-read/SSRF chain.** `CertificateTemplate.backgroundPdfUrl` was stored with zero shape validation (REST `z.string().max(500)`; MCP prefix-only `LOCAL_URL_RE` — `/uploads/../../.env` passed) and TWO readers consumed it with NO guard, bypassing the July-9 hardened `loadCertificatePdfBytes` they were meant to use: `render.ts fetchBackgroundPdf` (`readFile(cwd/public/url)` no traversal check + bare `fetch` no allowlist) and the `/duplicate` route's `fetchBackgroundBuffer` — which then **re-uploads the fetched bytes to a world-readable `/uploads` URL and returns it**, turning arbitrary-file-read into a public exfiltration channel (`DATABASE_URL`, `NEXTAUTH_SECRET`, Stripe keys) and SSRF into readable output, reachable by any ORGANIZER or MCP key. Fix = validate on write (new `validateBackgroundPdfUrl()` in [pdf-loader.ts](src/lib/certificates/pdf-loader.ts) — local must be `/uploads/certificates/` with no `..` segment/NUL; remote https on the Supabase allowlist; wired into both REST Zod + the MCP validator) AND guard on read (both fetch helpers delegate to the hardened loader, which gained a 15s timeout). +11 tests. **(2) `bc06124` — H1/H2/H3.** **H1**: worker run-state transitions were unconditional `update`-by-id, so a Cancel committing ms before a phase-complete write was silently resurrected (manual→AWAITING_REVIEW, or auto→SENDING, which then emailed the cancelled certs) — new `transitionRunStatus()` does a conditional `updateMany` on the expected prior status across all four phase-complete sites + `failRun` (never overwrites a terminal run), mirroring the July-11 comms worker fix that was never carried here. **H2**: a missing/unfetchable background PDF silently issued + emailed the "No background PDF uploaded yet" placeholder as a real cert (serial + audit + no review gate) — `renderCertificate` now THROWS on real issue paths; only preview opts in via `{ allowPlaceholder: true }`. **H3**: the auto-issue sweep suppressed duplicates only against `autoIssue:true` runs, so a manual run started seconds earlier never suppressed the auto-sweep and BOTH emailed the same cert (the July bundle rework removed the fail-at-link net that made this a prior "false positive") — the guard now matches any NON-TERMINAL run (manual OR auto), excluding FAILED/CANCELLED so nobody is stranded. **(3) `05f0695` — H4/H5.** **H4**: the template `/duplicate` route hand-listed copied fields and silently dropped `role`/`cmeHours`/`autoIssueOnSurvey`/`autoIssueTag` (duplicating a CME cert → blank `{{cmeHours}}`; duplicating an auto-issue template → a clone that silently never auto-issued) — now copies role/cmeHours/autoIssueTag; `autoIssueOnSurvey` is forced OFF (a live clone would instantly double-issue the source tag audience) + returns `{ autoIssuePaused }`. **H5**: deleted the dead `POST .../certificates/issued/[id]/resend` route (449 LOC, zero callers) + `useResendCertificate` hook + its test — an orphaned 4th cover-email pipeline hand-rolled inline that had already drifted off the audit-copy (`storeBody`) contract. **(4) `a4b080d` — M1–M5.** **M1**: a P2002 on the GLOBAL `serial` index (cross-event collision — `serial` is globally unique with a non-unique `Event.code` prefix) was misdiagnosed as a recipient dup (wrong `ALREADY_ISSUED` / burned serials); new shared `isSerialCollision()` discriminates `err.meta.target` (durable `@@unique([eventId, serial])` deferred). **M2**: the auto-issue candidate query gained `status != CANCELLED` (cancel-after-survey inside the sweep+backoff window otherwise emailed a cert to a cancelled reg). **M3**: `precheckBulkEmailViability` now 400s `INVALID_FILTER` for a certificate send explicitly targeting CANCELLED (the "Cancelled Re-engagement" tile / MCP could otherwise mint real certs for cancelled regs). **M4**: the worker send phase now resolves a multi-cert bundle cover via the editable `certificate-bundle-delivery` template before the hardcoded default (the one send path that skipped it, so an edited bundle cover was ignored on auto bundles). **M5**: the legacy `/api/cron/certificate-issues` shim got a loud DEPRECATED-ROLLBACK-HANDLE guard + a runtime warn (wiring the real advisory lock would couple src→worker and wouldn't hold across the transaction pooler anyway — P3 limitation). **Docs**: `CERTIFICATES.md` corrected (M7 per-template-not-per-category uniqueness + the global-serial note; L5 stale tick "60s"→"every 3 min" + 5MB→10MB cap); the stale `abstractTitle`-XSS ROADMAP item struck (M8 — already fixed under `escapeDynamic`). Also fixed a **pre-existing lint failure** on clean HEAD (`35e8c19` — `mcp-bulk-parity.test.ts` had 10 `no-explicit-any` errors the prior "green" claim missed). +25 tests (suite 2535 → net 2535 after deleting the ~20-case dead-route test); every phase verified tsc/eslint/vitest/build green. **Deferred (ROADMAP):** M6 (send-phase crash windows), M9 (`duplicate_certificate_template` MCP tool), the `@@unique([eventId,serial])` durable fix, L1–L4/L6/L7.

- **Services parity batch — `updateRegistration()` extraction + MCP bulk/send parity (July 13, 2026, pkg 0.4.18→0.4.19)** — Two gated commits closing the biggest remaining cross-caller duplication + the MCP-parity MED cluster. **(1) `a0b427f` — `registration-service.updateRegistration()` (cross-caller #5):** the registration-update body (sponsor INCLUSIVE invariant, billing-account + ticket-type/tier validation, shared repricing, seat/promo transition, optimistic lock, attendee patch, audit/sync/stats/checkout-expiry fan-out) now lives in ONE service; the REST PUT + MCP `update_registration` are thin delegations (REST keeps auth/EMAIL_IMMUTABLE/Zod/financials/redaction; MCP keeps loose-input parsing). Drift fixed in the extraction: **M1** the lookup binds `{id, eventId}` (a mis-scoped agent call can't touch a sibling event's registration), **M7** the sponsor invariant is change-scoped on MCP too, **L4** MCP attendee empty-strings clear to null, MCP audits now carry full before/after snapshots (Activity-diff-compatible) + full-merge Contact sync, and the REST audit write became fire-and-forget (M13 class). - **Per-event presentation-type offering (July 13, 2026, organizer request)** — Organizers now choose WHICH presentation types their event's abstract form offers ("abstracts to have Oral/Poster, Oral, Poster, Video — but not to show all; show what the organizer chooses"). **Storage:** `Event.settings.abstractPresentationTypes` (JSON string array — no migration); **owner decisions:** all five types (incl. Workshop) stay pickable in the organizer's list, and an **unconfigured event offers all five** (existing events unchanged). - **Blind-review integrity (abstracts H8/H9) + bulk-email filter guard (comms M7) (July 13, 2026, pkg 0.4.17→0.4.18)** — The remaining genuinely-open abstracts HIGHs plus the MCP/API over-send hazard. **(1) H9a — author decision email anonymized:** `consolidateReviewNotes` ([src/lib/abstract-review.ts](src/lib/abstract-review.ts)) prefixed each note with the reviewer's NAME — every multi-reviewer decision email broke blind review while the dashboard deliberately anonymized the author's view. Now numbered (`— Reviewer N:`); single note stays bare; format pinned by tests so attribution can't quietly return. **(2) H9b — submissions GET view matrix tightened:** the full per-reviewer view (identities/notes/per-criterion) was granted to ANY org-attached role via a bare `isOrgMember` check — **MEMBER** (read-only, sponsor-side per the docs) saw everything. Full view is now org STAFF (ADMIN/SUPER_ADMIN/ORGANIZER) + pool reviewers only; MEMBER/ONSITE get the same anonymized shape the submitter gets ([submissions/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/abstracts/%5BabstractId%5D/submissions/route.ts)). **(3) H8 — MCP `assign_reviewer_to_abstract` now honors `conflictFlag`:** the schema advertised it, the executor dropped it — "assign Dr X, flag the conflict" returned success with NO flag while COI has been an *enforcement* input since June 26 (a conflicted reviewer is blocked from scoring), so the dropped flag let their score count. Persisted on create + toggleable on the idempotent upsert (REST parity), audited with `previousConflictFlag`; **MCP clients reconnect** (pkg bumped). **(4) Comms M7 — a bad filter value no longer silently widens the audience:** a typo'd `status`/`paymentStatus` ("CONFIRMD", "PAID,COMPLIMENTRY") used to fail its safeParse, silently drop the predicate, and send to **everyone** (a reminder re-admitting CANCELLED) — unreachable from the dialog but fully reachable via MCP/REST/n8n. New `assertValidBulkEmailFilters()` in [src/lib/bulk-email.ts](src/lib/bulk-email.ts) rejects any unknown value (ANY bad token in a comma list; "all" sentinel passes) with 400 `INVALID_FILTER`, wired through `precheckBulkEmailViability` so the enqueue + schedule routes 400 synchronously and a legacy persisted row fails loudly at fire time; the abstracts `status as never` cast (cryptic Prisma throw) replaced with a validated parse. +17 tests (suite 2469 → 2486); tsc/eslint/vitest/build green.

- **Door-day batch + refund credit-note amount gate (July 11, 2026, pkg 0.4.16→0.4.17)** — The roadmap's "fix before the next live event" cluster plus the one deferred money-gate item, shipped as one verified batch with three owner decisions locked in. **(1) Gate policy (check-in M2) — DECIDED, no behavior change:** FAILED + REFUNDED stay **admitted** at the door (a failed charge attempt / goodwill refund doesn't bar entry); pinned as an explicit owner decision in `isPaymentAdmissible`'s comment ([src/lib/check-in.ts](src/lib/check-in.ts)) + truth-table tests, so badges keep following automatically. **(2) Audited desk payment override (check-in M1):** `checkInGate` gained `allowPaymentDue`; the check-in POST accepts `{ overridePayment: true }` (desk-gated population; owner decision: covers ANY payment block — webhook-lagged PENDING, UNPAID, FAILED…), warn-logs `check-in:payment-override` + audits `paymentOverride`/`paymentStatusAtOverride`; gate rejections now carry a machine-readable `code`, and the registration detail sheet offers **"Admit anyway (override)"** when a check-in is refused PAYMENT_REQUIRED. **(3) Scanner honesty (M5/M6):** a venue-network drop mid-scan now beeps the failure tone + writes an explicit "Network error — NOT checked in" Recent-Scans row (+ clears the 2s same-code debounce so an immediate retry isn't swallowed), and a successful scan invalidates the registrations query so the attendance counter stays live instead of freezing ~5 min. **(4) DTCM import integrity (M3/M4 + half of L2):** every row runs in its own try/catch (P2002 → per-row "concurrent import" error; anything else → per-row error with a log pointer) so the report always survives; the email lookup is deterministic (non-cancelled preferred, newest first); replacing a different existing barcode is warn-logged. **(5) DECLINED speaker ⇒ companion cascade (the physical-access gap):** setting a speaker to DECLINED/CANCELLED used to leave their companion registration CONFIRMED — a valid badge + entry barcode forever. New `cascadeSpeakerDecline()` + `isSpeakerDeclineTransition()` in [src/services/speaker-service.ts](src/services/speaker-service.ts) — ONE implementation for both status-write callers (REST speaker PUT + MCP `update_speaker`), delegating the cancel to `payment-service.cancelRegistration` (refund:false) so seat/promo/audit/checkout-cleanup ride the single cancel op. **Companion-only by owner decision** (declining to speak ≠ not attending): a real linked registration is never touched — the UI/agent get a "review it separately" note. Both speaker detail surfaces (page + sheet) intercept the decline save and prompt **"Cancel registration too (revokes badge + entry barcode)" vs "Keep registration"**; MCP `update_speaker` gained `cancelCompanionRegistration` (keep-by-default; **MCP clients reconnect** — pkg bumped). Cascade audited (`SPEAKER_COMPANION_CANCELLED`). **(6) Refund credit-note AMOUNT gate (July 7 review M2, closed):** `refundRegistration` previously only checked a non-cancelled CN *existed* — a $1 CN unlocked a $500 refund. Now cumulative `refundedAfter` may not exceed **Σ non-cancelled CN totals**; new `CREDIT_NOTE_INSUFFICIENT` (409) with `{creditedTotal, refundedBefore, requested, maxRefundable}`; the refund dialog caps + pre-fills at `min(remaining, credited − refunded)` and routes the 409 to the credit-note dialog. Also verified in-round: the registrations-review **M4** ("refund routes whole balance through newest payment") was a **stale finding** — already fixed by `1191b25`'s multi-payment slicing. +13 tests (suite 2456 → 2469); tsc/eslint/vitest/build green.

- **Communications / bulk-email production review — anti-double-send batch shipped in 3 phases (July 11, 2026)** — A 4-angle review (send lifecycle · RBAC/info-exposure · concurrency/idempotency · drift/duplication/logging) of the bulk-email domain produced **0 BLOCKER / 2 HIGH / 7 MED / 6 LOW**; full report in [docs/CODE_REVIEW_COMMUNICATIONS.html](docs/CODE_REVIEW_COMMUNICATIONS.html) (browseable at `/admin/docs`), M/Ls deferred to [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md) §"Communications / bulk-email review". The send core is genuinely well-built (logContext threaded, no swallowed send errors, atomic row claims, a real slug-drift test) — findings clustered on **duplicate/mis-targeted sends**. The owner chose the **anti-double-send batch** (H1/H2/M1/M2/M3/M6), shipped one gated commit per phase. **(1) `fadfc44` — route layer.** **H2**: the "Send now" route ([emails/bulk/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/emails/bulk/route.ts)) did `db.scheduledEmail.create` with no dedup, so a double-click / HTTP-retry of the 202 made two identical rows and the worker drained both (whole audience twice; the 20/hr limit fit both, in-memory per-container = ~2× during blue/green) — now a best-effort content+2min window returns the existing jobId. **M2**: the route only shape-validated before enqueue, so every real viability check (untagged cert template, missing agreement template, unbuilt survey, deactivated custom slug) fired only at worker time — a green "queued" toast then a FAILED row a minute later; extracted the checks from `executeBulkEmail` into a shared **`precheckBulkEmailViability()`** (one impl, no drift) that both the enqueue + schedule routes call synchronously → a real 4xx now, plus fixed the stale worker comment claiming a synchronous 400 still exists. **M3**: the schedule-edit PATCH ([schedule/[id]/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/emails/schedule/%5Bid%5D/route.ts)) replaced the whole `filters` JSON with a `{status,ticketTypeId}`-only schema, stripping send-critical keys (`templateSlug`/`certificateTemplateIds`/`surveyExpiryDays`/`paymentStatus`/`ticketTypeIds`/…) — `filters` removed from the edit schema (the dialog never edits it; audience changes = cancel+recreate). **(2) `1e7c45e` — worker layer.** **M1**: the 10-min stuck-sweep keyed on `updatedAt` with no heartbeat during a send, so a legitimately long send (thousands of recipients / per-recipient PDF gen) was flipped to FAILED mid-flight and resurrectable into a concurrent second send, and `processRow`'s completion write was unconditional-by-id → a 2-min heartbeat (no-op `retryCount` increment refreshes `@updatedAt`) keeps a live send from being swept, and the SENT/SENT-0/FAILED writes became conditional `updateMany(where:{id,status:PROCESSING})` — a superseded completion logs `completion-superseded` + skips the audit/notify instead of clobbering + double-notifying. **(3) `5d03569` — additive migration `20260711120000`.** **H1**: `executeBulkEmail` had zero per-recipient idempotency — any re-run re-emailed everyone; after a genuine crash mid-send (row swept FAILED → operator Retry) the delivered portion got a second email. New `ScheduledEmail.emailedKeys String[] @default([])` (blue-green safe); the send skips `alreadyEmailedKeys` and reports each batch's sent ids via `onBatchEmailed` (worker appends via `{ push }`), so a retry resumes; certificate sends unaffected (own issue-or-reuse). **M6** closed for free: the survey-invitation token re-mint (`deleteMany`+`create`) sits below the skip filter, so an already-emailed recipient's link is never invalidated on a re-run. +19 tests (suite 2438 → 2456); each phase verified tsc/eslint/vitest/build green. **Deferred (ROADMAP):** M4 (`email-preview` org-null collapse — mitigated by `denyReviewer` today), M5 (recipient-count predicate triplicated; speakers copy already missing `sessionRole` → latent count≠send), ~~M7~~ (**✅ SHIPPED July 13, `46330af`** — `assertValidBulkEmailFilters` rejects unparsable filter values with 400 `INVALID_FILTER` instead of silently widening the audience; also closed the abstracts `status as never` LOW), and the LOWs (unlogged post-auth rejection cluster; `presentationDetails` raw HTML; preview rate limit; legacy-cron advisory-lock gaps).


- **Check-in "Print All" bounded + unknown-barcode logging — H4/H5 fixed; all 8 HIGHs of the check-in review now shipped (July 11, 2026, `935c1f7`)** — Phase 3, the last of the check-in/badges HIGHs. **H4**: "Print All" rendered every barcode with a bare `Promise.all(registrations.map(...))` — up to ~2000 simultaneous CPU-bound `bwip-js` rasterizations building the whole PDF in one request, on the single box that also serves the live scanner + the Stripe webhook, so a "Print All" during the arrival rush stalled the door. New **[src/lib/concurrency.ts](src/lib/concurrency.ts)** `mapWithConcurrency` (no new dep) caps in-flight renders at 8 (barcodes deduped first); a per-request cap of 2500 via `take: cap+1` returns 400 `BADGE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED` over it (batch instead of freeze), logged. Worker-tier offload stays deferred. **H5**: the unknown-barcode scan (the highest-value line to trace at a live door) now logs at warn (eventId + userId — never the raw scanned code, a credential), along with the check-in POST/PUT event-not-found (the ONSITE cross-event denial), registration-not-found, QR missing-code, and all four import/barcodes 400s. +5 tests (suite 2433 → 2438). **The check-in/badges review is now HIGH-complete** across three phases: door correctness (H1/H2/H3/M7 `706ba17`), credential exposure (H6/H7/H8/L4 `aac727a`), Print All + logging (H4/H5 `935c1f7`); 2401 → 2438. ~~**Deferred (ROADMAP):** the gate-policy MEDs (M1/M2), DTCM-import integrity (M3/M4/L2), and scanner UX (M5/M6)~~ — **✅ all closed July 11 (`b55a18c`, the door-day batch)**: M1 audited desk payment override (any payment block); M2 DECIDED as-is (FAILED/REFUNDED stay admitted — explicit owner call, pinned in `isPaymentAdmissible`); M3 per-row try/catch; M4 deterministic email match; M5 live counter; M6 failure beep + NOT-checked-in row; L2 half (overwrite warn-logged).


- **Check-in credential exposure — H6/H7/H8 fixed (July 11, 2026, `aac727a`)** — Phase 2 of the check-in/badges review. `Registration.qrCode` (the entry barcode) and `dtcmBarcode` (the Dubai DTCM credential) are **physical-access credentials** that were returned via `include:` on both registration GETs and were **not** in `FINANCIAL_KEYS`, so `redactFinancialFields` never stripped them. New **[src/lib/barcode-visibility.ts](src/lib/barcode-visibility.ts)** is the single source of truth (`canViewEntryBarcode()` + `redactBarcodeFields()`) — deliberately its **own** boundary, NOT finance: `FINANCE_ROLES` includes MEMBER + ONSITE, but **MEMBER** (a read-only sponsor-side observer) must NOT hold a door credential while **ONSITE** (desk staff who print badges) MUST, so the set is SUPER_ADMIN/ADMIN/ORGANIZER/ONSITE + API keys. **H7**: the registrations LIST GET (no `denyReviewer` — it guards the POST; `buildEventAccessWhere` grants org-attached callers the event) now strips barcodes unless `canViewEntryBarcode`, composed with the finance redaction (MEMBER keeps finance, loses barcodes; an internal-domain REGISTRANT can't harvest every barcode). **H8**: the detail GET bound the row only to `{ id, eventId }` so an external REGISTRANT could fetch any registration's full payload by id — org-null REGISTRANTs are now bound to their own `userId`; and the registrant barcode-PNG route's org-staff branch org-scoped event-wide (ONSITE could cross events) now routes through `buildEventAccessWhere` (assignment-scoped for ONSITE via `settings.onsiteUserIds`), plus a 120/hr per-user rate limit (L4). MCP `list_registrations` still returns barcodes (org-API-key/ADMIN-equivalent, per the "API key = admin" model). +20 tests (suite 2413 → 2433). **Deferred (ROADMAP):** H4 (Print All unbounded at scale), H5 (unknown-barcode scan logs nothing) + the gate-policy/import/UX MEDs.


- **Check-in door-day correctness — H1/H2/H3 fixed (July 11, 2026, `706ba17`)** — Phase 1 of the check-in/badges production review ([docs/CODE_REVIEW_CHECKIN_BADGES.html](docs/CODE_REVIEW_CHECKIN_BADGES.html)), the three things that bite on the morning of day one. **H1 — badge = door parity.** The badge route filtered `PAID || complimentary`, silently dropping **INCLUSIVE** (sponsor-paid) and **UNASSIGNED** (pay-at-desk) delegates whom `checkInGate` admits — a pharma-sponsored VIP scanned in fine and had no badge, and selecting only that block yielded "No paid or complimentary registrations found", blaming them for not paying. New **`isPaymentAdmissible()`** in [check-in.ts](src/lib/check-in.ts) is the single source of truth for "does payment block entry?"; both the gate and the badge route derive from it, so they can't drift again (badge = everyone the door admits; the empty-result 400 is reworded + logged). **H2 — a real undo.** Nothing in `src/` ever wrote `checkedInAt: null` — the only affordance was flipping status back to CONFIRMED, which left `checkedInAt` set and made `checkInGate` refuse that attendee **forever** with ALREADY_CHECKED_IN while the attendance tile showed them as not in. New **`undoCheckIn()`** clears status + `checkedInAt` together via a conditional claim (idempotent), reverts to CONFIRMED, does NOT touch the seat (undo un-checks-in, it doesn't cancel), audits `CHECK_IN_UNDO`, no notification; new **`DELETE .../check-in`** handler (desk-gated, assignment-scoped, 404s logged) + an "Undo Check-in" button on the registration detail sheet. **H3 + M7 — race-safe commit.** `executeCheckIn` committed with an unconditional `update`-by-id, so two stations scanning one badge concurrently both passed the in-memory gate and both wrote (clobbered first-entry time, duplicate audit rows + admin notifications). It's now a **conditional claim** (`updateMany where { checkedInAt: null }`); the loser loads the already-checked-in row and returns it idempotently with no duplicate fan-out. For the reactivation path the claim gates `applyRegistrationTransition`, so two concurrent `allowCancelled` overrides can't double-increment the seat + promo counters (M7). All three callers (both REST handlers + MCP `check_in_registration`) share `check-in.ts`, so H3/M7 are fixed once for everyone. +12 tests (suite 2401 → 2413). **Deferred (ROADMAP):** H4 (Print All unbounded at scale), H5 (unknown-barcode scan logs nothing), **H6–H8** (qrCode/dtcmBarcode are physical-access credentials in the registration GET payloads, not in `FINANCIAL_KEYS`, so `redactFinancialFields` never strips them; list GET has no `denyReviewer`; detail GET is row-unscoped; the registrant barcode route lets ONSITE cross events), and the gate-policy/import/UX MEDs.


- **Program / agenda / sessions production review — 2 BLOCKERs + all 5 HIGHs remediated in 4 phases (July 10, 2026)** — A 4-angle review (scheduling lifecycle · RBAC & public exposure · concurrency/integrity · drift/failure-visibility) produced **2 BLOCKER / 5 HIGH / 9 MED / 5 LOW**; full report in [docs/CODE_REVIEW_PROGRAM_AGENDA.html](docs/CODE_REVIEW_PROGRAM_AGENDA.html) (browseable at `/admin/docs/CODE_REVIEW_PROGRAM_AGENDA.html`), M/Ls deferred to [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md) §"Program / agenda / sessions review". All shipped same-day, one gated commit per phase. **(1) `835c49d` — two live credential leaks.** **B1**: `GET /api/events/[eventId]/sessions` has **no `denyReviewer`** (the guard covers the POST) and `buildEventAccessWhere` grants org-null attendee roles the event by linkage — so any **REGISTRANT** could pull `zoomMeeting.startUrl` (the Zoom **host** start link), `streamKey` and `passcode`, and take host control of a live webinar. New [src/lib/zoom-visibility.ts](src/lib/zoom-visibility.ts) is the single source of truth (mirrors `finance-visibility`): `canViewZoomHostCredentials()` + `redactZoomHostFields()`; host roles = SUPER_ADMIN/ADMIN/ORGANIZER only, deliberately **narrower** than `FINANCE_ROLES` (MEMBER + ONSITE record payments but don't host webinars); API keys are admin-equivalent; `joinUrl` stays visible (it's the attendee link). **B2**: the public session-**detail** route imported no auth at all, accepted DRAFT events, returned `recordingUrl` + `recordingPassword`, and was the **only** public session route with **zero** rate limiting — the recording passcode for a paid/CME session was readable by anyone. New registration-gated [.../sessions/[sessionId]/recording](src/app/api/public/events/%5Bslug%5D/sessions/%5BsessionId%5D/recording/route.ts) mirrors `zoom-join`'s auth (org staff OR non-cancelled registration, session bound to the event, 60/hr, `no-store`); detail keeps only the non-secret `recordingStatus`, 404s DRAFT for non-org-staff (org staff keep their preview), and gained a 240/hr limit (M4). The session page fetches the credential on click (tab opened synchronously so popup blockers don't eat it) and surfaces 401/403/failure. **(2) `12e01d1` — new [src/services/session-service.ts](src/services/session-service.ts)**, done as an **extraction rather than a route patch** because H1/H4/L2 all converge on one place. **H1**: the REST PUT deleted and rebuilt every `SessionSpeaker` + `SessionTopic` **before** checking the optimistic lock, non-transactionally — a stale save destroyed the other editor's roster and *then* returned 409 "nothing was saved, reload"; a mid-loop failure truncated the agenda. The service now **claims the lock FIRST** inside a `$transaction`; parent update + both child replaces commit atomically or not at all. **H4**: MCP `create_session` wrote **no audit row** and sent **no admin notification** (every agent/n8n-created session was invisible in `AuditLog`) and silently dropped `status`, `abstractId` and topic `sortOrder`; capacity disagreed (REST `min(1)` vs MCP `Math.max(0,…)`) and MCP `update_session` allowed a **zero-duration** session REST rejects (L2). Both REST routes + both MCP executors now delegate; authorization stays at the boundary (route does the org-scoped event lookup, 404 not 403); the service never imports `next/server`. **(3) `ce1f635` — Zoom integrity.** New [src/lib/zoom/cleanup.ts](src/lib/zoom/cleanup.ts) `deleteRemoteZoomMeeting()` is the one teardown path for all three call sites and **never throws** (a Zoom outage must not fail a local op; an orphan costs capacity, not correctness). **H2**: the create route's existence check is check-then-act — two concurrent POSTs both called Zoom's create API before `ZoomMeeting.sessionId @unique` rejected the second **row**, leaving a live, **billable**, joinable meeting with no local record; the P2002 loser now tears down the meeting it just created and returns 409 `ZOOM_MEETING_EXISTS` (a failed rollback logs at `error` with the orphaned id). **H3**: session DELETE had **zero** Zoom references — it now tears the remote meeting down *before* the cascade removes the row that identifies it, and **refuses to delete the WEBINAR anchor session** (409 `WEBINAR_ANCHOR_SESSION`), which used to dangle `settings.webinar.sessionId` so the producer could never open the room again. **(4) `1d61af6` — H5**: swept every silent business rejection to zero across 9 session/track/public routes (bare 401 left unlogged, consistent with the payments M12 + abstracts M11 sweeps). +62 tests (suite 2374 → 2401). **Deferred (ROADMAP):** **M1** (`provisionWebinar`'s unlocked read→create window still mints two anchors + two billable webinars under concurrency), **M6** (retime never re-syncs Zoom), **M7/M8** (public agenda buckets days in the *viewer's* TZ while rendering times in the *event's*; the dashboard agenda uses hardcoded Asia/Dubai for the list and browser-local for the grid — neither the event's), **M2/M9/M10/M11** and L1–L5.

H5 (gate half): `computeSubmissionAggregates` exposes `scoredCount` and the gate counts SCORED submissions (an overallScore or non-empty criteriaScores), not rows. M4: the count read is now tx-consistent. **(4) `314e45e`** — H6 remainder: the `/my-reviews` portal feed filters DRAFT/WITHDRAWN out (they leaked as PENDING work), and both the REST + MCP reviewer-assignment paths refuse a non-reviewable target (`NOT_REVIEWABLE`). +34 tests across the phases (suite → 2336). REFUNDED) with truthful portal text; H2: `checkout.session.completed` now flags a payment landing on a **CANCELLED** reg (Payment row + PAID kept for money truth; docs email suppressed; error log + "issue a refund" admin alert); H3: checkout's post-Stripe "→ PENDING" write became a conditional claim (lost race → the just-created session is **expired**), closing the PAID→PENDING→UNPAID demotion/double-charge path. **(2) `b490392` charge-level webhook idempotency** — H1: idempotency re-keyed from "is the reg PAID?" to "was this payment intent recorded?" (`Payment.stripePaymentId` unique); a second real settlement (two tabs, or desk cash racing Stripe) is now RECORDED + flagged "⚠ Possible double payment" instead of silently dropped from the books; in-tx P2002 = already-processed; the duplicate-documents-email fallthrough is gone; M3: `charge.refunded` for an unknown intent on a <24h charge returns 500 so Stripe retries (out-of-order delivery no longer loses the refund forever). **(3) `b579bbe` crash-safe refunds** — H4/H5: new **`RefundAttempt`** table (migration `20260710120000`, additive) persisted atomically with the optimistic-lock claim BEFORE the Stripe call; the attempt id is the idempotency key AND rides in the refund's metadata, so every outcome is verifiable against Stripe — the error path **verifies before rolling back** (refund exists → success; provably absent → conditional rollback; unverifiable → booking kept + new 502 `REFUND_STATE_UNKNOWN`), and [src/lib/refund-reconciliation.ts](src/lib/refund-reconciliation.ts)'s sweep (rides the invoice-reconciliation worker tick, 10-min) settles stale PENDING/UNKNOWN attempts (confirm / roll back + alert / terminal manual-review). Kills both the book-a-refund-that-never-happened crash window and the idempotency-key wedge. **(4) `1191b25` multi-payment refunds** — H6/M4: new **`Payment.refundedAmount`** per-payment counter (migration `20260710130000`, additive + backfill); refunds **allocate across payments** (Stripe slices capped at each charge, manual remainder recorded, per-slice attempts; mid-plan failure → guarded-decrement un-booking + 502 `REFUND_PARTIALLY_COMPLETED`; `RefundSummary.slices[]`); `charge.refunded` reconciles per charge, so a prior manual refund can no longer eat a Dashboard refund's delta on mixed regs. **(5) `c480834` invoice IDOR + ONSITE finance scoping** — H9: `createInvoice` (+ the REST POST) binds the body registrationId to event+org (an organizer could mint an invoice from ANY registration, leaking its attendee/billing into this org's list + PDF; MCP already bound correctly); H10: the entire invoice/quote GET surface (list/create/detail/PDF/send/export/quote + 3 registrant staff branches) now routes through `buildEventAccessWhere` — ONSITE/MEMBER are finance-capable, so the July 7 desk-route fix's class also applied here; +6 isolation tests ([finance-cross-event-isolation.test.ts](__tests__/api/finance-cross-event-isolation.test.ts)). **(6) `da2531c` book-cooking writes** — H12: REST PUT + MCP single/bulk paymentStatus writes accept only the admin-settable subset (new `ADMIN_SETTABLE_PAYMENT_STATUSES`, drift-guarded against the UI's `MANUAL_PAYMENT_STATUSES`); "mark 200 regs REFUNDED" as a bare flag is rejected with a pointer to the gated refund flow; M6: MCP `update_invoice_status` narrowed to CANCELLED/OVERDUE (dashboard parity); pkg 0.4.15→0.4.16 (MCP clients reconnect). **(7) `48e7397` Dashboard-refund parity** — H11: the `charge.refunded` out-of-band branch now writes the REFUND_ISSUED audit row + admin notification and **no longer emails the attendee** (one policy across both refund entry points); CN recorded via `issueCreditNoteForRegistration` (send:false — also closes the old deferred silent-CN-cap-rejection). **(8) `fa96114` manual-capture truthfulness** — H7: a partial desk capture no longer flips full-PAID nor emails false full-total documents — PAID + documents only when the captured total covers the computed amount owed (same-currency; partials accumulate; foreign currency never counts); divergence warn+audit; 60/hr rate limit on the widest money-write population; M11: the route's hand-mirrored fan-out replaced by the shared `issuePaidRegistrationDocuments`.
