each phase verified tsc/eslint/vitest/build green.

- **Certificate resend previews + sent-email audit copy (July 10, 2026)** — Organizer request: "give a preview before resend, be it single or bundle, and save the html body." **(1) Preview before resend** — both confirm dialogs on the per-person Certificates card (per-row "Resend latest version" + "Resend all") now fetch and display a **read-only render of exactly what will be emailed** (To/Subject header + sandboxed iframe) before the operator confirms; a preview failure degrades to the old no-preview confirm with a warning, never blocking the resend. Backed by `POST .../certificates/issued/resend-preview` (60/hr/user) → `previewReissueEmail()` / `previewResendBundleEmail()` in [deliver.ts](src/lib/certificates/deliver.ts), which call the newly extracted **`renderBundleEmailContent()`** ([bundle.ts](src/lib/certificates/bundle.ts) — the content step of `sendCertificateBundleEmail`, so previews are byte-identical to sends by construction). **(2) Resend-bundle cover parity fix** — the "Resend all" route used only the hardcoded multi default; the shared `resolveResendBundleCover()` now routes 2+ certs through the editable `certificate-bundle-delivery` template on BOTH the send and its preview, and threads `recipientFirstName/LastName`. **(3) Sent-email audit copy** — new `EmailLog.htmlBody @db.Text` (additive migration `20260710160000_add_email_log_html_body`), populated only for opt-in senders via `EmailLogContext.storeBody` (set by `sendCertificateBundleEmail` → covers every cert email path: single/bundle/bulk/auto-issue/reissue); `getEmailLogsFor` strips the text and exposes a `hasBody` flag; `GET /api/email-logs/[id]/body` (org-scoped, denyReviewer) serves it; the [ActivityTimelineCard](src/components/activity/activity-timeline-card.tsx) shows a **"View email"** action on cert-email rows opening the stored copy in a sandboxed iframe dialog. Pre-migration rows have no copy (404 `NO_STORED_BODY`). +12 tests (5 preview services, 3 storeBody/hasBody mapping, +4 harness). Docs: CERTIFICATES.md §"Preview-before-resend", user-guide §18.
- **Certificate bulk send — audience is ALL registrations, tag is the only gate (July 10, 2026)** — Organizer-reported bug: the Communications **Send Certificates** tile pre-filtered recipients to `status: "CHECKED_IN"`, so CONFIRMED (never-scanned) registrants were invisible to the certificate send. Per the organizer's decision, **check-in does NOT gate certificates — the template tag is the only routing rule** ("no tag, no certificate"). Four coordinated changes: **(1) Tile** ([communications/page.tsx](src/app/%28dashboard%29/events/%5BeventId%5D/communications/page.tsx)) — `send-certificates` drops the CHECKED_IN pre-filter (`filters: {}`, `matches: r.status !== "CANCELLED"`); an explicit status filter in the dialog still narrows the send. **(2) Server guard** ([bulk-email.ts](src/lib/bulk-email.ts)) — the existing "no explicit status ⇒ exclude CANCELLED" rule (payment-reminder) now also applies to `emailType: "certificate"`, mirroring the Issue-tab eligibility rule (a cancelled reg can never be issued a cert via bulk email). **(3) Skip ≠ failure** ([bulk-issue.ts](src/lib/certificates/bulk-issue.ts)) — a recipient holding NONE of the selected templates' tags is now **skipped** (new `skippedCount` on the result + optional `BulkEmailResult.skippedCount`, per-recipient `cert-bulk:no-applicable-certs` warn kept), not counted as a per-recipient failure — before this, an all-registrations send with 50 tagged of 300 would have reported 250 "failures". The worker surfaces it in the `scheduled-email:sent` log, the audit row, and the admin notification message. **(4) count == send** — `BulkEmailEffectiveFilters` gained `emailType`, and both `recipientCountFor` implementations (Communications page + registrations list) exclude CANCELLED for certificate/payment-reminder counts when no explicit status is set. The manual Issue-tab flow was already correct (tag pool over non-CANCELLED, no check-in gate) — unchanged. +4 tests ([bulk-email-certificate-audience.test.ts](__tests__/lib/bulk-email-certificate-audience.test.ts): all-non-cancelled where, explicit-status respected, skippedCount passthrough, no guard on other types) + the zero-match test flipped to skip semantics. Docs: [docs/CERTIFICATES.md](docs/CERTIFICATES.md) §"Bulk-email certificate send" + user-guide (Communications callout + §18 pointer). tsc/eslint/vitest 2179/build green. **Same-day follow-up — certificate previews in the send dialog:** the dialog's footer **Preview** used to toast "Preview isn't available for this email type" for certificate sends (`emailTypeToSlug` → null; the cert cover email isn't an EmailTemplate slug). Now (a) **cover-email preview** — `POST /email-preview` accepts `slug: "certificate"` + `certificateTemplateIds` (1–5, event-bound, selection order preserved so the first template drives single-cover precedence), rendered by the new `buildCertCoverEmailPreview()` in [bundle.ts](src/lib/certificates/bundle.ts) (mirrors `coverEmailFor` precedence: custom override → single template's saved cover → category/multi system default; sample "Dr. Sample Attendee", PREVIEW-DRAFT serials, `speakerId: null` so `{{abstractTitle}}` can't leak a random speaker's abstract; real event branding; no DB writes); (b) **per-template PDF preview** — each row in the dialog's template picker links to the existing `GET /certificates/preview?templateId=…` sample PDF in a new tab (works for tagless templates too; the anchor sits outside the checkbox label so it never toggles selection). +5 precedence tests in [certificates-bundle.test.ts](__tests__/lib/certificates-bundle.test.ts). Suite 2198. **Cover-email source picker (same day, organizer request):** a **"Cover email"** dropdown in the certificate send dialog pre-fills the editable Subject/Message fields from (a) a selected certificate template's **saved cover** (edited in the cert template editor) or (b) a **saved email template** (active custom `EmailTemplate`s; `stripDocumentWrapper` applied) — "Certificate default" clears them. Pure pre-fill: the FIELDS drive the send (existing customSubject/customMessage pipeline — no backend send change, scheduled sends unaffected; deselecting the source cert template resets the picker to default without touching the copied fields). To make saved email templates render as covers, [email-tokens-resolver.ts](src/lib/certificates/email-tokens-resolver.ts) gained **`{{firstName}}`/`{{lastName}}`** (optional `CoverEmailTokenContext` fields threaded from bulk-send recipients + the preview; `firstName` falls back to full `recipientName` on the manual-Issue path — run items snapshot only the full name — and `lastName` to empty) plus **`{{eventDate}}`/`{{eventVenue}}`** aliases; [bundle.ts](src/lib/certificates/bundle.ts) `sendCertificateBundleEmail` accepts optional `recipientFirstName/LastName` (escaped on the HTML path, threaded by [bulk-issue.ts](src/lib/certificates/bulk-issue.ts)). +6 tests (5 resolver-token + 1 name-threading). Suite 2223. **Per-person Issue is now multi-select (same day, organizer request):** the registration/speaker detail-card "Issue certificate" dialog is a **checkbox multi-select** of the facet's templates (already-held ones annotated amber "will be re-attached", not disabled) issuing as **ONE bundle email**, one PDF per cert. New `issueCertificateBundle()` in [deliver.ts](src/lib/certificates/deliver.ts): issue-or-reuse per template via `findOrIssueCertificate` (an already-held template is re-attached with its existing serial — deliberately UNLIKE `issueSingleCertificate`'s strict 409 ALREADY_ISSUED, matching the bulk-email semantics), single-template saved cover vs bundle default, per-template `failures[]` partial-send (all-failed → `ALL_TEMPLATES_FAILED`), audits only newly minted certs, **tags ENFORCED** (same-day correction after the organizer caught an untagged person receiving certs: the `selectAutoIssueTargets` predicate gates each selected template — non-matching → `failures[]`, zero matching → 422 `NO_MATCHING_TAG`; the card mirrors it client-side via a new `recipientTags` prop — non-matching templates disabled with the reason, untagged person gets an amber "tag them first" notice; "no tag, no certificate" has NO operator override), `ISSUED_SEND_FAILED` when the email fails post-issue (recover via "Resend all"). [issue-single route](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/certificates/issue-single/route.ts) accepts `templateIds` (1–10; legacy `templateId` kept) and returns `{ certs[], failures[] }` + legacy first-cert fields; `issueSingleCertificate` stays as a service API (tests only, no route caller). +8 service tests ([certificates-deliver.test.ts](__tests__/lib/certificates-deliver.test.ts)). Cert-scope suites 79/79 green; the concurrent session's in-flight invoice-service edits owned the only full-suite reds at commit time. **Bundle cover email is now an editable template (same day, organizer request):** the hardcoded multi-cert cover text became a per-event **system EmailTemplate** — slug `certificate-bundle-delivery` ("Certificate Delivery (Multiple Certificates)", editable under Communications → Email Templates; seeded content byte-equal to the old default so nothing changes until edited; added to `DEFAULT_TEMPLATES` + `TEMPLATE_VARIABLES` + the `SYSTEM_TEMPLATE_SLUGS` mirror). Resolved by `loadBundleCoverEmailTemplate(eventId)` in [bundle.ts](src/lib/certificates/bundle.ts) (via `getEventTemplate`, hardcoded constants as lookup-failure safety net) and wired into ALL multi-cert senders: `issueCertificateBundle` (deliver.ts), `coverEmailFor`/`executeCertificateBulkSend` (bulk-issue.ts — loaded once per batch), `buildCertCoverEmailPreview`, and the Issue-tab multi-run dialog pre-fill (certificates page via `useEmailTemplates` + client-safe `CERT_BUNDLE_COVER_TEMPLATE_SLUG`). Single-cert emails keep the cert template's own saved cover; custom overrides still win. +3 tests across the three harnesses.
- **Dinner RSVP (July 8, 2026) — P1→P3 + logging hardening + email-template preview** — A new **Event → Setup → Dinner RSVP** feature: invite people to the event's dinners with a **personalized link** and track who's coming. **Model:** one event has many `RsvpDinner` rows (Day 1 Dinner, Day 2 Gala…); each invited person is one `RsvpInvite` (unique unguessable token, `@@unique([eventId, inviteeEmail])`) whose **single link covers all dinners**; per-dinner attendance + guest count live in `RsvpDinnerResponse` (`@@unique([inviteId, dinnerId])`); a single dietary note on the invite. `RsvpStatus` enum (PENDING/RESPONDED). Additive migration `20260708120000_add_dinner_rsvp` (new enum + 3 tables, blue-green safe). Shared lib [src/lib/rsvp/rsvp.ts](src/lib/rsvp/rsvp.ts): token gen, email normalize, Zod schemas, `computeDinnerHeadcounts` (per-night tiles). **Organizer API** (org-scoped, `denyReviewer` on writes, rate-limited, audited): dinners CRUD (`/api/events/[id]/dinners[/[dinnerId]]`), roster+headcounts+CSV + bulk-add (dedup on `(eventId,email)`) + delete (`/api/events/[id]/rsvp-invites[/[inviteId]]`), and **send** (`/api/events/[id]/rsvp-invites/send` `{target:"all"|"pending", subject?, message?}`). **Public API** `GET/POST /api/public/events/[slug]/rsvp/[token]` — token-gated (lookup by unique token, event-slug asserted), per-IP rate-limited, re-submittable upsert, deadline-gated. **UI:** public RSVP form ([e/[slug]/rsvp/[token]](src/app/e/%5Bslug%5D/rsvp/%5Btoken%5D/page.tsx) — checkbox per dinner + guests + dietary), organizer console ([events/[id]/dinner](src/app/%28dashboard%29/events/%5BeventId%5D/dinner/page.tsx) — manage dinners, add/**import** invitees from Registrations/Speakers via [ImportInviteesDialog](src/components/dinner/import-invitees-dialog.tsx), roster + per-dinner headcount tiles + CSV + copy-link + **Email invitations**/**Remind pending**), Setup-hub card. **The invitation is a first-class email template** — `dinner-rsvp-invitation` in `DEFAULT_TEMPLATES` (editable under Communications → Email Templates; vars firstName/eventName/rsvpLink/personalMessage/organizerName/organizerSignature); the send route renders it via `getEventTemplate` + `renderAndWrap`, and the send dialog has a **Preview** button (`/email-preview` slug → `EmailPreviewDialog`). **MCP tool** `list_dinner_rsvps` (read-only: dinners + headcounts + per-invitee responses; [tools/dinner.ts](src/lib/agent/tools/dinner.ts); pkg 0.4.13→0.4.14). **Owner decisions:** each day = its own dinner; guests per-dinner, dietary once; invitees via picker+manual; **auto-reminder cron deliberately NOT built** (manual "Remind pending" suffices). **Every failure path logs** (all 404/429/public-400 branches + frontend catches). Docs: [docs/DINNER_RSVP.md](docs/DINNER_RSVP.md) + user-guide §Dinner RSVP. Verified each push tsc/eslint/vitest 2055/build green. **Reviewed twice**: Round 1 (Survey+RSVP, [docs/CODE_REVIEW_SURVEY_RSVP.html](docs/CODE_REVIEW_SURVEY_RSVP.html) — B2/H2/H4/H5 shipped) + Round 2 (July 16, [docs/CODE_REVIEW_DINNER_RSVP_R2.html](docs/CODE_REVIEW_DINNER_RSVP_R2.html) — 12 MED fixed across 4 batches; remaining LOWs in ROADMAP).
- **Cancel-a-registration-with-refund + `payment-service` extraction (July 8, 2026, commits `dbaf3a2` → `722d65f`)** — Changing a registration's status to **CANCELLED** now handles the money, and the refund/credit-note/cancel logic lives in a new service. Shipped + reviewed in phases. **Phase 1 (`dbaf3a2`) — `src/services/payment-service.ts`**: behavior-preserving extraction of `refundRegistration()` + `issueCreditNoteForRegistration()` from the refund + credit-notes routes (errors-as-values, owns side effects incl. a new audit log, never imports `next/server`); both routes delegate. **Phase 2a (`d05a262`) — a CANCELLED reg owes nothing**: the detail GET/PUT `financials` force `balanceDue: 0` + `hasOutstandingBalance: false` when `status === CANCELLED` (price kept for history, non-destructive), and the **payment-reminder** bulk email never chases a CANCELLED reg (adds `status != CANCELLED` when no explicit status filter is set). **Phase 2b-i (`4806e8d`) — `cancelRegistration()` + `POST .../registrations/[id]/cancel`**: **refund-BEFORE-cancel** — for a PAID reg with `refund:true`, auto-issue a full credit note → refund the remaining balance → then cancel (claim status, release seat via `planSeatTransition`/`releaseSeat`, release promo usage). A refund failure **aborts the cancel** (reg stays active + recoverable — no money in limbo); UNPAID/COMPLIMENTARY/INCLUSIVE have nothing to refund → just cancelled; an already-fully-refunded PAID reg cancels without a second refund. Endpoint is `denyReviewer` (blocks ONSITE too) + `denyFinance`, event-access gated. **Phase 2b-ii (`6532d45`) — UI** ([registration-detail-sheet.tsx](src/app/%28dashboard%29/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/registration-detail-sheet.tsx)): changing a PAID reg to CANCELLED + Save pops a confirm dialog — **Cancel & refund X** (hits `/cancel { refund:true }`), **Just cancel, no refund** (runs the normal PUT — releases seat/promo + preserves other staged edits), or **Keep**. **Review fix (`722d65f`) — HIGH H1**: if the on-open detail fetch failed (`financials` absent → `refundRemaining` 0), a paid-cancel used to fall through to a **silent no-refund cancel**; now it's blocked with a "reload before cancelling a paid registration" toast — it never silently skips the refund decision. Adversarial review returned **no BLOCKER**; deferred M/L findings (Cancel&refund drops other staged edits; refund-ok-but-cancel-tx-fail returns a generic 500; auto-CN-vs-refund amount divergence on odd offline captures; L1–L3) tracked in [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md) "Cancel-with-refund + payment-service — deferred review findings". **Decisions locked with the owner:** paid-cancel = *explicit confirm then auto-refund* (not silent); unpaid "reset to 0" = *show balance 0, keep price* (not destructive). +26 tests; suite 1988 → 2005. Each phase verified tsc/lint/vitest/build + pushed separately.
- **Gated partial refunds + partial credit notes + refunded-so-far total (July 7, 2026, commits `b02c361` → `dd5df4c` → `4553dc1`)** — Refunds went from **full-only** to **full-OR-partial, end-to-end**, and the flow is now **credit-note-gated + organizer-driven**. **The model:** the organizer issues a **credit note first** (full or partial), which unlocks **Issue Refund**; the refund amount is entered **separately** at refund time; partial refunds **accumulate** and the registration **stays PAID** until fully refunded, then flips to REFUNDED. **Schema:** `Registration.refundedAmount Decimal @default(0)` (additive migration `20260707120000`) — the running refunded total, in `FINANCIAL_KEYS` (hidden from MEMBER). **`createCreditNote`** ([invoice-service.ts](src/lib/invoice-service.ts)) gained an optional `amount` (partial; defaults to the full outstanding), now allows **multiple credit notes per registration** capped at the paid total, scales subtotal/discount/tax proportionally (tax reconciled to the remainder so subtotal−discount+tax===total), and throws `CreditNoteAmountError` (`INVALID_AMOUNT`/`CREDIT_LIMIT_EXCEEDED`). **The cap is enforced INSIDE the tx under a `SELECT … FOR UPDATE` lock on the registration row** (review fix **H1**) so two concurrent issues can't both slip past it and over-credit. **New route** `POST .../registrations/[id]/credit-notes` ([credit-notes/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/%5BregistrationId%5D/credit-notes/route.ts)) — the "Issue Credit Note" action: full/partial `amount`, optional `send` (emails the CN), `denyReviewer`+`denyFinance`, org-scoped via `buildEventAccessWhere`, rate-limited, audited (`CREDIT_NOTE_ISSUED`). **Refund route** ([refund/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/%5BregistrationId%5D/refund/route.ts)) rewritten: **gates on a non-cancelled credit note existing** (409 `CREDIT_NOTE_REQUIRED` otherwise — it no longer *creates* the CN), accepts a partial `amount` (default = full remaining), **optimistic-locks on `refundedAmount`** (conditional `updateMany`), Stripe **partial** refund (`refunds.create({payment_intent, amount})` + cumulative idempotency key `refund-{paymentId}-{refundedAfter}`) or offline record, keeps PAID on partial / flips REFUNDED + flips the `Payment` row only on **full**. **`charge.refunded` webhook** reconciles Stripe's **cumulative** `amount_refunded` into `refundedAmount` (delta-only, retry-safe via a `refundedAmount < cumulative` claim), keeps PAID on partial, and mints a CN only for **out-of-band Dashboard** refunds; `paidTotal` is the **sum of ALL PAID payments** (aggregate) so a full refund of one charge on a Stripe+manual multi-payment reg can't mislabel the whole reg REFUNDED (review fix **H2**). **No automatic attendee email** on refund anymore — the organizer communicates it manually (consistent with the credit-note flow); the `sendRefundConfirmationEmail` helper was removed. **UI** ([registration-detail-sheet.tsx](src/app/%28dashboard%29/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/registration-detail-sheet.tsx)): the Billing tab shows **"Refunded X of Y · Z remaining"**, an **Issue Credit Note** dialog (amount/reason/"email to attendee"), and an **Issue Refund** dialog (partial amount, capped at remaining) that is **disabled until a credit note exists** ("Issue a credit note before refunding" hint) — the detail GET/PUT `financials` now expose `refundedAmount`, `paidTotal`, and `creditedAmount` (sum of non-cancelled CNs) so the button gates client-side; on a 409 the refund dialog toasts + opens the CN dialog. **Deferred review findings** (M1 payments-sum-vs-computed-total cap divergence, M2 server refund-amount gate — UI already gates on CN *existence*, M3 conditional Stripe-error rollback, L1 reset-on-repay, L2 silent webhook-CN-cap-rejection, L3 client/server cap mismatch) are tracked in [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md) "Partial refunds + credit notes — deferred review findings". **This SUPERSEDES the earlier "Manual/offline refund path + branded credit-note PDF" entry below** on three points: credit notes are now **multiple-per-reg** (not one idempotent one), the refund **requires** a CN first (doesn't auto-create it), and the **refund confirmation email is gone**. tsc/eslint/vitest 1964/build green.
- **Stripe receipt stored locally as a durable snapshot (July 7, 2026)** — Stripe's `charge.receipt_url` is a **persistent** (non-expiring, non-signed) hosted **HTML** page — but it lives on Stripe's servers, mutates over time (starts showing "Refunded" after a refund), and can break if the account is closed/migrated. So we now keep our own copy. **Schema** (additive migration `20260707140000_add_payment_stripe_receipt`, blue-green safe): `Payment.stripeReceiptUrl` (the live Stripe URL — dedicated field, no longer overloading `receiptUrl` which also carries the manual-payment proof artifact) + `Payment.stripeReceiptFile` (our local snapshot path). **Capture** ([src/lib/stripe-receipt.ts](src/lib/stripe-receipt.ts) `captureStripeReceipt`): SSRF-guarded (only fetches `*.stripe.com` over https), 10s timeout, downloads the receipt HTML and re-hosts it via [storage.ts](src/lib/storage.ts) `uploadStripeReceipt` → `/uploads/stripe-receipts/{YYYY}/{MM}/<uuid>.html` (local or Supabase per `STORAGE_PROVIDER`). **Fully failure-isolated** — NEVER throws (returns null on any problem); runs **fire-and-forget** off the `checkout.session.completed` webhook after the Payment row + documents are issued, so it can never affect payment processing. The webhook sets `stripeReceiptUrl` on `Payment.create`, then updates `stripeReceiptFile` once the snapshot lands. **UI**: the Billing panel "View receipt" link now prefers the durable local snapshot (`stripeReceiptFile`) → the live Stripe URL → the manual proof (`receiptUrl`). Note: this is **supplementary** — we already generate our **own branded receipt PDF** (`createPaidReceipt`) as the canonical durable artifact; the Stripe snapshot is extra proof. Only Stripe payments get it (manual/offline have `stripeReceipt*` null). **DR:** because the snapshot lands under `public/uploads/`, it's mirrored to the Singapore DR bucket by the existing hourly uploads sync (`aws s3 sync .../public/uploads/ s3://ea-sys-dr-singapore/uploads/`) with **no cron change** — ~60-min RPO, same as all uploads (holds while `STORAGE_PROVIDER=local`); the `stripeReceiptFile` DB pointer rides the twice-daily `pg_dump`. Bundled with a **doc-drift fix**: the April-29 manual-payment note wrongly claimed card-onsite/cash capture a "receipt number" — never implemented (schema has only `cardBrand`/`cardLast4` and `cashReceivedBy`); corrected in this file. tsc/eslint/vitest/build green.
- **Responsive mobile banner — art-directed `<picture>` (July 7, 2026, commit `c74daf0`)** — Public event banners were a single wide `<img>` scaled to fit, so on a phone a wide banner (e.g. 1400×300, ~4.7:1) shrank to ~60–160px tall and the baked-in heading became illegible. Added an **optional per-event mobile banner** served **below 576px** via a `<picture><source media="(max-width: 575.98px)">`; the main banner shows at **576px and above**. Only the matching image downloads (true art-direction, not CSS show/hide). **Schema:** `Event.bannerImageMobile` (additive migration `20260707000000_add_event_banner_image_mobile`, `ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS` — blue-green safe); Event PUT accepts/persists it, clone copies it, both public routes ([slug] + complete-registration) expose it. **New shared component** [EventBanner](src/components/public/event-banner.tsx) — renders the `<picture>`, falls back to the main banner at every breakpoint when no mobile banner is set (identical to prior behaviour), takes the img `className` so each page's layout is unchanged. **Settings → Branding** gained a "Mobile Banner (optional)" upload beside the desktop one (label the existing one "Banner Image (desktop)"), with **~700×400 / 576px** guidance in the hint (700×400 ≈ 1.75:1 keeps the heading ~200px tall on phones; 700×300 would be ~160px). **8 public pages** converted to `<EventBanner>` (register, category register, complete-registration, abstract register, login, forgot/reset-password, my-registration) — the auth pages' `next/image` banners became plain `<img>` inside `<picture>` (next/image can't do art-direction; they already ran `unoptimized`). **Not yet converted** (still one banner at all sizes; deferred): confirmation, survey, session, presenter-agreement, speaker-agreement. tsc/eslint/vitest 1870/build green.
- **Event time-of-day removed from public event-info cards (July 7, 2026, commit `984acc6`)** — The public event-info header (register, category register, complete-registration, login, my-registration, forgot/reset-password, abstract register — 8 pages) showed a `Clock` + time line derived from `event.startDate` (e.g. "12:00 AM") — an arbitrary/meaningless time from the date picker for a multi-day event. Removed the time line (and the now-unused `Clock` import) on all 8 pages; the **date** line is kept. Per-session schedule times on the agenda/session pages are unchanged (those are meaningful and shown in the event timezone). Pure UI removal.
- **Registration detail sheet — no more auto-save; Edit → Save only (July 7, 2026, commit `334d57a`)** — Every field on the registration detail sheet ([registration-detail-sheet.tsx](src/app/%28dashboard%29/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/registration-detail-sheet.tsx)) that used to **write immediately on change** (each inline Select/input fired its own `updateRegistration.mutate` PUT) now **stages into the edit form and commits together via the Save button**. **View mode is read-only** (the selects are `disabled`); the operator clicks **Edit → change → Save**. Converted: Registration Type, Badge Type, Attendance, Registration Status, Payment Status, Sponsor, "Charge to" billing account, Payer reference, Attendee-is-guarantor. **The Pricing Tier picker is the one exception** — it keeps its own explicit **Apply tier** button (staged `pendingTierId` + Cancel), sitting next to the promo Apply/Remove in the Payment Summary (the promo Apply/Remove were already explicit, not auto-save). **Mapping** ([registration-edit-mapping.ts](src/app/%28dashboard%29/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/registration-edit-mapping.ts)): `RegistrationEditData` gained `ticketTypeId, badgeType, attendanceMode, status, paymentStatus, sponsorId`; **`toServerPayload` now takes the loaded-row snapshot as a 3rd arg and sends each registration-level field ONLY when it changed** — an unrelated attendee edit no longer re-sends an unchanged `paymentStatus`/`sponsorId` (review **H1**). **INCLUSIVE guard** is now change-scoped on both ends: the client blocks only when *changing to* INCLUSIVE without a sponsor, and the **PUT** ([registrations/[registrationId]/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/%5BregistrationId%5D/route.ts)) runs the `INCLUSIVE_REQUIRES_SPONSOR` + `SPONSOR_NOT_FOUND` checks only when the request actually touches `paymentStatus`/`sponsorId` (`touchingSponsorFields`) — so a legacy INCLUSIVE-without-sponsor (or later-removed-sponsor) row **stays editable** for unrelated fields (review **H2**). New UI state `badgeCustomOpen` (custom-badge free-text) + `pendingTierId`/`tierApplying`; also the sheet now **fetches the full detail (with `financials`) on open** so the Payment Summary shows the price immediately for a tier-priced reg (the list payload doesn't compute `financials`). Independent review: **SAFE TO SHIP**, H1+H2 fixed; the one deferred item (M2) is cosmetic — a staged tier pick can survive an unrelated Edit→Save (Apply still uses a fresh optimistic-lock token, no double-submit). +8 mapping tests (diff mode + reg-level fields); tsc/eslint/vitest 1870/build green. **Operator behavior change:** changing a status/payment/type/badge/attendance now takes **Edit → change → Save** (or **Apply** for the tier) instead of a one-click dropdown.

- **Payment-reminder ("Pay Now") email amount fix — tier/virtual/discount/tax aware (July 7, 2026)** — The admin single-send **payment-reminder** email ([registrations/[registrationId]/email/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/%5BregistrationId%5D/email/route.ts) `type: "payment-reminder"`) built `{{amount}}` + the Pay-Now link from **`registration.ticketType.price` only**. For a **tier-priced** registration (ticket type base 0, real price on the pricing tier) or a **virtual** one (priced via `virtualPrice`), that rendered **"USD 0.00"** and a `price=0` link — the payment-collection email told the registrant they owed **nothing** — while the *confirmation* email for the same reg correctly showed the tier price + tax (it delegates to `sendRegistrationConfirmation`). Same "tier-priced base looks free" class the finance work fixed elsewhere; this path was missed. **Fix:** resolve the amount the canonical way — `readRegistrationBasePrice(registration)` (prefers stamped `originalPrice`, falls back tier→ticket) → `computeRegistrationFinancials` (nets promo discount, adds tax) → `{{amount}}` = the **true tax-inclusive amount due**, matching what Stripe charges; the Pay-Now link carries that total too. No new query (the route already loads `originalPrice`/`pricingTier`/`discountAmount`/`event.taxRate`/`taxLabel`). The `type: "confirmation"` branch was already correct (delegates to `sendRegistrationConfirmation`); the Stripe payment-confirmation + refund-confirmation emails were also verified correct in the same review. **+4 route tests** ([registration-payment-reminder-email.test.ts](__tests__/api/registration-payment-reminder-email.test.ts): tier / tier+tax / discount+tax / virtual — all would fail against the old `ticketType.price` path). tsc/eslint/vitest 1858/build green.
- **Manual/offline refund path + branded credit-note PDF (July 7, 2026)** — "Issue Refund" on the registration detail sheet used to **hard-require a Stripe payment** — it looked up the most-recent PAID `Payment`, and if it had no `stripePaymentId` (a cash / bank-transfer / card-onsite capture, or a PAID reg an admin hand-flipped with no `Payment` row at all) it 400'd with "No Stripe payment found". So the whole offline-payment population — the exact registrations the manual-payment-capture feature creates — could never be refunded from the UI. **Option A fix** ([refund/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/%5BregistrationId%5D/refund/route.ts)): the route now branches on `const isManualRefund = !payment?.stripePaymentId`. **Manual path** skips Stripe entirely — the organizer returns the money out-of-band (reverses the transfer / hands cash back) — and we just **record** the reversal: optimistic-lock the reg → REFUNDED (`updateMany where paymentStatus:"PAID"`, 409 on a lost race), flip the `Payment` row → REFUNDED **if one exists** (a hand-flipped reg may have none), and issue a credit note. **Stripe path** is unchanged (`stripe.refunds.create` with `idempotencyKey: refund-{paymentId}`, rollback-to-PAID + 502 on Stripe error). The refunded **amount** comes from the `Payment` row when present, else is **computed** from the registration (`computeRegistrationFinancials` over `readRegistrationBasePrice` + discount + event tax — tax-inclusive total, matching manual capture); the select now pulls `originalPrice`/`discountAmount`/tier+ticket price/`event.taxRate`+`taxLabel` for that. Credit note reason is tagged `Offline refund of {amt}` vs `Stripe refund of {amt}`. Response shape: `{ refundId: stripeRefundId|null, manual: boolean, status: "succeeded"|"recorded" }`. **UI** ([registration-detail-sheet.tsx](src/app/%28dashboard%29/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/registration-detail-sheet.tsx)): the confirm text now spells out that Stripe payments reverse automatically but **offline payments must be returned to the attendee manually** (both mark the reg Refunded + issue a credit note, irreversible); the success toast branches on `data.manual` ("Offline refund recorded — return the money manually" vs "Refund issued via Stripe"). Refund confirmation email + admin notification fire on both paths. **Credit-note PDF branding parity** ([credit-note-pdf.ts](src/lib/credit-note-pdf.ts) rewritten): the credit note now shares the invoice/quote layout via [document-layout](src/lib/pdf/document-layout.ts) — **logo + 3-column header + boxed bill-to/meta + line-items table + totals + page footers** — titled **"CREDIT NOTE"** with a **"TOTAL CREDIT"** line and a REASON block, instead of the old hand-rolled logo-less PDF. `CreditNotePDFData` gained `logoPath`; [invoice-service.ts](src/lib/invoice-service.ts) passes `logoPath: org.logo`. **Behavior note:** credit-note amounts now render **positive** (standard convention — the document type conveys the credit), was negative. **Idempotency:** `createCreditNote` now returns `{ invoice, created }` and issues **exactly one credit note per registration** — a route-initiated Stripe refund creates the CN *and* triggers a `charge.refunded` webhook (which Stripe retries) that would each mint a second CN + duplicate email; when a CN already exists it's returned with `created: false` and both callers ([refund route](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/%5BregistrationId%5D/refund/route.ts) + [webhook](src/app/api/webhooks/stripe/route.ts)) skip re-emailing. **+9 refund-route tests + 1 idempotency service test** ([refund-route.test.ts](__tests__/api/refund-route.test.ts): manual no-Stripe flip+credit-note, PAID-with-no-payment-row, Stripe path unchanged, Stripe-fail rollback→502, not-PAID 400, lost-lock 409, 401, MEMBER 403) + 2 stale [events/refund.test.ts](__tests__/api/events/refund.test.ts) cases updated (old 400-on-manual → 200 manual refund). All verified tsc/eslint/vitest/build green; credit-note PDF smoke-rendered OK.
- **Per-event ONSITE (registration-desk) staff + adversarial-review security fix (July 7, 2026)** — ONSITE was org-bound and saw **every** event in the org; now a temp desk worker is assigned to **specific events** and sees/acts on only those — mirroring the REVIEWER per-event model. Shipped, then adversarially reviewed, then hardened, across commits `893d3b3` (feature) → `93deed7` (security fix + UI). **No schema/migration** — assignment lives in `Event.settings.onsiteUserIds` (JSON). **The feature (`893d3b3`):** [buildEventAccessWhere](src/lib/event-access.ts) gained an ONSITE branch scoping to `settings.onsiteUserIds` (org-bound AND assigned; unassigned ⇒ zero events); `POST/GET/DELETE /api/events/[eventId]/onsite-staff` (assign/list/unassign — org-scoped, `denyReviewer`-guarded, atomic `updateEventSettings`, audited); `GET /api/organization/onsite-staff` (every ONSITE account + its assigned events); and a **Settings → Onsite Staff** tab ([onsite-staff-card.tsx](src/components/settings/onsite-staff-card.tsx), admin-only) to create a temp (reuses `POST /api/organization/users` role=ONSITE + password mode) + assign to event(s), manage per-row assignments (searchable popover), remove-from-event, and delete-account (strips stale ids first). One temp can span multiple events; **no backfill** (existing ONSITE users need reassignment — scoping + UI shipped together). **The BLOCKER + fix (`93deed7`):** an adversarial review found the per-event scoping only enforced *visibility* via `buildEventAccessWhere` — the 5 desk routes ONSITE actually uses (registrations list/create, detail PUT, check-in POST+PUT, badge print) authorized on **org membership alone**, so an ONSITE user assigned to Event A could read/write **any** Event B in the same org: full attendee + **payment** data (ONSITE is finance-capable), create/edit registrations, check people in, and print badge PDFs (which carry **entry barcodes** — a physical-access credential). Fix = route every ONSITE-reachable event lookup through `buildEventAccessWhere` (assignment-gated for ONSITE, org-scoped for admin/organizer/API-key — the list GET is API-key-aware via `getOrgContext`'s `userId/role`). The payments route + detail GET already used it. **+7 cross-event isolation tests** ([onsite-cross-event-isolation.test.ts](__tests__/api/onsite-cross-event-isolation.test.ts), real `buildEventAccessWhere`): unassigned ONSITE → 404 on list/create/check-in/badge; admin + API-key stay org-scoped. **Doc-drift corrected:** the old CLAUDE.md claim that ONSITE money is hidden (`canViewFinance` excludes it) was **wrong** — `FINANCE_ROLES` includes ONSITE since the June 17 "desk staff record payments" decision, which is why the cross-event gap also leaked payment data. Plan/history in [docs/ONSITE_PER_EVENT_PLAN.md](docs/ONSITE_PER_EVENT_PLAN.md). Remaining review items (H1 page-404 for unassigned events, M1 stale-id cleanup on direct-API account delete, M2 organizer-can-assign trust boundary + create+assign partial-failure surfacing) deferred to [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md). All verified tsc/eslint/vitest 1844/build green.

- **Identity & Roles operator runbook — "one person, many hats" (July 2, 2026)** — New [docs/IDENTITY_AND_ROLES.md](docs/IDENTITY_AND_ROLES.md) from a read-only audit of the overlap cases (speaker↔registrant, speaker↔reviewer, committee↔speaker↔reviewer). - **Promo codes on existing registrations + discount consistency + "Free registration" price-resolution fix (July 1, 2026)** — A cluster of registration-finance work, adversarially reviewed (fix-then-ship, 0 blockers), shipped across several commits; all verified tsc/eslint/vitest 1774/build green.
  - **Apply/remove a promo code against an EXISTING unpaid registration** — both organizer (registration detail sheet → Billing) and registrant self-service (`/my-registration` pay-later flow). The discount stores on `Registration.discountAmount` + `promoCodeId`, which the pay-later checkout, quote PDF, and invoice already read. New service [src/services/promo-code-service.ts](src/services/promo-code-service.ts) `applyPromoCodeToRegistration` / `removePromoCodeFromRegistration` — errors-as-values + **sentinel-rollback** (a failed step never commits a partial release), unpaid-only gate (UNASSIGNED/UNPAID/PENDING), **same validity rules for organizer + registrant** (no override — active / date-window / ticket-type applicability / maxUses / maxUsesPerEmail), **replace-not-stack** (releases the old code first), atomic `usedCount` guard, per-email limit excludes the reg's own prior redemption, audit + structured logs. Organizer route `POST/DELETE /api/events/[eventId]/registrations/[registrationId]/promo` (`denyReviewer`+`denyFinance`, org-scoped, rate-limited); registrant route `POST/DELETE /api/registrant/registrations/[registrationId]/promo` (ownership-checked). UI: registrant "Have a promo code?" input in the Payment Required block (discount line + net-tax, refetch on apply/remove); organizer apply/remove under the Payment Summary. +15 service tests.
  - **Discount now reflects in the quote PDF + confirmation email.** The Stripe charge was already discounted, but the quote PDF hardcoded discount to 0 and the confirmation email's payment block showed the pre-discount price. [quote-pdf.ts](src/lib/quote-pdf.ts) `QuotePDFData` + `RegistrationForQuotePDF` gained `discountAmount`/`discountLabel` (passed to `drawTotals`, which already taxes the net); [email.ts](src/lib/email.ts) `sendRegistrationConfirmation` got `discountAmount`/`promoCode` params → the payment block itemises Subtotal / Promo discount / tax-on-net / Total and threads the discount into the attached quote. All send callers pass base-price + discount (public register, registrant resend, admin resend) — no double-subtraction. Organizer `/quote` + public `/document` routes include the promo + pass the discount.
  - **Billing summary shows Promo code applied · Discount · Total · Outstanding** (both the Details-tab block + Billing-tab Payment Summary); balance row relabelled "Outstanding".
  - **Admin resend of "Registration Confirmation" now sends the quote PDF + a valid payment block** — the admin single-send route ([registrations/[registrationId]/email/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/%5BregistrationId%5D/email/route.ts)) delegated the built-in confirmation to `sendRegistrationConfirmation` (was rendering the template generically → unresolved `{{paymentBlock}}` + no quote).
  - **HIGH #1 — "Free registration" false-positive fixed** ([registration-financials.ts](src/lib/registration-financials.ts) `resolveRegistrationBasePrice` + `readRegistrationBasePrice`). A tier-priced ticket type (base price 0, real price on the tier) with **no `pricingTierId`** — or a VIRTUAL registration (priced via `virtualPrice`, tier nulled) — resolved subtotal to 0 via `pricingTier?.price ?? ticketType?.price ?? 0`, so the detail sheet showed "Free registration — no payment required" on a reg that owes money (and the promo service wrongly rejected it as FREE_REGISTRATION). Now **`Registration.originalPrice` is stamped at create** (tier + virtual aware; the service's `effectiveTicketPrice` also fixed to use the pricing-tier price, not just `ticketType.price`) at the main create paths (public register, registration-service, speaker-companion, MCP `create_registrations_bulk`) and **read first** at every money surface (detail GET, checkout, payment-status, stripe webhook, invoice-service, quote-pdf, my-registration, promo-service) with a tier/ticket fallback for un-stamped rows. **No backfill** (forward-looking — a pre-fix row shows correctly once re-created); the charge path is safe (existing null-`originalPrice` rows fall back to today's behavior). **Deferred:** stamping the 3 CSV/EventsAir/import-contacts create paths (backfill-less + read-fallback cover them; the one edge left is a *new* virtual-via-CSV reg).
  - **HIGH #2 — per-email TOCTOU race closed.** `maxUsesPerEmail` was a non-atomic `count()`-then-`create()`, so two applies of the same code on two registrations sharing an email (the pay-later-then-re-register flow) could both bypass the cap. Fixed by serializing concurrent applies of a promo with a **transaction-scoped row lock** (`SELECT id FROM "PromoCode" WHERE id = ? FOR UPDATE`) in both the promo-code service and the public register route — scoped to the one promo row (different codes/events keep independent per-email limits), chosen over `@@unique([promoCodeId, email])` (which would break `maxUsesPerEmail > 1` + risk failing the migration on existing duplicates). No schema change.
  - **Deferred review findings (tracked in [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md)):** MEDIUM 100%-off code hides the registrant's own Remove button; the fragile `replaced` flag; LOW `discountValue` sign/cap not validated; register-route increments `usedCount` before the per-email check; MEMBER can see the applied promo *code* (amount redacted — product call); the 3 unstamped import create-paths.

- **`PricingTier.soldCount` double-leak fixed — tier-aware seat accounting (June 29, 2026)** — A registration is counted on exactly ONE capacity counter: the **`PricingTier.soldCount`** (only the public-register path increments it — `createdSource === PUBLIC_REGISTER && pricingTierId != null`) or the **`TicketType.soldCount`** (admin/service create always uses the type even with a tier set; virtual nulls the tier). The decrement/transition paths previously **unconditionally moved `TicketType.soldCount`**, so a public+tier registration cancelled leaked **both** ways — the tier counter leaked up (phantom sell-out) and the ticket-type counter leaked down (could go negative → oversell). Fix makes the seat model tier-aware: [registration-seat.ts](src/lib/registration-seat.ts) `seatCounter(row)` picks the counter + `planSeatTransition` returns a `SeatCounter` (`{kind:"tier"|"ticketType", id}`); new guarded appliers [registration-seat-db.ts](src/lib/registration-seat-db.ts) `releaseSeat`/`releaseSeats` (`soldCount >= n` → never below 0) + `claimSeat` (atomic `soldCount < quantity`). Applied at all **5** decrement/transition sites — REST PUT (cancel/reactivate/type-change), REST DELETE, [bulk-type](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/bulk-type/route.ts), MCP `update_registration` + `bulk_update_registration_status` ([tools/registrations.ts](src/lib/agent/tools/registrations.ts)); refund is a no-op (leaves status). **Type-change** nulls the stale `pricingTierId` on both the transition `next` state AND the persisted row (else a later cancel releases the wrong counter). DELETE + both bulk paths also picked up the latent **virtual-reg** counter bug (they gated only on status, ignoring `attendanceMode`). The model also excludes **speaker companions** (`createdSource === SPEAKER_COMPANION`) — faculty are uncapped + created with no soldCount increment, so they consume no counter (a prod dry-run caught the reconciliation otherwise inflating every event's Faculty counter; one-line `seatCounter` guard + test). One-time **reconciliation script** [scripts/reconcile-soldcounts.ts](scripts/reconcile-soldcounts.ts) recomputes both counters from row-truth reusing the *same* `holdsSeat`/`seatCounter` helpers (can't drift; dry-run default, `--write`, `--event`, `--exclude <ids>`). +14 seat-model + integration tests (tier-routing per path). Adversarial review = **SAFE TO SHIP, 0 new bugs**. **Data repair deferred:** `soldCount` is **dormant today** (almost all events are unlimited-seat — nothing enforces these counters), so the leak's live impact is ~nil; the code fix is future-proofing for **capacity limits / multi-tenancy**. The prod `--write` is **held** until then (re-run the dry-run when it matters). **MED-1 (pre-existing):** legacy public+tier rows pre-2026-06-05 have `createdSource = NULL` → route to ticketType; a `--write` shifts their counts tier→ticketType (June-29 prod dry-run: ~7 rows on OSH Monthly Meeting + 1st Heart Failure Forum — `--exclude` them pending the keep-on-tier-via-backfill decision). tsc/eslint/vitest 1747/build green.

- **Communications/bulk-email audience filters + Activity edit-history diffs + public SEO + Add-form parity + faculty data fix (June 29, 2026)** — A batch of operator-facing improvements (all verified tsc/lint/build/vitest green; bulk-email work adversarially reviewed, 0 blocker/0 high):
  - **Bulk-email audience filters (registrations).** The "Send Bulk Email" dialog — used from BOTH the registrations-list "Email All" AND the Communications page — now exposes **in-dialog, multi-select** audience filters in a collapsible **"Filter recipients"** section (collapsed by default so the dialog opens compact; auto-opens when a filter is pre-applied from a tile/the list filter bar): **Payment status** + **Registration type** (multi checkbox; new `ticketTypeIds` filter, Prisma `in`, supersedes the legacy single `ticketTypeId`) + **Badge type** (multi checkbox; `badgeTypes`, `in`) + **Tags any-of** (`tagsInclude`, `hasSome`). Semantics are **OR within a field, AND across fields**; an empty field = no restriction (the empty-array guard omits the `where` key — never `in: []`). Wider dialog (`sm:max-w-4xl`) with the three multi-selects laid out **3-up**; recap joins multi-values with **"or"** (a registration has one type, so AND would always be 0); per-filter footnotes. Backend in [src/lib/bulk-email.ts](src/lib/bulk-email.ts) (`BulkEmailFilters` + Zod + registrations `where`); UI in [src/components/bulk-email-dialog.tsx](src/components/bulk-email-dialog.tsx) (fetches `useTickets`/`useEventTags`, takes a `badgeOptions` prop from the host); both host pages pass `badgeOptions` and updated their live recipient-count predicates to the multi shape (**count == send** preserved). **Also fixed a real bug:** the registrations-list "Filter by tag" control was never passed to "Email All", so a tag filter was silently ignored on send. No schema change.
  - **"Exclude faculty / speakers" toggle + single filter surface (follow-on).** Added an `excludeFaculty` filter — a one-click checkbox in the dialog's Filter recipients section; the registrations `where` spreads `EXCLUDE_FACULTY_WHERE` (`NOT { ticketType: { isFaculty: true } }`) so organizers email **delegates only**, keyed on the `isFaculty` ticket type (robust to new delegate types / null badges). And **the duplication was unified**: the Communications page's own (single-select) registration Advanced-filters block was **removed** — the **dialog is now the single registration-filter surface**, shared by the Communications page + the registrations-list "Email All"; the Speakers card keeps its Advanced filters (the dialog has no speaker-filter controls). Plus a one-accent **cerulean** color pass on the Communications page (header + audience-card icons, workflow-tile icons, per-tile recipient counts; bold-cerulean "Filter recipients" label + count number) and an Email-Type trigger height fix (the base `data-[size=default]:h-9` data-variant needs a same-variant override — a plain `h-12` loses to it under tailwind-merge → `data-[size=default]:h-auto min-h-12`).
  - **Activity edit-history now shows field-level diffs.** The registration + speaker Activity timeline ([src/lib/activity-feed.ts](src/lib/activity-feed.ts) → [src/components/activity/activity-timeline-card.tsx](src/components/activity/activity-timeline-card.tsx)) already read `AuditLog` but omitted the `changes` blob, so edits rendered as a bare "Updated". It now derives **before→after field diffs** from the stored snapshots — including one level into the nested `attendee` (so phone / registrationType / additionalEmail edits surface) — with humanized labels, noise keys skipped (`updatedAt`/ids/etc.), capped at 15, newest-first (last 3 on top). **Financial fields are redacted for non-finance viewers** via `redactFinancialFields`; both activity routes thread `canViewFinance(session.user.role)`. **Activity-code dedup (follow-on):** (1) the shared `ActivityItem`/`ActivityFieldDiff`/`ActivitySource` types were extracted to a **client-safe** [src/lib/activity-feed-types.ts](src/lib/activity-feed-types.ts) (no `db` import) — both the server builder and the client card import them (were maintained as two hand-synced copies); (2) the two **global** audit feeds ([src/components/activity-feed.tsx](src/components/activity-feed.tsx) — event dashboard — and [src/app/(dashboard)/activity/global-activity-feed.tsx](src/app/%28dashboard%29/activity/global-activity-feed.tsx) — org-wide) now share [src/components/activity/audit-log-display.ts](src/components/activity/audit-log-display.ts) (`auditEntityIcon`/`auditActionColor`/`describeAuditAction`/`auditActorLabel` + `AuditLogLike`) instead of byte-identical copies of the icon/colour maps + describe/actor functions (~60 LOC of dup removed). **The two global feeds stay separate components** (different data/layout/filters) — only the display logic is shared; and the global audit feed is deliberately NOT merged with the per-person `ActivityTimelineCard` (different subsystems).
  - **Faculty registration-type data correction (backfill — RUN ON PROD).** "Faculty" is a badge, not a profession, but 33 legacy companion attendees had `Attendee.registrationType = "Faculty"` (written before the June-26 companion fix). [scripts/backfill-faculty-registration-type.ts](scripts/backfill-faculty-registration-type.ts) now **defaults unknown-profession faculty to "Physician"** (changed from the prior "blank to null") — **3 restored** to the linked speaker's real profession, **30 → "Physician"**, **0 left as "Faculty"** — and writes an `AuditLog` per change so each shows as a diff in the new Activity timeline. Review the defaulted set via the registrations filter **Badge=Faculty + Type=Physician** and fix the rare non-physician. **Faculty designation (`badgeType="Faculty"` + the `isFaculty` ticket type) is untouched**, and the **live companion-creation path is deliberately UNCHANGED** — no "assume Physician" baked into create; new faculty with no profession stay blank ([src/lib/speaker-companion.ts](src/lib/speaker-companion.ts) untouched).
  - **Speaker phone/additionalEmail enrichment (backfill — RUN ON PROD).** [scripts/backfill-speaker-contact-from-registration.ts](scripts/backfill-speaker-contact-from-registration.ts) — **enrich-only**: fills a speaker's blank `phone`/`additionalEmail` from its counterpart registration's attendee (`sourceRegistrationId`, else same-email), **never overwriting** an existing value, audited. 1 row enriched (45 correctly left untouched — no richer counterpart). Speaker and Attendee are separate rows with no live sync; this is a one-time copy.
  - **Add Registration ↔ Add Speaker field parity.** Both Add forms now render the **identical** personal section via the shared [src/components/forms/person-form-fields.tsx](src/components/forms/person-form-fields.tsx) — Title, First/Last, Email, **Additional Email**, Org, Job Title, **Phone**, **Bio**, Photo, City, **State**, **Zip**, Country, Specialty, **Custom Specialty (when "Others")**, Tags. The speaker Add form was hand-rolled and **silently dropped Phone**; it's now converted onto the shared component (keeping its speaker-only Role/Status/Website/Social-links sections). Frontend-only — both create backends + models already accepted every field.
  - **Public-page SEO metadata.** Public `/e/[slug]/*` pages are client components that inherited the generic root `<title>`. New **server `layout.tsx`** files now emit **per-event** OpenGraph/Twitter tags (event name, HTML-stripped description, banner as the share image) and **per-section titles** ("Register — Event", "Agenda — Event", the session's own name, …) via a shared `buildEventMetadata()` ([src/lib/public-event-metadata.ts](src/lib/public-event-metadata.ts), event lookup wrapped in React `cache`) + `metadataBase` on the root layout so the banner's relative URL resolves absolute for crawlers. **Known follow-up (tracked):** the slug lookups are org-unscoped — fine single-org; must add `organizationId` when multi-tenant lands (`docs/MULTI_TENANCY_IMPACT.md`).
  - **scheduled-email 0-recipient = benign skip.** A scheduled bulk send that resolves to **zero** recipients at fire time is now a terminal `SENT` (0 counts) logged at info — not a `FAILED` + error-level admin page. `BulkEmailError` gained `NO_RECIPIENTS_CODE` that [src/lib/scheduled-emails-worker.ts](src/lib/scheduled-emails-worker.ts) branches on; the immediate "Send now" route still returns a 400 so an operator gets feedback. Stops the auto-enqueued webinar sequence on empty/test events from paging hourly.
  - **Smaller:** removed the "Back to Event Page" button on the post-registration confirmation page ([confirmation/page.tsx](src/app/e/%5Bslug%5D/confirmation/page.tsx)); deleted the **orphaned `docker/Dockerfile`** (dead/unreferenced; `Dockerfile.dev` + root `Dockerfile`/`Dockerfile.worker` are the live ones); narrowed the dashboard sidebar `w-64 → w-56`; added `.vscode/launch.json` debug configs.

- **Billing payers — event-level inline entry with org-level consolidation (June 29, 2026)** — Previously a payer ("Charge to another account") could only be created at the **org** level (Settings → Billing), then attached to an event, then picked on the registration — a 3-step context switch. Now an organizer can add a payer **inline from the registration Charge-to picker** (the full-page Add Registration form), mirroring how Contacts work: capture in context, consolidate into one org record. New `findOrCreateBillingAccount()` ([billing-account-service.ts](src/services/billing-account-service.ts)) — **exact (case-insensitive, trimmed) name → reuse** the existing org payer (never a duplicate); a **near-duplicate name** (fuzzy: one alphanumeric key contains the other, e.g. "Cleveland Clinic" vs "Cleveland Clinic Foundation") → create + flag `needsReview` for an admin to merge later (advisory, never blocks). New event-scoped `POST /api/events/[eventId]/billing-accounts` ([route](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/billing-accounts/route.ts), `denyReviewer`+`denyFinance`) does the find-or-create at the org level **and auto-attaches** the `EventBillingAccount` junction. New reusable [AddPayerDialog](src/components/billing/add-payer-dialog.tsx) (name + type + contact/email/phone/address/city/country/tax) + `useCreateAndAttachBillingAccount` hook; wired into the full-page form ("+ Add a new payer"). The payer stays a **single shared org row** (only the per-event attachment is event-specific) — exact-name reuse does NOT clobber the existing record's details (edit those in Settings → Billing). +4 service tests (reuse / create / fuzzy-flag / NAME_REQUIRED). **Follow-ups (reusable component makes them trivial):** the registration detail-sheet reassign picker + the quick-add dialog + an admin merge UI for `needsReview` payers. tsc/eslint/vitest 1737/build green.

- **Event clone now copies custom email templates (June 29, 2026)** — Event clone already copied email **branding** (header/footer image, footer HTML, from address/name, CC) + all the HTML content fields (registration/abstract/speaker-agreement) + **survey** (`surveyConfig` + `surveyIntroHtml`, deliberately NOT the `surveyShareLink` token or responses). The one missing "communications" piece was the per-event **`EmailTemplate`** rows (the custom/edited templates under Communications → Email Templates) — they were silently dropped on clone. [clone/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/clone/route.ts) now `include`s `emailTemplates` and `createMany`s them onto the new event inside the same transaction (slug/name/subject/htmlContent/textContent/isActive copied; no ID remap needed; the new event has no templates so the `@@unique([eventId, slug])` can't collide). **Scheduled emails are intentionally NOT cloned** (time-specific sends tied to the source event). +1 clone test (templates copied with fields + isActive preserved). tsc/eslint/vitest/build green.

- **Event.settings / Organization.settings lost-update fixed — atomic merge helper (June 29, 2026, data-loss audit #4)** — The settings JSON blob holds many features' config (reviewerUserIds, sponsors, webinar, zoom, cme, registrationOpen, …) and **every** writer did read-whole-blob → spread → `db.event.update({ data: { settings } })` **outside any transaction** — a lost-update race: two requests touching DIFFERENT keys both read the old blob, second write silently drops the first (e.g. saving sponsors wiped a concurrently-added reviewer). New [src/lib/event-settings.ts](src/lib/event-settings.ts) `updateEventSettings(eventId, patch)` + `updateOrganizationSettings(orgId, patch)`: an atomic `SELECT … FOR UPDATE` row-lock + merge + write inside `db.$transaction` (the lock holds across Prisma's interactive tx, including through the pgbouncer transaction pooler — single backend per tx). Object patch = shallow-merge (preserve unspecified keys); function patch `(cur)=>next` = full replace (for array append/remove / key delete, computed from the **locked** current). Migrated **all ~13 writers**: event PUT, org PUT, sponsors, webinar, zoom/settings, certificates/settings (cme), reviewers add (function-form append, deduped) + remove (filter), MCP `update_cme_settings`/`upsert_sponsors`, webinar-provisioner, org zoom creds (PUT + function-form DELETE), org eventsair creds. The general event PUT still strips `reviewerUserIds` from the incoming settings (helper preserves the existing list). +6 helper tests + crud settings test updated. **Adversarial review: 0 blockers/highs**; fixed MED (reviewer add same-key double-add → Set dedupe inside the lock). **Deferred (ROADMAP, low/admin-only):** cross-field atomicity in the split PUTs (settings + scalar columns are now 2 sequential writes — partial write on crash) + `settings.webinar` sub-key last-write-wins. tsc/eslint/vitest 1732/build green. **Part of a 4-fix data-loss batch** (#1 EventsAir import enrich-only `5024e42`, #2 MCP accommodation atomic re-book `b37db44`, #3 bulk-type + import-contacts oversell guards `37b0ab7`, #4 this).

- **Contact sync is now enrich-only — a sparse registration can't wipe Contact data (June 29, 2026)** — `syncToContact()` upserts the org-wide Contact (`@@unique([organizationId, email])`) from every event interaction. Its `cleanFields()` previously stripped only `undefined`, so a value of `null`/`""` **overwrote** (cleared) the Contact field — and the public new-event register passes `field || null` for blank optionals, meaning **a sparse later registration silently wiped richer data an earlier event had populated** on the same Contact (the sync is one-way event→Contact + latest-write-wins, and null counted as a write). Fix: `cleanFields()` now also skips `null` and `""` ([contact-sync.ts](src/lib/contact-sync.ts)) → the sync can **fill in or update** a field with real data but **never clears** an already-populated Contact field; the Contact accumulates the best-known value per field across events. Required name fields + `eventIds` always sync. **Behavior change (accepted):** intentionally *clearing* a field on a registration no longer propagates the clear to the Contact — to clear a Contact field you edit the Contact directly (that path doesn't go through this sync). The old comment claimed it stripped "undefined/null" but the code only stripped undefined — now they match. +5 tests ([contact-sync.test.ts](__tests__/lib/contact-sync.test.ts): null/undefined/"" skipped on update+create+upsert, real values still written, eventIds appended). tsc/eslint/vitest 1720/build green.

- **Faculty no longer shows as a "registration type" (June 26, 2026)** — Bug report: a faculty member's registration showed **"Faculty"** as the registration type, but registration type should always be a professional category (Physician / Allied Health / Nurse / Others). Root cause: a speaker's companion registration sits on the hidden **isFaculty** ticket type (needed to exclude faculty from paid capacity/revenue), the list/detail/CSV display the **ticket-type name**, and the companion's attendee row also **hardcoded** `registrationType = "Faculty"` ([speaker-companion.ts](src/lib/speaker-companion.ts)). "Faculty" is a **badge/role** (`badgeType`), not a profession. **Fix (3 parts):** (1) **Data** — `ensureSpeakerCompanionRegistration` now sets the companion attendee's `registrationType` to the **speaker's** professional category (`Speaker.registrationType`, which the Add-Speaker form already captures), blank if unrecorded — never "Faculty". Threaded `registrationType` through `CompanionSpeakerInput` + all callers (speaker-service, submitter route, batch helper). (2) **Display** — new pure `displayRegistrationType()` helper in [faculty-filter.ts](src/lib/faculty-filter.ts): for a faculty row (`ticketType.isFaculty`) it shows the profession (or "—"), **never** the literal "Faculty"; for delegates it's the ticket-type name (which IS their category). Wired into the registrations list badge, CSV export, and the detail sheet (reviewer read-only display + the editable Registration-Type cell, which for faculty becomes a read-only profession line since a faculty companion's ticket type isn't a reassignable delegate category). The list API + front-end `TicketType` type gained `isFaculty`; the list API attendee select gained `registrationType`. The Faculty status stays visible via the **Faculty badge**. (3) **Backfill** — [scripts/backfill-faculty-registration-type.ts](scripts/backfill-faculty-registration-type.ts) (dry-run default, `--write`, `--event`, idempotent) flips existing companion rows off `registrationType = "Faculty"` to the linked speaker's profession (or blank). **Operator-run AFTER deploy.** Note: someone who registered as a delegate (e.g. Physician) and was *then* made faculty already showed Physician correctly (the companion logic links their existing registration); only faculty-added-without-a-delegate-registration showed "Faculty". +8 tests (helper truth table + companion uses-profession-not-Faculty). tsc/eslint/vitest 1715/build green.

- **Reviewer-invite resend + silent-failure surfacing (June 26, 2026)** — Reviewer-audit finding: when the add-reviewer invite email fails, `findOrCreateReviewerUser` logs a warn and returns `invitationSent: false`, so the organizer can't tell a failed send from "sent, not yet accepted" — and there was no way to resend, leaving a reviewer permanently stranded with no account/link. New `POST /api/events/[eventId]/reviewers/[reviewerId]/resend-invitation` ([route](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/reviewers/%5BreviewerId%5D/resend-invitation/route.ts)): a **pending** account (`emailVerified` null) → re-mints a fresh setup token (deleteMany + create in a tx) + resends the `reviewer-invitation` setup email; an **active** account → resends the `reviewer-pool-invitation` reminder via `notifyReviewerPoolAdded`. Crucially, unlike the silent add path, a send failure **surfaces** as a 502 (`EMAIL_SEND_FAILED`) so the organizer knows it didn't go. 20/hr/user rate limit, org-scoped, `denyReviewer`-guarded, audited. UI: a "Resend" button on each **pending** reviewer row (Settings → Reviewers) next to Remove, via `useResendReviewerInvitation`; toast distinguishes setup-resend vs reminder. +4 route tests (pending→setup+token-mint, active→pool, send-fail→502, not-in-pool→404). tsc/eslint/vitest 1705/build green.

- **Conflict-of-interest enforcement on abstract review (June 26, 2026)** — Reviewer-audit finding: `AbstractReviewer.conflictFlag` was advisory only (stored + badged in the UI, never enforced) — a reviewer flagged conflicted on an abstract could still open and score it, and that review counted toward the decision. Now a conflicted reviewer is **blocked from submitting** (`403 CONFLICT_OF_INTEREST`) across all three submit paths: the REST submissions POST ([submissions/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/abstracts/%5BabstractId%5D/submissions/route.ts)), MCP `submit_abstract_review`, and MCP `admin_submit_review_on_behalf` (which checks the **target** reviewer's flag, not the caller's) — each adds `conflictFlag` to its existing assignment lookup + a guard right after the reviewer-auth check, logged `abstract-submission:coi-blocked`. Pool reviewers with no explicit `AbstractReviewer` row carry no flag (unaffected). They can still *read* the abstract (GET) — hard-gating read is a possible follow-up. +3 route tests (conflicted→403+no-upsert, non-conflicted→submits, pool-reviewer→submits). No MCP version bump (tool params/schema unchanged). tsc/eslint/vitest 1701/build green.

- **Draft-abstract save no longer emails "submitted" (June 26, 2026)** — Reviewer/submitter audit finding. The abstract create POST ([abstracts/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/abstracts/route.ts)) fired the `abstract-submission-confirmation` email **and** the "New Abstract Submitted" admin notification for both `SUBMITTED` and `DRAFT` — so saving a work-in-progress draft told the author they were done and pinged organizers about a non-submission. Both are now gated on `status === "SUBMITTED"`; a draft save is silent (it isn't submitted and is invisible to reviewers). `refreshEventStats` stays unconditional. Two-line behavioral gate (no test added — a predicate test would just re-implement the condition; the full suite confirms nothing relied on the old behavior). tsc/eslint/vitest 1698/build green.

- **Reviewer pool-add notification (June 26, 2026)** — Continuation of the reviewer "operational closure" cluster. Adding a reviewer to an event's pool (Settings → Reviewers, `POST .../events/[id]/reviewers`) told a **pre-existing** account nothing — only brand-new accounts got the account-setup invite (`reviewer-invitation`); an already-existing REVIEWER (or a speaker already linked to a User) was added silently. Now a pre-existing account gets a `reviewer-pool-invitation` email ("you've been added as a reviewer for {event}", link to `/my-reviews`) via a new `notifyReviewerPoolAdded` helper ([src/lib/abstract-reviewer-notify.ts](src/lib/abstract-reviewer-notify.ts)). The "pre-existing vs new" distinction is a real `existed` flag threaded out of `findOrCreateReviewerUser` (+ the speaker-with-userId path) — NOT the ambiguous `invitationSent` (which is also false when a new account's setup email *fails*, and that account can't log in yet so a "go review" email would be useless). New accounts still get only the setup invite (no double-email). New `reviewer-pool-invitation` system template (DEFAULT_TEMPLATES + TEMPLATE_VARIABLES + SYSTEM_TEMPLATE_SLUGS — drift test green); failure-isolated; logged to `EmailLog` as `entityType: USER`. +3 tests. **Still open in the cluster:** the per-abstract reviewers card omitting pool members, the reminder mechanism, COI enforcement, reviewer-invite resend/silent-failure. tsc/eslint/vitest 1698/build green.

- **Per-abstract reviewer-assignment notification (June 26, 2026)** — Follow-up to the reviewer/submitter audit. Assigning a reviewer to a *specific* abstract previously wrote the `AbstractReviewer` row and told the reviewer **nothing** — via REST (`POST .../abstracts/[id]/reviewers`) or the MCP `assign_reviewer_to_abstract` agent tool. Now both call a shared `notifyReviewerAssigned` helper ([src/lib/abstract-reviewer-notify.ts](src/lib/abstract-reviewer-notify.ts)) on a **new** assignment (NOT on idempotent re-assigns or role/COI flips), emailing the reviewer the abstract title + their role (Primary/Secondary/Consulting label) + a link to `/my-reviews`. New `reviewer-assignment` system email template (added to `DEFAULT_TEMPLATES` + `TEMPLATE_VARIABLES` + `SYSTEM_TEMPLATE_SLUGS` — drift test green). Fully failure-isolated (the helper never throws — a send failure logs but never breaks the assignment). Logged to `EmailLog` as `entityType: USER`. +5 tests (role-label mapping, name fallback, failure-isolation, no-template skip). No MCP version bump — the tool's name/params/schema are unchanged, only the executor's side-effect. Remaining reviewer "operational closure" items (pool-add notify, reminder mechanism, COI enforcement, invite-resend) still open in [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md). tsc/eslint/vitest 1695/build green.

- **Reviewer/submitter lifecycle audit + 2 production-breaking fixes (June 26, 2026)** — A 3-agent end-to-end trace of the reviewer + submitter (+ the submitter→speaker→attendee crossover) flows. The core model is sound (per-reviewer scored submissions preserved on unassign, ACCEPTED/REJECTED both email + portal-surface, survey correctly optional-per-event, cross-org reviewer scoping leak-free), but surfaced two **live-impacting** gaps, both now fixed. **Fix #1 — self-registered submitter-speakers got NO companion registration → no badge / entry barcode / check-in / survey / attendance cert.** The public submitter route ([submitter/route.ts](src/app/api/public/events/%5Bslug%5D/submitter/route.ts)) created the Speaker with a raw `tx.speaker.create` and never called `ensureSpeakerCompanionRegistration` — unlike every other speaker-add path (createSpeaker service, CSV import, import-contacts, bulk). Since check-in/survey/cert all hang off the companion `Registration`, a faculty member who entered as an abstract submitter literally couldn't be scanned in. Now mints the companion after the account create (failure-isolated, mirrors createSpeaker; the existing backfill script recovers already-affected rows). **Fix #2 — resubmit-after-revision was silent.** The abstract PUT path's `isSubmission` gate was `status==="SUBMITTED" && existing==="DRAFT"`, so a `REVISION_REQUESTED → SUBMITTED` resubmit didn't re-stamp `submittedAt`, sent no confirmation to the author, and never told reviewers/organizers the revised abstract was back ([abstracts/[abstractId]/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/abstracts/%5BabstractId%5D/route.ts)). Broadened to "INTO SUBMITTED from any non-SUBMITTED state" + added the confirmation email + `notifyEventAdmins` (labelled "Abstract Resubmitted" for the revision case), mirroring the create POST. +7 tests (2 route-level for the companion call incl. failure-isolation, 5 for the resubmission predicate). The **remaining audit findings** (reviewer per-abstract notify + reminder mechanism, COI not enforced, reviewer-invite silent-failure + no resend, accepted→present handoff is manual, draft-save emails "submitted", feedbackOnly dead code, mean-score visible to submitters) are catalogued in [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md) "Reviewer/submitter lifecycle audit" for scheduling. tsc/eslint/vitest 1690/build green.

- **Hybrid attendance mode-change — seat-accounting unification + lazy barcode (June 26, 2026, pkg 0.4.12)** — Closed "the one real hybrid gap": switching a registration **virtual→in-person** left `qrCode` null (un-scannable) and — discovered mid-build — the update paths **mis-handled `soldCount`** for virtual regs entirely (a virtual reg never consumed a venue seat, but cancel/reactivate/type-change still moved the counter, since the old logic keyed off `status` alone). Fixed by introducing a **single seat-accounting model** in [src/lib/registration-seat.ts](src/lib/registration-seat.ts): `holdsSeat(status, mode)` (a reg holds a seat iff `status≠CANCELLED && IN_PERSON`), `planSeatTransition(prev, next)` → `{ release, claim }` ticket-type ids, and `needsQrCode`. Both update paths — REST PUT [registrations/[registrationId]/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/%5BregistrationId%5D/route.ts) and MCP `update_registration` ([tools/registrations.ts](src/lib/agent/tools/registrations.ts)) — now **route every `TicketType.soldCount` delta through `planSeatTransition`** (replacing the ad-hoc status/type branches; preserves the existing cancel/reactivate/type-change behavior exactly for non-virtual + fixes virtual) and **lazily mint a barcode** on virtual→in-person (in-person→virtual releases the seat, keeps the barcode for audit). Capacity-guarded via the atomic `soldCount < quantity` claim predicate — a sold-out virtual→in-person hard-fails `CAPACITY_EXCEEDED` and the reg stays virtual (a valid state, nobody stranded). New **Attendance** Select on the registration detail sheet ([registration-detail-sheet.tsx](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/registration-detail-sheet.tsx), HYBRID events + `!isReviewer`, via `useEvent`); MCP `update_registration` gained an `attendanceMode` param (pkg 0.4.11→0.4.12 + lockfile). Tests: 15 unit (the pure model — every transition incl. the latent virtual bugs) + 3 integration (the MCP executor actually moves `soldCount` + mints/keeps the barcode + CAPACITY_EXCEEDED). **Adversarial review = no blockers**; in-band it also closed a pre-existing REST IDOR (the request-supplied `ticketTypeId` is now event-scoped before the tx, parity with MCP) + added `attendanceMode`/`qrCodeMinted` to the MCP audit + documented the no-reprice boundary. New `src/lib/can-write.ts` `canWrite(role)` helper (added in the same session for the abstracts MEMBER-gate) is unrelated to this toggle (the toggle uses `!isReviewer` to match the PUT's `REGISTRATION_DESK_ALLOW`). **Deferred (review-flagged, in ROADMAP):** mode change does NOT recompute price/amount-owed (`virtualPrice` vs in-person — documented in the toggle + MCP description, matches the deferred "tier-windowed virtual pricing"); the detail-sheet inline-Select TOCTOU (quick-actions don't send `expectedUpdatedAt` → two concurrent seat-moving edits can double-release) is pre-existing + folds into the P1.1 `soldCount` reconciliation pass. tsc/eslint/vitest 1683/build green.

- **Correctness batch — auto-issue stall-reclaim + frontend silent-failure surfacing (June 26, 2026)** — Three backlog correctness fixes from [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md), each gated + atomic. **(1) Cert auto-issue Phase-2 H2 — `reclaimStalledRuns` is now `autoIssue`-aware** (`f1ca449`, [src/lib/certificates/issue-worker.ts](src/lib/certificates/issue-worker.ts)). The worker's stall detector demoted any stalled `SENDING` run → `AWAITING_REVIEW`; correct for **manual** runs (operator re-confirms via Send) but a **survey-gated auto run has no operator**, so if its email phase stalled >10 min (SES outage / container restart mid-send) it sat in `AWAITING_REVIEW` un-emailed forever — and the registration is already terminally stamped, so the sweep won't re-enqueue → **silent cert non-delivery**. Now the SENDING reclaim partitions: manual (`autoIssue: false`) → `AWAITING_REVIEW`; auto (`autoIssue: true`) → **stay `SENDING`**, just refresh `lastTickAt` so the next tick re-drains the remaining `emailedAt`-null items (send phase is re-entrant; per-item failures already marked + excluded). Exported `reclaimStalledRuns` + 2 unit tests (the worker's render/send mechanics had no prior unit coverage). **(2) Registrant portal no longer silently shows "not registered" on a failed fetch** (`3fd6ca1`, [src/app/e/[slug]/my-registration/page.tsx](src/app/e/%5Bslug%5D/my-registration/page.tsx)). It ignored React Query's `isError`, so a failed `/api/registrant/registrations` fetch fell through to the "Not registered yet" empty state — a paying registrant would think their registration vanished. Now branches on `isError` → a red "Couldn't load your registration — your registration is safe, please try again" card with a Try-again (`refetch`) button, and logs to console/Sentry; the `queryFn` error carries the HTTP status. (Loading was already an early-return; the global `/my-registration` gateway is a server component that throws to the error boundary, so neither needed changing.) **(3) Bulk-tag failure now toasts** (`a1d4559`, [src/components/bulk-tag-dialog.tsx](src/components/bulk-tag-dialog.tsx)). `handleSubmit` awaited the caller's `onSubmit` and on a thrown mutation surfaced nothing (the caller's success toast is skipped by the throw); now it catches → `toast.error` + `console.error` and keeps the dialog open for retry — covers both the registrations + speakers callers (DRY, in the shared dialog). All verified tsc/eslint/vitest 1662/build green; ROADMAP rows updated (H2 shipped; "Frontend silent failures" now partial — MEMBER `canWrite(role)` gate + GET-load `!res.ok` swallows still open).
