Security primitives baked in: extension allowlist (`.md`, `.html`, `.htm`), directory blocklist (`node_modules`, `.next`, `.git`, `.turbo`, `out`, `dist`, `build`, `coverage`, `playwright-report`, `test-results`, `.vercel`, plus `public/uploads/` as a hard block at the directory level), path-traversal guard via `resolveSafe()` (absolute path must stay within `process.cwd()`, nulls rejected, leading separators stripped, re-checked after symlink resolution), 1 MB per-file cap (anything bigger is a sign of something that shouldn't be in /docs), literal-substring search (NOT regex — protects against ReDoS from operator-typed patterns), 100-hit cap on search results. Three API routes ([src/app/api/admin/docs/tree/route.ts](src/app/api/admin/docs/tree/route.ts), [src/app/api/admin/docs/file/route.ts](src/app/api/admin/docs/file/route.ts), [src/app/api/admin/docs/search/route.ts](src/app/api/admin/docs/search/route.ts)) each re-check `role === "ADMIN" || role === "SUPER_ADMIN"` server-side (page-level guard is defense-in-depth, sidebar uses `adminOnly: true` flag). Search route has 60/hr/user rate limit. Page at [src/app/(dashboard)/admin/docs/page.tsx](src/app/%28dashboard%29/admin/docs/page.tsx): split layout, collapsible tree on left with auto-expand of ancestors when a deep-linked file is active (React 19's "store info from previous render" pattern, not `useEffect + setState`), content on right. Markdown → ReactMarkdown + remark-gfm with the same `prose` styling the help-chat uses but with `prose-code:bg-transparent prose-code:text-foreground` so inline code blends with the dashboard theme (no muted backgrounds, no white-on-dark). HTML → sandboxed iframe with `sandbox="allow-same-origin"` only (no `allow-scripts`), so the styled `docs/*.html` files (EC2_HARDENING, CERTIFICATES, user-guide) keep their original look without colliding with the dashboard theme AND any future supply-chain injection in a committed HTML file can't execute inside the dashboard origin. "Open in new tab" affordance for the full-screen styled HTML view. Default landing tries `infra/dr/README.md` (most useful "where do I start" doc for ops work), falls back to `docs/HANDOVER.md`, then `CLAUDE.md`. Debounced 300ms search (typing "registr" doesn't fire 7 requests), grouped results by file path with line + ~80-char context, max 5 hits shown per file with "+N more" tail. Copy-path button on every file header. Verified: tsc + lint + 1328/1328 vitest + build clean.

- **Certificates system — v3 PDF-overlay + multi-template + tag-driven Issue + cover-email editor + audit hardening (June 2, 2026)** — Major build over 12+ commits (`b226f16` → `425d979`). The v2 compose-from-assets cert renderer (banner + signatures + footer logos assembled by the platform) was replaced wholesale with a **PDF-overlay model**: the designer hands the organizer a finished cert PDF (or PNG/JPG that the upload route server-converts via `pdf-lib`'s `embedPng` / `embedJpg`), the canvas editor at [src/components/certificates/certificate-canvas-editor.tsx](src/components/certificates/certificate-canvas-editor.tsx) rasterizes page 1 via `pdfjs-dist` (self-hosted worker at `/pdfjs/pdf.worker.min.mjs`, copied by [scripts/copy-pdfjs-worker.mjs](scripts/copy-pdfjs-worker.mjs) at postinstall), and `react-rnd` handles drag + resize of text-box overlays. The renderer at [src/lib/certificates/render.ts](src/lib/certificates/render.ts) is ~250 LOC of pdf-lib code that loads the background PDF, embeds the 12 standard fonts on demand, and paints each text box with `mergeBody()` token substitution + alignment + the top-left ↔ bottom-left coordinate flip the editor's editor-Y → pdf-lib-Y conversion needs.

  **Cert types collapsed 4 → 2**: ATTENDANCE + APPRECIATION (was ATTENDANCE / PRESENTER / POSTER / CME). Migration `20260602110000_collapse_certificate_types_to_two` does the Postgres `ALTER TYPE RENAME` + swap + ALTER COLUMN dance (no live data — Phase C was shipped earlier the same day with zero issued certs). CME / accreditations stay as event-level data consumed via `{{cmeHours}}` / `{{accreditationBody}}` / `{{accreditationReference}}` tokens on either category's text boxes — not a separate cert type any more.

  **Multi-template per category**: replaced the `Event.settings.certificateTemplates` 2-slot JSON with a proper `CertificateTemplate` table (migration `20260602120000_certificate_template_table`). An event can have N templates per category — "Standard Attendance", "VIP Attendance", "Chairman Appreciation", etc. Each has its own backgroundPdfUrl, textBoxes, sortOrder, and (post-`32a3610`) optional `emailSubject` + `emailBody` cover-email defaults. `IssuedCertificate.certificateTemplateId` + `CertificateIssueRun.certificateTemplateId` FKs preserve audit-trail integrity (SetNull on delete; the API layer additionally blocks DELETE with 409 when any issued cert references the template).

  **One cert per recipient per category** invariant is enforced by `IssuedCertificate`'s dual `@@unique([eventId, type, registrationId|speakerId])` constraints, catching concurrent operator clicks + MCP retries that race past the application-level eligibility exclusion. Serials are category-scoped via `CertificateSerialCounter` (atomic upsert+increment under a `@@id([eventId, type])` PK).

  **Tag-driven manual Issue (no auto-eligibility)** — per the organizer's "no auto eligibility" call. The eligibility worker takes a `tag` parameter; ATTENDANCE template + tag X → registrations in event where `Attendee.tags` includes X (Registration→Attendee FK; tags live on Attendee), APPRECIATION template + tag X → speakers where `Speaker.tags` includes X (abstract submitters inherit `Speaker.tags` because submitters are persisted as Speaker rows with `Abstract.speakerId` as a required FK). The `/eligible` route has two modes via the same response shape — without `tag` it returns `availableTags: [{ tag, count }]` for the picker, with `tag` it returns the filtered recipient list. Issue route body requires `{templateId, tag, emailSubject, emailBody}`; the concurrent-run guard + tx are unified into a single `$transaction` (H5 fix from the audit) so two fast-clicks can't both pass the in-progress check.

  **Cover-email editor opens at Issue click** — Tiptap WYSIWYG dialog at [src/components/certificates/cert-email-editor-dialog.tsx](src/components/certificates/cert-email-editor-dialog.tsx), reused twice (once for per-template defaults from the Templates tab, once for per-run overrides from the Issue tab). 8 tokens total (recipientName, eventName, eventDateRange, venueLine, organizationName, certificateType, certificateSerial, plus abstractTitle on APPRECIATION which looks up the speaker's accepted abstract via Abstract FK, POSTER preferred). Token resolver split between client-safe constants (`src/lib/certificates/email-tokens.ts` — system defaults + spec) and server-only resolver (`src/lib/certificates/email-tokens-resolver.ts` — DB lookups + structured warn logs) because Turbopack tried to bundle the server-only Pino logger into the client when the page imported the constants. Snapshotted onto the run row at Issue confirm so a later template edit doesn't change in-flight emails. The send phase applies the per-event branding pipeline via `wrapWithBranding()` + `inlineCss()` — header image, footer HTML, footer image, sender override, CSS inlining all apply (H1 fix from the audit: pre this change the cert email bypassed the pipeline entirely).

  **Image upload conversion** — Upload route at [src/app/api/upload/pdf/route.ts](src/app/api/upload/pdf/route.ts) accepts PDF/JPG/PNG via magic-byte detection (`%PDF-`, `89 50 4E 47`, `FF D8 FF`); images get wrapped in a single-page PDF where page dims = image's intrinsic pixel dimensions as points, so downstream code only ever sees PDFs. 10 MB cap (was 5 MB; bumped because full-res PNG cert designs commonly land at 5-8 MB). The route validates `eventId` against a cuid regex BEFORE touching the filesystem (B1 from the audit: defense-in-depth against `../../media` traversal) AND verifies the event belongs to the caller's org via `db.event.findFirst` (H7 from the audit: cross-tenant upload-into-another-org's-directory is structurally impossible).

  **Issue lifecycle**: PENDING → RENDERING → AWAITING_REVIEW → SENDING → COMPLETED, with FAILED + CANCELLED branches. The AWAITING_REVIEW gate is the operator's spot-check before 300-5000 emails fan out. Cron worker drains 50 renders/tick + 25 emails/tick (SES-safe at 14/sec sustained), heartbeats `lastTickAt` so the stall detector reclaims runs stuck >10 min, per-item try/catch so one bad recipient can't kill a batch, and HARD-fails the run rather than fall back to a placeholder PDF if the template gets deleted mid-run (H4 from the audit). The design-approval gate was dropped — the PDF-overlay model makes the design tangible enough (canvas + Preview button) that a separate SUPER_ADMIN sign-off step is unwarranted.

  **MCP tools (5)**: `list_certificate_templates`, `create_certificate_template`, `update_certificate_template`, `delete_certificate_template`, `update_cme_settings`. All accept the cover-email defaults; tool definitions at [src/lib/agent/tools/certificates.ts](src/lib/agent/tools/certificates.ts), Zod params at [src/lib/agent/register-mcp-tools.ts](src/lib/agent/register-mcp-tools.ts). The Issue flow itself is NOT exposed via MCP — interactive email-confirmation step, operator-only.

  **Independent senior code review** caught 4 BLOCKERs + 8 HIGHs in the post-build pass; all blockers + 6 highs fixed in-band: B1 path-traversal + cross-tenant upload (cuid + org-bound check), B2 XSS in cert delivery email (escapeHtml on recipientName/eventName/orgName), B3 canvas PATCH spam (page-level 400ms debounce + optimistic React Query cache + flush on editor close — typing "Hello" was 5 server writes), B4 draft-wipe-on-window-focus (`JSON.stringify` deep-equal instead of object-reference comparison since React Query's `refetchOnWindowFocus: true` returns fresh objects), H2 silent-4xx logging sweep, H3 sortOrder race (transactional aggregate+create), H4 template-deleted-mid-run (fail run hard), H5 concurrent-run guard not transactional (moved findFirst into the same `$transaction` as the create), H6 package version bump for MCP cache invalidation, H8 no-org logging consistency. H1 (cert-email branding-pipeline bypass) landed in `32a3610` along with the cover-email editor.

  **User-facing docs**: full §18 added to [public/user-guide.html](public/user-guide.html) (operator-facing — picked up by the help chat at module init, no chat-code change needed); developer architecture at [docs/CERTIFICATES.md](docs/CERTIFICATES.md). MCP reference at [docs/MCP_REFERENCE.md](docs/MCP_REFERENCE.md) gained a Certificates section (now 70 tools). HANDOVER.md Recent Major Additions header updated. Help chat starter chips at [src/components/help-chat/help-chat-sheet.tsx](src/components/help-chat/help-chat-sheet.tsx) gained "How do I issue certificates after the event?" for SUPER_ADMIN / ADMIN / ORGANIZER roles.

  **Deploy story**: blue-green via `scripts/deploy.sh` — applies the migrations (additive: cert types collapse + template table + email-fields columns) before container swap. STORAGE_PROVIDER setting was an early-build false alarm and is currently unset (defaults to `local`, which is correct for EC2 — Phase C cert PDFs land in `public/uploads/certificates/issued/{runId}/{certId}.pdf`). Package bumped 0.3.9 → 0.4.0 (cert collapse) → 0.4.1 (image upload) → 0.4.2 (cover-email editor) → 0.4.3 (MCP cover-email fields). Verified: tsc clean, lint clean, 1328/1328 vitest, `npm run build` clean.

- **Help-chatbot (Sonnet 4.6, KB-grounded) — sidebar drawer (May 21, 2026)** — Read-only AI assistant accessible from the dashboard sidebar footer. Answers "how do I" questions from `public/user-guide.html` via Anthropic prompt-cached system prompt. **Distinct from the existing AI Agent** (which mutates event data via 65+ tools): this one only explains, can't act. Six-commit staged rollout (`c076aa0` → `b3a6bc4`), planned in [docs/HELP_CHATBOT.md](docs/HELP_CHATBOT.md). **Architecture**: new `src/lib/ai/` provider abstraction (`AiProvider` interface + Anthropic implementation + central model config — future vendor swaps are config flips, not rewrites; the existing AI Agent stays untouched and retrofits later as v1.1 work); `src/lib/help-chat/guide-loader.ts` (reads + strips HTML once at module init, security-tested removal of `<script>`/`<style>`/comment bodies); `src/lib/help-chat/system-prompt.ts` (two-block `SystemBlock[]`: cached stable instructions + guide + uncached role-aware tail — cache-prefix order matters and is unit-pinned); `POST /api/help-chat` with SSE streaming via the abstraction, per-user 50/hr rate limit, Zod-validated body, role-aware system prompt (SUPER_ADMIN / ADMIN / ORGANIZER / MEMBER / REVIEWER / SUBMITTER / REGISTRANT — MEMBER specifically warned to refer finance questions to admin per the Mecomed-sensitive RBAC policy); React drawer (`src/components/help-chat/help-chat-sheet.tsx`) on the `Sheet` primitive with typing-dots placeholder, ReactMarkdown + remark-gfm rendering matching the AI Agent's `prose` styling, localStorage persistence (`ea-sys:help-chat:v1:<userId>`, 40-msg cap, schema versioned); `HelpChatProvider` mounts the drawer once at the dashboard root and exposes `useHelpChatLauncher()` so the sidebar Help button opens it without prop-drilling. **Cost (measured vs planned)**: guide is ~12K tokens (planned 30K); warm-cache call ~$0.008 (planned $0.022); 1k Q/month ~$8 (planned $33). **Privacy posture**: Anthropic enterprise terms; logs metadata only (userId, role, token counts, latency) — message bodies NEVER logged. **Visual differentiation from AI Agent**: HelpCircle icon vs Sparkles; "Help Assistant" header vs "AI Agent"; muted drawer styling vs primary-tinted; explicit "for doing things on an event, use the AI Agent in Tools" prompt copy. **Tests**: +44 unit (11 Anthropic adapter — system block cache flag mapping, stream filtering, null-cache-token mapping, missing API key fail-fast; 12 stripHtml — script/style/comment body removal as security property, entity decoding, space-replace tag stripping; 21 system prompt — 2-block structure, refusal-pattern keywords pinned as safety harness, role-tail differentiation, name/org fallbacks). Suite 1237 → 1281. **E2E**: `e2e/help-chat.spec.ts` — hermetic with mocked SSE response (no real Anthropic in CI); pins UI shell (sidebar trigger, drawer opens, role-tailored starter chips, clear-chat hidden in empty state) + plumbing (fetch → SSE parse → markdown render → clear chat resets). Caveat: spec requires Playwright to spawn its own dev server (the saved port-drift memory about `PORT=3113`); reusing a locally-running dev server bound to the development DB will fail at login because the test users don't exist there — stop the dev server before `npm run test:e2e`. **Deferred to v1.1** (in [docs/HELP_CHATBOT.md](docs/HELP_CHATBOT.md) §17): retrofit existing AI Agent onto the `AiProvider` abstraction; provider-fallback for reliability; local Ollama as a privacy escape hatch; `👍/👎` feedback capture per assistant message; cross-device server-side conversation history; multi-language; public-guide widget; quote-style markdown subset trimming for tighter style control.

- **registration-detail-sheet.tsx staged refactor — A → E (May 20, 2026)** — The 2,174-line monolithic registration detail sheet went through a careful 5-commit staged refactor, each step independently revertable, each gated by tsc + lint + full vitest + build + Playwright regression. **Step A (`8ad760b`)** typed `useBillingAccounts` / `useBillingAccount` returns in `src/hooks/use-api.ts` (new `BillingAccountRow` / `BillingAccountDetail` interfaces mirroring the API response shape) → removed 3 `any[]` casts from the picker call sites. **Step B (`25b3299`)** extracted [src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/registrations/registration-edit-mapping.ts](src/app/%28dashboard%29/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/registration-edit-mapping.ts) — pure `toEditData(reg)` + `toServerPayload(editData, expectedUpdatedAt)` mappers + `RegistrationEditData` interface + `EMPTY_REGISTRATION_EDIT_DATA` defaults. The same ~30-field shape used to live inline three times in the sheet (initial useState defaults / `startEditing` populate / `saveEdits` payload assembly). Critical: the mappers preserve every null-vs-undefined-vs-trim normalization decision exactly — billing/tax/payer trim-to-null on save (deliberate clear), attendee free-text → undefined (PUT treats as "unchanged"), association/memberId/studentId → null (CAN clear), photo `?? null`, payer triplet atomicity (setting `billingAccountId=""` forces `payerReference=null + attendeeIsGuarantor=false`), `expectedUpdatedAt` is the W2-F8 optimistic-lock token. 14 unit tests pin every decision + the studentIdExpiry ISO parse + the `attendeeIsGuarantor ?? false` legacy-null path + a round-trip identity. Sheet **−99 lines**. **Step C (`9cdf002`)** introduced [src/lib/api-fetch.ts](src/lib/api-fetch.ts): `ApiError` (Error subclass with `status` + `code` + raw `data`) + `apiFetch` / `apiPostJson` / `apiPutJson` / `apiDelete` thin method helpers. The existing `fetchApi` in `use-api.ts` throws plain `Error(message)` which is fine for queries, but mutations sometimes need to branch on status + code (STALE_WRITE, BILLING_ACCOUNT_INACTIVE, CAPACITY_EXCEEDED). All 5 mutations in the sheet (update / check-in / send-email / delete / refund) collapsed from 8-line fetch+throw boilerplate to one-line arrow expressions; `updateRegistration.onError` uses `error instanceof ApiError` to branch on STALE_WRITE instead of manual error-shape casting. `apiPostJson` skips Content-Type when body is undefined (empty-body action routes like `/check-in`, `/refund`). +8 unit tests pin the helper. Sheet **−38 lines**. **Step D (`5e3d486`)** fixed the prop-sync. The previous `if (registration !== selectedRegistration && registration !== null)` compared the prop to **derived state** which (a) tripped React 19's setState-during-render rule and (b) had a latent **prop-revert race** — after a mutation's onSuccess updated `selectedRegistration` to the fresh server row, the stale parent prop diverged and the next render would silently revert the just-saved data. Replaced with React 19's canonical "Storing information from previous renders" pattern: a `prevRegistration` state snapshot is compared against the incoming prop; `setPrevRegistration` and the derived-state updates fire in the same render pass; sync runs ONLY when the prop actually changes. Diff +21/−4. **Step E (`64dc640`)** extracted 5 inline handlers near the existing `handlePreviewRegistrationEmail`: `handlePrintBadge` (was a 30-line inline async block with try/catch/finally + blob lifecycle + setTimeout cleanup), `handleDeleteClick`, `handleRefundClick`, `openEmailDialog(type)` (collapses 4 near-identical DropdownMenuItem onClicks), `handleConfirmSendEmail`. JSX call sites now read as one-liner `onClick={handleX}` expressions. **Cumulative**: sheet 2,174 → ~2,063 lines (~−110 net), **+22 unit tests** that didn't exist before, one latent bug squashed, type signatures tightened end-to-end. **F + G + H tracked in [docs/ROADMAP.md](docs/ROADMAP.md)** "registration-detail-sheet.tsx staged refactor remainder" with explicit trigger conditions for when to revisit each (F: only with H or under measured input lag; G: when file >3k lines or next feature touches >2 sections painfully; H: when a feature needs per-field control like autosave-on-blur). Verified post-step by running the 62-spec Playwright suite — 58 passed, 0 regressions from A–E (the 4 unrelated bulk-email failures pre-date these commits; git diff proved none of the 7 files touched appear in the bulk-email dialog import graph).

- **Per-event payer scoping — EventBillingAccount junction (May 20, 2026)** — The v1 ship (May 19) made `BillingAccount` org-scoped, which caused **picker overflow**: every active payer in the org appeared in every event's "Charge to" dropdown. Refactored to a many-to-many via junction so a payer must be **explicitly attached** to each event where it's available — same logical row, never duplicated across events. **Schema**: new `EventBillingAccount { id, eventId, billingAccountId, addedAt, addedByUserId, @@unique([eventId, billingAccountId]) }`; FKs Cascade from both ends (deleting either entity unlinks but doesn't delete the other; Registration→BillingAccount stays Restrict so existing assignments survive a detach). Migration `20260520120000_event_billing_account_junction` is additive + junction starts empty (v1 not yet deployed, no pairs to backfill). **API**: `GET /api/billing-accounts?eventId=…` filters via junction membership (org-bound at the event end too — a foreign eventId returns `[]`, no cross-tenant attachment leak); new idempotent `POST/DELETE /api/events/[eventId]/billing-accounts/[billingAccountId]` (denyReviewer+denyFinance, both ids org-bound before touching the junction). **Hooks**: `useBillingAccounts({ eventId })` threaded into Add Registration form + detail-sheet reassign picker — each event now sees only its attached payers. **Edge case**: detail-sheet Select shows a synthetic option `(no longer attached to this event)` when a registration's current payer was detached after assignment, so the value renders truthfully instead of going blank. **UI**: `BillingAccountsCard` (Settings → Billing) gained a clickable "Events" count column + a `CalendarDays` icon action → `EventsAttachmentDialog` with one checkbox per org event (attach/detach with idempotent fetch + toast + queryClient invalidation). Detail GET on `/api/billing-accounts/[id]` now returns `attachedEvents` alongside the registrations AR view. **View-mode UX fix (May 20, also `d939a20`)**: registration-detail-sheet Billing tab always shows a "Charge to:" status row in view mode ("Cleveland Clinic · attendee is guarantor · Ref PO-12345" or "Attendee — self-pay"), so organizers don't have to click Edit to see the current state. **Tests**: +10 new attach/detach cases (RBAC for MEMBER, IDOR org-binding on both ends, inactive-payer 400, upsert idempotency on POST, deleteMany idempotency on DELETE). Suite 1205 → 1215. tsc + lint + build clean. **Software-engineering name**: this is a **many-to-many association via a junction (associative / link / bridge) table** with **shared identity** — the BillingAccount is referenced by multiple Events through the junction, never duplicated. In DDD terms, BillingAccount is its own aggregate; the junction makes per-event availability an explicit relationship rather than ownership. Package unchanged at 0.3.7 (no MCP-visible tool surface change).

- **"Charge to another account" — third-party payer / BillingAccount (May 19, 2026)** — Doctors are often paid for by their hospital or by a pharma grant covering a specific HCP. New reusable org-scoped `BillingAccount` model (the payer) + `Registration.billingAccountId` / `payerReference` / `attendeeIsGuarantor`. **Orthogonal to `paymentStatus` by design** (the explicit anti-INCLUSIVE decision): money is still owed and the registration stays UNPAID/PENDING — this only redirects the invoice *bill-to* party and suppresses the attendee Pay-Now path. Distinct from `Event.settings.sponsors[]` (bulk pre-paid INCLUSIVE) and the `Registration.billing*` block (same payer, different address). Migration `20260519120000_add_billing_account` is purely additive (every existing reg defaults to self-pay). **Service**: [src/services/billing-account-service.ts](src/services/billing-account-service.ts) (create/update, soft-delete via `isActive`, `@@unique([organizationId,name])` dedupe → `DUPLICATE_NAME` with existing id in meta, errors-as-values, audit). **Registration wiring**: `registration-service.createRegistration` + REST POST + REST PUT + MCP `create_registration`/`update_registration` accept the three fields with org-scoped+active validation (new codes `BILLING_ACCOUNT_NOT_FOUND` / `BILLING_ACCOUNT_INACTIVE`); PUT/MCP `billingAccountId:null` reverts to self-pay (the fallback path). **Invoice/Quote PDF**: bill-to renders the payer (name/address/VAT) with the attendee dropped to a reference line + PO/grant ref ([src/lib/quote-pdf.ts](src/lib/quote-pdf.ts), [src/lib/invoice-pdf.ts](src/lib/invoice-pdf.ts), [src/lib/invoice-service.ts](src/lib/invoice-service.ts)). **Finance boundary**: `billingAccount`/`billingAccountId`/`payerReference`/`attendeeIsGuarantor` added to `FINANCIAL_KEYS` — MEMBER never sees who funds a doctor (Mecomed-sensitive); BillingAccount REST routes ([src/app/api/billing-accounts/route.ts](src/app/api/billing-accounts/route.ts) + `[billingAccountId]`) are `denyFinance`+`denyReviewer` gated, org-scoped. **UI**: `BillingAccountsCard` in Settings → Billing (CRUD + soft-delete + needs-review badge); payer picker + PO + guarantor on the full-page Add Registration form; reassign/guarantor/revert + "Billed to" pill on the registration detail sheet's finance-gated Billing tab. Package 0.3.6 → 0.3.7. **Tests**: +13 (billing-account-service, registration-service payer cases, finance redaction). Suite 1195 → 1205; tsc + lint + build clean. **Deferred to v1.1** (tracked in ROADMAP): public-registration "who pays" step (schema/route already carry `needsReview` for the dedupe flow), the quick-Add *dialog* picker (consistent with its existing pricingTier/sponsor gap), standalone `list/create_billing_account` MCP tools (payer mgmt is a Settings task; the agent assigns existing payers via the create/update params), registrations-list "Payer" column + CSV, AR aging by payer, VAT reverse-charge by payer taxNumber (v1 prints the number but does NOT change the rate — finance-correctness), consolidated invoicing, auto-revert-on-nonpayment cron.

- **Multi-agent audit remediation — 2 BLOCKERs + 4 HIGHs (May 18, 2026)** — A supervisor + 4 specialist review agents (React, Prisma, backend/RBAC, architecture) swept the codebase; the six findings verified against source were fixed in one batch. **(B1) Cross-tenant IDOR on event email templates** — [src/app/api/events/[eventId]/email-templates/[templateId]/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/email-templates/%5BtemplateId%5D/route.ts) GET/PUT/DELETE/POST/PATCH resolved the template by `{ id, eventId }` (both from the URL) with **zero `organizationId` binding** — any authenticated user in any org could read/overwrite/reset/delete another org's templates or exfiltrate rendered content via POST `action:"test"`. All five handlers now bind the event to `session.user.organizationId` (404, not 403, to avoid enumeration) before touching the template, mirroring the sibling list route. **(B2) `soldCount` never released on cancel via MCP** — REST PUT decremented `TicketType.soldCount` on →CANCELLED and re-incremented on reactivate, but MCP `update_registration` only adjusted soldCount on ticket-type change and `bulk_update_registration_status` was a bare `updateMany` with none — so "cancel all unpaid registrations" via the agent/n8n silently inflated soldCount and the event **falsely reported sold-out, rejecting paying registrants**. Both MCP paths in [src/lib/agent/tools/registrations.ts](src/lib/agent/tools/registrations.ts) now mirror REST: single-update gets the four-case branch (becoming-cancelled→decrement / reactivating→capacity-guarded increment with `CAPACITY_EXCEEDED` / type-change / no-op) and bulk groups affected rows per ticket type inside a transaction (cancel→decrement, reactivate→increment; bulk reactivation may oversell but logs `registration:bulk-reactivate-oversold` rather than failing 200 rows — single-row still hard-blocks). **(H3) Registrations LIST finance leak** — [src/app/api/events/[eventId]/registrations/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/route.ts) GET returned full `payments` (amount, cardLast4, receiptUrl, bank ref) + prices with no redaction while detail/tickets/event GETs redacted for MEMBER; now `redactFinancialFields` when `orgCtx.role` is a non-finance role (API-key auth, `role:null`, stays full — admin-equivalent, MEMBER can't mint keys). **(H4) Contacts write-guard bypass** — `contacts/route.ts`, `contacts/[contactId]/route.ts` (PUT+DELETE), `contacts/bulk-tags`, `contacts/import`, `contacts/[contactId]/email` used inline `ctx.role === "REVIEWER" || "SUBMITTER"`, letting **MEMBER + REGISTRANT write/delete org contacts**. All six sites now route through `denyReviewer({ user: { role: ctx.role ?? undefined } })` (single source of truth — blocks REVIEWER/SUBMITTER/REGISTRANT/MEMBER; API-key `role:null`→undefined passes as before). **(H5) PaymentStatus enum drift** — `ALL_PAYMENT_STATUSES` in [src/lib/agent/tools/_shared.ts](src/lib/agent/tools/_shared.ts) was a hand-list missing `INCLUSIVE`, so MCP `update_registration`/`bulk_update_registration_status` rejected INCLUSIVE as invalid and the sponsor-paid handling downstream was unreachable; now derived from `Object.values(PaymentStatus)` (the generated Prisma enum) so it cannot drift, and the local `PAYMENT_STATUSES` filter list in `registrations.ts` (was also missing UNASSIGNED+INCLUSIVE) collapsed to the same derived set. **(H6) `getNextSerialId` race** — [src/lib/registration-serial.ts](src/lib/registration-serial.ts) used `aggregate(_max: serialId) + 1`, which takes no row lock under Read Committed even in a transaction → concurrent registrations collided on `@@unique([eventId, serialId])` and the public register route mis-reported the P2002 as "You are already registered". Replaced with an atomic upsert+increment on a new `RegistrationSerialCounter` table (one row per event, PK `eventId`, `onDelete: Cascade`); migration `20260518120000_add_registration_serial_counter` is additive + backfills `lastSerial = MAX(serialId)` per event so it's blue-green safe (old container keeps MAX+1 against an untouched table; first new-code increment yields the same MAX+1; `@@unique` remains the net). **Tests**: +20 (auth-guards MEMBER/REGISTRANT/undefined cases; new `agent-payment-status-set`, `registration-serial`, `registration-cancel-soldcount`, `api/events/email-templates/idor`). Suite 1175 → 1195. Package 0.3.5 → 0.3.6 (MCP cache-invalidation hint — agent tool *behavior* changed). Verification: tsc + lint + 1195 vitest + build clean. **Corroborated-but-not-yet-fixed** (deferred, tracked): accommodation overbooking TOCTOU, registration DELETE deleting a shared Attendee, `PricingTier.soldCount` one-way leak on delete/bulk-type, Stripe post-payment invoice/email fire-and-forget with no reconciliation, registrant invoice/quote routes missing `denyFinance`, `refreshEventStats` lost-update, ~8 silent `safeParse`→400 sites, frontend silent failures (bulk-tag toast, registrant portal "no registrations" on fetch error), MCP finance boundary / OAuth role-snapshot, blue-green non-additive-migration guardrail. Doc drift noted: CLAUDE.md says `src/middleware.ts` (now `src/proxy.ts`, Next 16.1 rename) and "0 silent Invalid-input paths" (false) and stdio MCP "drifts" (stale — now shares `registerAllMcpTools()`).

- **Admin full pricing-tier control on manual add (May 18, 2026)** — The manual Add Registration full-page form ([src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/registrations/new/page.tsx](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/new/page.tsx)) filtered the Pricing Tier picker to `isActive` tiers only, so organizers couldn't record a late registrant at a *closed* Early Bird rate as a courtesy. The backend (`registration-service.ts`) already only validated tier→ticket-type membership (no `isActive` requirement), so the restriction was a frontend-only artifact. Fix: `activeTiers` → `availableTiers` (drop the `.filter(isActive)`), POST guard validates against the full set, inactive tiers render as `Early Bird (inactive) — USD 400` so the admin picks informed, ticket-type Select hides the `- $X` suffix when the type has **any** tiers (the tier dropdown is the source of truth on this path). **Asymmetry preserved by design**: the public self-register path (`/api/public/events/[slug]/register`) still gates `isActive: true`. **The add-registration *dialog* has no tier picker** (the full-page form is the only tier-selection surface); its `isActive` price-suffix check is correctly scoped and unchanged. **Accepted tradeoffs, documented in a block comment at [src/services/registration-service.ts](src/services/registration-service.ts) tier-validation** (organizer decision — leave as-is, don't re-add the restriction): (1) the manual path bumps only `ticketType.soldCount`, never `PricingTier.soldCount`, so a manually-assigned (esp. closed) tier does **not** consume that tier's inventory and is never blocked by its quantity/closed cap — intentional, a courtesy seat must not burn a real paid Early Bird seat; consequence is `PricingTier.soldCount` under-counts vs actual rows, so the "Registrations by Tier" dashboard tile (counts rows, not soldCount — correct) is authoritative and anything reporting off `PricingTier.soldCount` directly will diverge; (2) tier is now an explicit assignment, not a proxy for "registered during that sales window" — an Early Bird row may have a `createdAt` after Early Bird closed, so finance reconciliation must treat tier as stated, not derived from registration date / `salesEnd`; (3) only ticket-type membership is enforced, not "the right tier within that type" — the field is as accurate as the admin's click. **All reporting verified accurate**: dashboard tile, list "Tier" column, CSV export, and `computeRegistrationFinancials` (subtotal = `pricingTier?.price ?? ticketType?.price`) all resolve the tier by id with no `isActive` gate, so a courtesy-rate registration is correctly named, counted, and priced. Verification: tsc + lint + build clean, 1175/1175 unit tests passing. Commit `434a45e` (feature) + this doc/comment follow-up.

- **Workflow tiles on Communications page (May 14, 2026)** — The 4-filter intersection model added in the previous round was technically powerful but cognitively heavy. Flipped to a **tiles + escape hatch** layout: each audience card (Registrations, Speakers) now opens with a grid of one-click workflow tiles at the top, with the existing dropdown filter grid moved into a collapsed `<details>Advanced filters</details>` block. **Speakers tiles** (6): Send Invitations (status=INVITED → invitation), Chase Agreements (CONFIRMED + unsigned → agreement), Brief Moderators (sessionRole=MODERATOR → custom), Brief Chairpersons (sessionRole=CHAIRPERSON → custom), Active Faculty (CONFIRMED + signed + hasSession → custom), Reinvite Declined (DECLINED → invitation). **Registrations tiles** (4): Chase Unpaid (CONFIRMED + UNPAID → custom), Welcome Paid (CONFIRMED + PAID/COMPLIMENTARY/INCLUSIVE → confirmation), Pre-event Reminder (CONFIRMED → reminder), Cancelled Re-engagement (CANCELLED → custom). Each tile shows a live recipient count (disabled at 0). Tile click bypasses the page-level filter state entirely (so an in-progress Advanced composition isn't clobbered), pushes filter combo + email type straight to the dialog. **Backend untouched** — tiles are pure frontend pre-set over `executeBulkEmail`. **New dialog prop** `defaultEmailType?: string` on [src/components/bulk-email-dialog.tsx](src/components/bulk-email-dialog.tsx) honored only on the closed → open transition, via React's "store info from previous render" pattern (set-during-render guarded by prev-value state) — `useEffect + setState` is banned under React 19's `react-hooks/set-state-in-effect`. **Welcome Paid caveat**: dialog payload supports one `paymentStatus` at a time so the tile narrows to PAID on send; matching predicate stays broad (PAID/COMPLIMENTARY/INCLUSIVE) so the count is accurate; sending to COMPLIMENTARY / INCLUSIVE separately needs Advanced filters. **Deferred**: organizer-saved tiles via `Event.settings.savedSegments[]`, tiles for Abstracts / Reviewers, multi-value `paymentStatus IN (...)` filter, audit `triggerLabel` field. Verification: tsc + lint + build clean, 1152/1152 unit tests passing.

- **Registration Type picker — drop misleading "- $0" suffix (May 14, 2026)** — On the Add Registration full-page form and dialog, the Registration Type Select rendered "Allied Health - $0" / "Physician - $0" etc. because when a type uses pricing tiers the base `TicketType.price` is typically 0 (real prices live on the tiers). The `$0` suffix read as "this is free" when the actual price comes from the Pricing Tier picker to the right. Rule: TicketType has active tiers → show just the name (Pricing Tier dropdown is the source of truth); no tiers + price > 0 → keep `Name - $X`; no tiers + price = 0 → just the name (same misleading-$0 cleanup for free / non-tier types). Applied to both surfaces ([src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/registrations/new/page.tsx:193](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/new/page.tsx#L193) + [src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/registrations/add-registration-dialog.tsx:163](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/add-registration-dialog.tsx#L163)). Public registration page handles tier-aware pricing in its own way and is unaffected. Shared `registration-type-select` doesn't render prices and is unaffected. Commit `af25e74`.

- **Communications page filters expansion (May 14, 2026)** — Two-part fix bringing the Communications page audience cards closer to parity with the registrations list page and what the bulk-email backend already supported. **Registrations card 2 → 3 filters**: added **Registration Status** dropdown (All / Pending / Confirmed / Checked In / Cancelled with live counts) at [src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/communications/page.tsx](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/communications/page.tsx). (a) **Agreement** — All / Signed / Unsigned, drives the canonical "send the agreement to everyone who hasn't signed yet" workflow, mirrors the existing MCP `list_speaker_agreements` filter. (b) **Has Session** — All / Has Session / No Session, separates active faculty (presentation guidelines, AV setup) from backup invitees. (c) **Session Role** — All / Speaker / Moderator / Chairperson / Panelist, targets role-specific briefings in a single bulk send instead of four manual ones. `sessionRole` implies "has session" naturally via the same `SessionSpeaker` join, so the filters combine freely without conditional UI. **Backend** ([src/lib/bulk-email.ts](src/lib/bulk-email.ts)): `BulkEmailFilters` type + Zod schema gain `agreementSigned: "signed" | "unsigned"`, `hasSession: "yes" | "no"`, `sessionRole: SessionRole`. No in-dialog re-select dropdowns — consistent with `statusFilter` pass-through (only `paymentStatus` has a dialog-level re-select today, added for a specific workflow). **Deferred to follow-up rounds**: MCP `list_speakers` parameter parity, Tier 2 dimensions (country / specialty / track), Tier 3 (has-accommodation / has-account), Tier 4 (tags / has-abstract), saved segments, recipient preview list. Verification: tsc + lint + build clean, 1152/1152 unit tests passing. E2e couldn't run in this round due to a pre-existing config drift — [playwright.config.ts:10](playwright.config.ts#L10) defaults `baseURL` to port 3000 while `npm run dev` now binds 3113 (per the April 29 `npm run dev` port default change), causing Playwright to try to start its own dev server and hit `EADDRINUSE` against the user's running one; the only existing bulk-email spec (`e2e/bulk-email-payment-filter.spec.ts`) exercises the registrations-recipient payment filter, which this change does not touch.

- **Pricing tier visibility — manual Add form + list column + dashboard tile (May 14, 2026)** — Organizer reporting gap: `Registration.pricingTierId` was captured on public Stripe-checkout registrations (via the URL category slug) but the manual Add Registration form never exposed a tier picker, so admin-added "Early Bird" registrations were tier-less in the database. No surface across the dashboard, list, or CSV export grouped by tier — finance had to manually correlate registration dates against tier sales windows. Triplet fix: (1) **REST POST Zod widened** at [src/app/api/events/[eventId]/registrations/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/route.ts) to accept `pricingTierId` (service already validated `PRICING_TIER_NOT_FOUND` if it didn't belong to the picked ticket type — just plumbing). (2) **Manual Add Registration form** ([src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/registrations/new/page.tsx](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/new/page.tsx)) now renders a second Select labeled "Pricing Tier" beneath the TicketType picker — only when the picked TicketType has active tiers (legacy types without tiers keep working). Tiers are read from the existing `/api/events/[id]/tickets` response's nested `pricingTiers` array (no extra fetch). When admin changes ticket type, the tier resets so a stale tier-from-a-different-type can't slip through; the body POST also guards against this by only sending `pricingTierId` when it appears in the current ticket type's active tiers. (3) **Registrations list page** gets a new "Tier" column rendered as an amber badge (visually distinct from the Type column), with `—` for tier-less rows. CSV export gains a "Pricing Tier" column between "Registration Type" and "Status". (4) **Event dashboard tile** "Registrations by Tier" at [src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/page.tsx](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/page.tsx): groups by tier *name* across all ticket types (so "Early Bird = 87" represents the union of Physician + Student + Allied Health Early Bird rows). Implemented as `db.registration.groupBy({ by: ['pricingTierId'] })` + a follow-up `pricingTier.findMany` to resolve names + sortOrder for display order. Excludes CANCELLED registrations and tier-less rows. Renders inline progress bars + percentages. Wrapped in try/catch so a failed aggregate logs but doesn't 500 the whole event page. Tile only shown when at least one tier-tagged registration exists — events without pricing tiers see no confusing empty card. **Detail sheet** already displays tier in the Payment Summary ("Standard · Early Bird"); editing tier post-create is a follow-up, intentionally deferred. **MCP `create_registration` tool definition** also gains `pricingTierId` exposure as a follow-up. **CSV import column for pricingTier** is the third follow-up (would mirror the sponsor name-resolution pattern). 1 new service test (happy-path tier persistence); suite 1151 → 1152. tsc + lint + build clean.

- **`PaymentStatus.INCLUSIVE` for sponsor-paid registrations (May 1, 2026)** — Organizer ask: when sponsors (Abbott, Pfizer, etc.) contract for N attendees and pay an offline lump sum, those registrations need to be flagged as no-money-due-from-attendee but distinguishable from regular `COMPLIMENTARY` (which is "VIP / speaker / sponsor-employee no-charge"). New enum value + new `Registration.sponsorId` column referencing an entry in `Event.settings.sponsors[]` (the existing JSON store — no Prisma table needed). Schema migration `20260501000000_add_inclusive_payment_status_and_sponsor_id` is pure-additive. **Violet badge** for INCLUSIVE (distinct from cyan COMPLIMENTARY) — see [src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/registrations/registration-enums.ts](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/registration-enums.ts) which also adds a `NO_PAYMENT_DUE_STATUSES` set (PAID/COMPLIMENTARY/INCLUSIVE/REFUNDED) for the bulk-email-chase-unpaid filter to exclude. **Service layer** ([src/services/registration-service.ts](src/services/registration-service.ts)) extended `CreateRegistrationInput` with `sponsorId`, added `INCLUSIVE_REQUIRES_SPONSOR` + `SPONSOR_NOT_FOUND` error codes (the latter returns the available-sponsors list in `meta` so callers can self-correct), and validates inside the service rather than the routes — single source of truth. INCLUSIVE was added to `MANUAL_PAYMENT_STATUSES` so admins can set it; OUTSTANDING_PAYMENT_STATUSES is unchanged, so the confirmation email + quote PDF are naturally skipped (no money due from the attendee). **`sponsorId` is preserved on status flips away from INCLUSIVE** — the historical attribution survives a revert; explicit `sponsorId: null` is the only way to clear. **REST PUT route** ([src/app/api/events/[eventId]/registrations/[registrationId]/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/%5BregistrationId%5D/route.ts)) gates the same way: computes effective `(paymentStatus, sponsorId)` after applying the patch, rejects INCLUSIVE without sponsor or unknown sponsor before the transaction so soldCount deltas don't roll back. Event lookup expanded to include `settings` for in-memory resolution. **MCP path** ([src/lib/agent/tools/registrations.ts](src/lib/agent/tools/registrations.ts)): `create_registration` + `update_registration` both accept `sponsorId`; the agent tool definitions now list the field with a description pointing at `list_sponsors` so Claude knows where to find ids. [src/lib/agent/register-mcp-tools.ts](src/lib/agent/register-mcp-tools.ts) Zod schemas + descriptions updated. Package bumped 0.3.4 → 0.3.5 (MCP cache-invalidation hint). **CSV import** ([src/app/api/events/[eventId]/import/registrations/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/import/registrations/route.ts)) gains three optional columns: `registrationStatus`, `paymentStatus`, `sponsor`. The first two are whitelist-validated against admin-settable subsets. `sponsor` is **resolved by name** (case-insensitive, whitespace-trimmed) against `Event.settings.sponsors[]` — ambiguous matches (two sponsors with the same name) are rejected with a row-level error rather than silently picking one. Required only when `paymentStatus === INCLUSIVE`. Existing CSV templates still work unchanged because all three columns default to today's behavior when absent. The import dialog ([src/components/import/csv-import-dialog.tsx](src/components/import/csv-import-dialog.tsx)) updates its sample row + help text to surface the new columns. **Detail sheet UI** ([src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/registrations/registration-detail-sheet.tsx](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/registration-detail-sheet.tsx)): payment-status dropdown gains "Inclusive"; selecting it without a sponsor first emits a client-side toast (avoids a confusing 400 round-trip). A sponsor-picker Select appears in the edit area when the row is INCLUSIVE, populated from `useSponsors(eventId)`. The Payment Summary card renders a violet "Sponsored by: Abbott" pill whenever `sponsorId` is set — even if status is no longer INCLUSIVE, since the attribution is preserved. **Workflow prerequisite**: organizer must add the sponsor on `/events/[id]/sponsors` *before* tagging registrations — empty-state UI surfaces a hint with a deep link. **Tests** ([__tests__/services/registration-service.test.ts](__tests__/services/registration-service.test.ts)): 5 new — INCLUSIVE without sponsorId → 400, INCLUSIVE with bad sponsorId → 400 with availableSponsors, happy path persists + skips email + audits, sponsorId orphan rejection on non-INCLUSIVE rows, default path unaffected. Suite 1146 → 1151. Verification: tsc + lint + build clean.

- **Manual payment capture for onsite/offline scenarios (April 29, 2026)** — Admin-driven flow to record payments that bypass Stripe — for onsite events (cash/card-on-site) and bank transfers where the registrant pays via wire and the organizer reconciles after the fact. New `POST /api/events/[eventId]/registrations/[registrationId]/payments` route ([src/app/api/events/[eventId]/registrations/[registrationId]/payments/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/%5BregistrationId%5D/payments/route.ts), ~400 LOC) accepts three methods: `bank_transfer` (organizer captures bank reference + uploaded proof URL), `card_onsite` (card brand + last-4 digits), `cash` (receiver name). Each path is Zod-validated with method-specific required-field refinements. **NOTE (corrected July 7, 2026):** there is **no dedicated "receipt number" field** for card-onsite or cash — the Zod schema captures only `bankReference`/`proofUrl` (transfer), `cardBrand`/`cardLast4` (card-onsite), and `cashReceivedBy` (cash). The invoice/receipt "Reference" line is derived from these (bank ref / `"Card ending NNNN"` / `"Cash — received by …"`). An earlier version of this note claimed a "receipt number" was captured for card/cash — that was never implemented (doc drift, now fixed). Inside one `$transaction`: re-reads the registration with `_count.payments` (race-safe precondition — paid registrations with at least one Payment row are 409'd; the recovery path allows manual capture for PAID-but-no-payments registrations that pre-date the migration), creates the `Payment` row with method + reference + receiptUrl + metadata JSON, flips `Registration.paymentStatus` to `PAID`, and fire-and-forget calls `createPaidInvoice` so the organizer gets the same INVOICE-status-PAID PDF + email Stripe registrants receive. UI: new `RecordPaymentDialog` ([src/components/payments/record-payment-dialog.tsx](src/components/payments/record-payment-dialog.tsx)) opens from the registration detail sheet's Billing & Payments tab — method selector with conditional fields (bank-transfer reveals reference + proof URL; card-onsite reveals card brand + last-4; cash reveals receiver name), amount + currency dropdown (12 supported currencies with USD default), notes, optional metadata. Wider on desktop (`sm:max-w-3xl`) per organizer feedback. Tests: 18 new in [__tests__/api/manual-payment-route.test.ts](__tests__/api/manual-payment-route.test.ts) covering all three methods, auth (401/403), Zod validation, race conditions (concurrent flip 409, payment-row-slips-in 409), recovery path (PAID-but-no-payments allows recording), invoice failure isolation. Suite 1126 → 1146. Commits: `0aab3cb` (feature), `a1d67cb` (UI tweaks + recovery path).

- **Default dev port → 3113 (April 29, 2026)** — Per organizer preference (and to stop colliding with miscellaneous services on 3000). - **MCP OAuth: per-client `rateLimitTier` for claude.ai web (April 28, 2026)** — Mirror of the API-key tier model on `McpOAuthClient`. claude.ai web (and any DCR client) registers a row when the user adds the integration; SUPER_ADMIN flips that row to INTERNAL afterwards, and every token minted from that DCR registration bypasses the MCP 100/hr cap. Two-step by design — can't tag a `client_id` that doesn't exist yet. Scope is per-DCR-registration so a leaked grant on someone else's claude.ai account stays NORMAL. Schema: reuses the `ApiKeyRateLimitTier` enum so OAuth + API-key tiers stay aligned. New routes: `GET /api/organization/oauth-clients` (org-scoped, ADMIN+, aggregated per-client with token count + lastUsedAt) and `PATCH /api/organization/oauth-clients/[clientId]` (SUPER_ADMIN-only, with org-ownership check so a SUPER_ADMIN in org A can't flip clients registered for org B). [src/lib/mcp-oauth.ts](src/lib/mcp-oauth.ts) `validateOAuthAccessToken()` joins `client.rateLimitTier` in the same query and returns it. [src/app/api/mcp/route.ts](src/app/api/mcp/route.ts) OAuth path now reads tier from the validator (was hard-coded NORMAL). UI: `OAuthClientsCard` rendered below `ApiKeysCard` in Settings → API Keys tab; SUPER_ADMIN sees a Switch toggle per row. Tests: 15 new (validator tier propagation + PATCH RBAC matrix). Migration `20260428100000_add_mcp_oauth_client_rate_limit_tier`. Commit `e27d64c`.

- **MCP/agent: log validation-error tool returns at warn level (April 28, 2026)** — MCP tools follow the convention of returning `{ error, code? }` for validation failures rather than throwing — the caller gets a structured error in the tool result, not a transport-level failure. The `runTool()` / agent-execute wrappers used to log every call as info regardless, which silenced ~345 validation-failure paths across 13 domain files. Both wrappers now inspect the result: if it has an `error` property, log warn with the message + code + duration; otherwise log info. Centralized fix — no per-tool changes needed. [src/lib/agent/register-mcp-tools.ts](src/lib/agent/register-mcp-tools.ts) covers MCP HTTP transport; [src/app/api/events/[eventId]/agent/execute/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/agent/execute/route.ts) covers the in-app agent. Per the "every failure path must log" rule. Commit `3a7b8ad`.

- **MCP: per-key `rateLimitTier` — INTERNAL bypasses 100/hr cap (April 28, 2026)** — Wave-3 verification scenarios + trusted internal automation were hitting the global 100/hr MCP rate limit at [src/app/api/mcp/route.ts:83](src/app/api/mcp/route.ts#L83). Added a per-key tier (`NORMAL` / `INTERNAL`) on `ApiKey`, SUPER_ADMIN-only to issue INTERNAL, every internal-key request logs `mcp:internal-key-used` so a leaked key surfaces in `/logs`. OAuth tokens originally hard-coded as NORMAL (claude.ai web couldn't bypass) — superseded by the per-client tier landed alongside in commit `e27d64c`. Migration `20260427120000_add_apikey_rate_limit_tier` adds the `ApiKeyRateLimitTier` enum + column (additive, no backfill). [src/lib/api-key.ts](src/lib/api-key.ts) `validateApiKey()` now returns `{ organizationId, rateLimitTier }`. UI: SUPER_ADMIN-only Switch in the API key creation dialog inside an amber-bordered warning panel + INTERNAL badge in the keys table. Tests: 13 new cases / 21 individual checks (validator propagation + POST RBAC matrix — ADMIN can issue NORMAL, ADMIN→INTERNAL is 403, SUPER_ADMIN→INTERNAL OK, default NORMAL, invalid tier 400). Suite 1098 → 1111. Commit `de6c702`.

- **Responsive email header/footer images + Tiptap → Media Library picker (April 28, 2026)** — Three gaps closed in one round per organizer ask: (1) New `Event.emailFooterImage` field parallel to the existing `emailHeaderImage` — organizer can now set a logo image at the very bottom of every email next to the existing footer-text block. Rendered between body and footer-text in source order. Migration `20260428000000_add_event_email_footer_image` (additive). Settings UI gets a new field next to the header image with the same preview pattern. (2) Header + footer + Tiptap-inserted body images all rendered with **Outlook-friendly** attribute set: `width="600"` HTML attribute (Outlook desktop reads this when CSS is ignored), `border="0"` (suppresses Outlook's blue link border), CSS `width: 100%; max-width: 600px; height: auto` (responsive on Apple Mail / Gmail / modern Outlook web), `align="center"` on parent `<td>` so Outlook doesn't float images left. New helper `responsiveImageBlock(src, alt)` in [src/lib/email.ts](src/lib/email.ts) generates the canonical block; new `normalizeBodyImages(html)` regex pass rewrites every `<img>` in the Tiptap body to the same attribute set, idempotent — overwrites any organizer-set width that would overflow the 600px body. (3) Tiptap "Insert Image" toolbar button replaced its `window.prompt("Enter image URL:")` with a proper Media Library picker dialog ([src/components/media/media-picker-dialog.tsx](src/components/media/media-picker-dialog.tsx), ~150 LOC) wrapping the existing org-scoped `/api/media` GET + POST — magic-byte validation, 2MB cap, auto-selects newly uploaded files. Dropped `allowBase64: true` from the Tiptap Image extension config to eliminate the data-URI clip risk (Gmail clips above 102KB). Tests: 13 new in [__tests__/lib/email-responsive.test.ts](__tests__/lib/email-responsive.test.ts) covering the responsive attribute set, idempotency of `normalizeBodyImages`, footer-image source order, attribute preservation. - **Add Speaker `photo:null` rejection + system-wide silent-400 logging sweep (April 27, 2026)** — User reported "Invalid input" on the Add Speaker form with no field name in the UI and no server log. Root cause: the form initialized `photo: null` but `createSpeakerSchema` accepted only `string | "" | undefined` — Zod rejected with a generic message that wasn't surfaced. The fix scope expanded into a system-wide hardening because the same silent-400 pattern appeared 44 other places. **Direct fix**: `createSpeakerSchema.photo` now accepts `.nullable()` (mirrors the update schema; `speaker-service` already normalizes null → null); `POST /speakers` emits `apiLogger.warn` with the flattened Zod errors so schema drift is visible in prod logs; the [Add Speaker page](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/speakers/new/page.tsx) now surfaces `data.details.fieldErrors` so the user sees WHICH field failed and `console.error` includes the full payload. **System-wide sweep — every silent 400 now logs**: User feedback "I do not like that there is no logs when something is not working, please logging is extremely important" was saved as feedback memory `feedback_always_log_failures.md` so future sessions honor the rule. New shared helper at [src/lib/api-errors.ts](src/lib/api-errors.ts): `zodErrorResponse()` + `apiErrorResponse()` — log + return the right NextResponse in one call. Programmatic migration: added `apiLogger.warn` before every previously-silent `"Invalid input"` 400 across **44 sites in 43 route files** (auth, organization, registrations, speakers, contacts, abstracts, events, tickets, hotels, accommodations, sessions, tracks, reviewers, scheduled emails, invoices, bulk-tags, bulk-type, profile, public/register, etc.). Coverage after sweep: **0 silent `"Invalid input"` paths remain** across `src/app/api/`. Verification: tsc clean, lint clean, full suite 1080/1080 passing. Commit `5aa92e5`.

- **Post-payment Invoice (not Receipt) + card details capture (April 24, 2026)** — Two tightly-related reworks driven by an organizer clarification: "Stripe should send the receipt, our system should send the invoice." (1) **Naming/semantic**: `createReceipt()` in [src/lib/invoice-service.ts](src/lib/invoice-service.ts) renamed to `createPaidInvoice()`. Emits `type: "INVOICE"` with `status: "PAID"` instead of `type: "RECEIPT"` — so the post-payment document shares the INVOICE numbering sequence with admin-issued pre-payment invoices. A temporary `export const createReceipt = createPaidInvoice` re-export keeps unmigrated callers compiling but is deprecated. Critical invariant: if an admin pre-created an INVOICE (status=SENT/DRAFT/OVERDUE) for this registration, `createPaidInvoice` **promotes it in place** inside the transaction (update → status=PAID + paidDate + paymentId + paymentMethod + paymentReference) rather than minting a second row with a fresh number. Fixes the "admin sent an invoice, then the registrant paid → two invoice numbers for one event" drift. Stripe webhook ([src/app/api/webhooks/stripe/route.ts](src/app/api/webhooks/stripe/route.ts)) now calls `createPaidInvoice` after `checkout.session.completed`. (2) **Schema**: four new nullable columns on `Payment` — `cardBrand`, `cardLast4`, `paymentMethodType`, `paidAt`. Migration `20260424000000_add_payment_card_details`. Legacy rows remain valid (all null). The webhook fetches the PaymentIntent's latest charge and pulls `payment_method_details.{type, card.brand, card.last4}` + `charge.created` (authoritative settlement timestamp — `createdAt` drifts under webhook retries). (3) **Invoice PDF**: new reusable `drawPaymentReceived()` helper in [src/lib/pdf/document-layout.ts](src/lib/pdf/document-layout.ts) renders a one-line "Payment Received" block on paid invoices — *"Paid on 24 Apr 2026 via Visa ending 4242"* with a second muted line for the Stripe PaymentIntent reference. Placed between the totals and the notes/bank section. Bank details are now suppressed on paid invoices (no transfer instructions needed after settlement). `InvoicePDFData` gains optional `paymentMethodType`/`cardBrand`/`cardLast4`/`paidAt`/`paymentReference` fields; `generatePDFForInvoice` + `sendInvoiceEmail` include the `payment` relation when loading so the data flows through. (4) **UI — Billing & Payments tab**: each payment row on the registration detail sheet now shows the instrument below the amount/date (*"via Visa ending 4242"* or *"via bank transfer"* for non-card methods), using `paidAt` as the date when available. A new "Download" row under Payment History surfaces the existing `InvoiceDownloadButtons` component whenever `paymentStatus === "PAID"` — same fallback logic as `/my-registration` (real Invoice → else Quote). (5) **Fallback safety**: `createPaidInvoice` passes `paidAt ?? new Date()` so when Stripe's charge lookup fails (rare), the Payment row still gets a non-null timestamp; the "Payment Received" block on the PDF is also gated on `isPaid && (paidAt || cardLast4 || paymentMethodType)` so a row with no captured instrument renders cleanly without the block. **Tests**: existing `createReceipt` suite in [__tests__/lib/invoice-service.test.ts](__tests__/lib/invoice-service.test.ts) renamed to `createPaidInvoice`, three cases — mint-fresh path with type=INVOICE/status=PAID assertions, paymentMethod=stripe default, and the new promote-existing-invoice path (explicit `mockFindFirst` returning a SENT invoice, assert `invoice.update` called and `invoice.create` NOT called). `setupTxMock` extended to default `tx.invoice.findFirst` to null so existing tests exercise the mint path. Full suite 1064/1064 (from 1063). Manual PDF smoke confirmed: paid invoice renders on 1 page with Payment Received block, reference line, and the existing PAID watermark. **Files touched**: [src/lib/invoice-service.ts](src/lib/invoice-service.ts), [src/lib/invoice-pdf.ts](src/lib/invoice-pdf.ts), [src/lib/pdf/document-layout.ts](src/lib/pdf/document-layout.ts), [src/app/api/webhooks/stripe/route.ts](src/app/api/webhooks/stripe/route.ts), [src/app/api/public/events/[slug]/register/route.ts](src/app/api/public/events/%5Bslug%5D/register/route.ts) (comment update), [src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/registrations/registration-detail-sheet.tsx](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/registration-detail-sheet.tsx), [src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/registrations/types.ts](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/types.ts), [prisma/schema.prisma](prisma/schema.prisma), new migration `20260424000000_add_payment_card_details`.

- **Inline speaker-agreement HTML → PDF attachment (April 24, 2026)** — Speaker-agreement emails now attach a personalized PDF rendered from the event's existing inline `Event.speakerAgreementHtml` (already edited in Event → Content → Speaker Agreement via Tiptap), alongside the existing `.docx` upload path. **Precedence**: `.docx` uploaded → `.docx` attachment (existing behavior preserved); else → PDF from inline HTML (new default); else → 400 pointing at both paths. **No new deps** — pure pdfkit (already in project) plus a hand-rolled HTML tokenizer + block parser + renderer at [src/lib/speaker-agreement.ts](src/lib/speaker-agreement.ts) ~1000 lines. Deliberately did NOT add `pdfmake` / `html-to-pdfmake` / `jsdom` — hand-rolled is testable in isolation and avoids Chromium/font-shipping concerns. **Supported HTML** (Tiptap subset + common Word-paste): `<p> <h1>..<h6> <ul> <ol> <li> <strong>/<b> <em>/<i> <u> <a href> <br> <hr> <blockquote> <div> <span> <table> <tbody> <thead> <tr> <td> <th>`. Unknown tags flatten to inner text. **Tables** render as a grid with header background, padded cells, vertical dividers, and page-break when a row doesn't fit — exercised against the MMG Invited Faculty Participation Agreement template's 7-row parties table + 5-row benefits table. **`<blockquote>`** renders as a callout (amber left border + tinted background) matching the `IMPORTANT — …` pattern used in that template. **Acceptance-page parity**: `GET /api/public/events/[slug]/speaker-agreement` now token-merges the HTML before returning; `POST …/accept` snapshots the merged HTML into `Speaker.agreementTextSnapshot`. The email attachment and the acceptance page render identical text for a given speaker (same `buildSpeakerEmailContext` + `mergeAgreementHtml`). **Hardening from independent review**: (1) `<a href>` scheme whitelist — `http`, `https`, `mailto`, `tel`, relative `/`/`#` only. `javascript:` / `data:` / `file:` / `vbscript:` render as plain underlined text with no link annotation, defusing pasted phishing URLs. (2) Defensive Unicode sweep — Helvetica's WinAnsi encoder throws on unencodable codepoints, so a stray emoji / CJK / box-drawing char would otherwise kill the whole batch; anything outside printable ASCII + Latin-1 Supplement + a few known-safe WinAnsi-mapped points (`—` `–` `•` `€` `™`) becomes `?`. Targeted substitutions for `☐ ☑ ☒ → ← ≤ ≥ ≈ × ÷ … † ‡` plus smart quotes, NBSP, non-WinAnsi dashes. (3) Named HTML entity decoder expanded from 6 to 26 common Word/web paste entities (`&copy; &mdash; &hellip; &ldquo; &rdquo;` etc.). (4) `<p>` inside `<li>` or `<td>` is transparent — Tiptap's default bullet-list extension emits `<li><p>text</p></li>`, so without this every bullet list was rendering as empty bullets + orphan paragraphs. (5) List-item renderer records baseline Y before drawing the marker — was previously positioning runs at `doc.y - BODY*LINE_HEIGHT` against a pen that `lineBreak:false` hadn't advanced, causing text to render ABOVE the marker. (6) `<br>` preserves line break — whitespace-collapse pass now has an opt-in `preserveNewlines` flag for explicit `\n` from `<br>`. **Tests**: 26 unit tests in [__tests__/lib/speaker-agreement-pdf.test.ts](__tests__/lib/speaker-agreement-pdf.test.ts) covering parser (tokenization, entity decoding), token merge (injection escape, unknown-token preservation, whitespace tolerance), every block type (paragraph, heading, list-item both ordered + unordered, table with/without tbody, cell header detection, blockquote→callout, hr rule), every hardening fix (`<li><p>`, `<td><p>`, `<br>` preservation, entity expansion, unknown entity pass-through, javascript:/data: stripping, safe-scheme preservation, relative-path preservation). Full suite 1063/1063 passing. Review-agent independent pass found 1 blocker + 3 high + 6 medium — B1 turned out to be intentional and documented (token merge is symmetric between PDF and acceptance page), all other findings fixed. **Files**: [src/lib/speaker-agreement.ts](src/lib/speaker-agreement.ts) (tokenizer/parser/renderer/PDF generator/merge helpers/href sanitizer/Unicode sweep, all new in this feature), [src/lib/bulk-email.ts](src/lib/bulk-email.ts) (precedence wiring + per-recipient PDF generation alongside the .docx path), [src/app/api/public/events/[slug]/speaker-agreement/route.ts](src/app/api/public/events/%5Bslug%5D/speaker-agreement/route.ts) (token-merge on GET + snapshot on POST), [src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/content/page.tsx](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/content/page.tsx) (collapsible merge-token reference), [src/components/events/speaker-agreement-template-card.tsx](src/components/events/speaker-agreement-template-card.tsx) (precedence explained in card description). Single-send route (`POST /api/events/[id]/speakers/[sid]/email`) has the same precedence wiring as bulk but committed separately via the parallel email-change feature's commit. Commits: `518320f` (HTML→PDF path), `a4413dc` (tables + callouts + checkbox fallback), `9ffddfd` (review fixes — list rendering / `<p>`-in-`<li>` / unicode / href whitelist / entity decoder / `<br>` preservation).

- **Email immutability + dedicated Change Email flow (April 24, 2026)** — Organizer-reported identity-drift bug: the inline email input on the Speaker detail sheet (and a latent equivalent on Contact PUT) updated only the entity row and left linked `User.email` + org `Contact` rows stale, silently splitting canonical identity across three tables. Fix is **Option A** — make email immutable via the general-purpose PUT paths and add three dedicated PATCH routes that do the full cascade atomically. **Locked PUT schemas**: [src/app/api/events/[eventId]/speakers/[speakerId]/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/speakers/%5BspeakerId%5D/route.ts), [src/app/api/events/[eventId]/registrations/[registrationId]/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/%5BregistrationId%5D/route.ts), and [src/app/api/contacts/[contactId]/route.ts](src/app/api/contacts/%5BcontactId%5D/route.ts) all reject `email` in the body with a 400 + `EMAIL_IMMUTABLE` code + a pointer to the dedicated PATCH endpoint — explicit, not silent-strip, so clients see the intended redirect. Dead email-uniqueness branches in the Speaker and Contact PUT handlers were removed along with `data.email` references that became unreachable once the Zod schema dropped the field. **Three new PATCH routes** share a small helper module at [src/lib/email-change.ts](src/lib/email-change.ts): `normalizeEmail()` (trim + lowercase + Zod-validate) and `repointOrgContactEmail(tx, …)` (returns `"updated" | "merged" | "none"` — when a Contact at the target email already exists in the org, the old Contact is deleted as a silent merge since the organizer already has a canonical row at the destination). **`PATCH /api/events/[eventId]/speakers/[speakerId]/email`** checks `Speaker.(eventId, email)` and `User.email` (global unique); cascades to `User.email` when `speaker.userId` is set; re-points Contact. Also emits an info-level `apiLogger.warn` when an unlinked speaker moves to an email that shadows an existing unrelated User row — a future register-to-account link flow would surface P2002 there, so the audit trail flags it up front (non-blocking). **`PATCH /api/events/[eventId]/registrations/[registrationId]/email`** is the most subtle of the three: `Attendee` rows can be shared across multiple registrations per schema (public-register's orphan-attendee reuse path produces this), so mutating `Attendee.email` in place would silently change email on sibling registrations. The route counts siblings inside the `$transaction` and **clones the Attendee row** (re-pointing this registration to the clone) when siblings exist, leaving the original untouched. The sibling-count read is inside the tx for consistency with the write. Cascades `User.email` when `registration.userId` is set. Response includes `attendeeCloned: true` so the caller can surface the info. **`PATCH /api/contacts/[contactId]/email`** is deliberately narrower — it updates the Contact row only and does NOT cascade to Speaker / User / Registration. Contact is a CRM snapshot, and propagating from there would re-introduce exactly the identity drift this feature prevents; the UI's contact-mode hint spells this out to the organizer. Org-scoped via `getOrgContext` (session or API key) because contacts aren't event-scoped. **Error codes** surfaced across the three routes: `INVALID_EMAIL` 400, `NO_CHANGE` 400, `EMAIL_IMMUTABLE` 400 (from the locked PUT paths), `SPEAKER_EMAIL_TAKEN` 409, `USER_EMAIL_TAKEN` 409, `CONTACT_EMAIL_TAKEN` 409, `EMAIL_TAKEN` 409 (P2002 race fallback between the pre-tx collision check and the transaction commit). **Rate limits**: Speaker + Registration share `email-change:${session.user.id}` at 30/hr (same user, same operation class); Contact uses a separate `contact-email-change:org:${organizationId}` 30/hr bucket because contact edits commonly arrive from API-key callers where `userId` is null. **UI**: new shared [src/components/change-email-dialog.tsx](src/components/change-email-dialog.tsx) (new-email + confirm-email inputs, current-email readout, contact-mode hint). Speaker / Registration / Contact detail sheets now render the email field as disabled read-only plus a "Change" button that opens the dialog; Speaker's save handler also strips `email` from the PUT payload as a defense-in-depth measure even though the server would reject it. Toast branches on `userCascaded`, `contactAction`, and `attendeeCloned` fields from the PATCH response. **Tests (29 new)**: [__tests__/lib/email-change.test.ts](__tests__/lib/email-change.test.ts) covers `normalizeEmail` edge cases + `repointOrgContactEmail` update/merge/none paths (6 tests); [__tests__/api/change-email-routes.test.ts](__tests__/api/change-email-routes.test.ts) covers all three routes end-to-end — every error code, the shared-Attendee clone path with sibling-count=1, the shadow-User warn path for unlinked speakers, user-cascade happy path, auth guards, and rate-limit 429 (23 tests). Verification: tsc clean, lint clean, `npm run build` clean, full vitest suite 1055/1055 (from 1048 pre-feature), independent review-agent checkpoint passed with both blockers addressed (B1 shared-Attendee clone + B2 shadow-User warn). E2E deferred — same seeded-test-DB environment limitation flagged earlier in the week. Shipped in commit `5da24e6`.

- **Services layer — Phase 2c registration-service extracted (April 23, 2026)** — Fourth and final Phase-2 extraction. [src/services/registration-service.ts](src/services/registration-service.ts) with `createRegistration()` now backs both REST admin POST `/api/events/[eventId]/registrations` and MCP `create_registration`. Originally planned to defer into Phase 3 (external-API-driven), but moved forward because Phase 0's in-place MCP patches had already aligned the two callers — making this extraction a low-risk consolidation rather than a new alignment. Scope is single-create only; public register (Stripe checkout + REGISTRANT account + orphan-attendee reuse + invoice auto-create) and MCP bulk (per-row error capture) are intentionally left inline due to divergent concerns. 9 finite-union error codes (EVENT_NOT_FOUND, TICKET_TYPE_NOT_FOUND, SALES_NOT_STARTED, SALES_ENDED, SOLD_OUT, PRICING_TIER_NOT_FOUND, ALREADY_REGISTERED with `meta.existingRegistrationId`, INVALID_PAYMENT_STATUS, UNKNOWN). Owns: atomic tx with typed `RegistrationServiceSentinel` class for discrimination (duplicate check inside tx is race-safer than pre-migration MCP's pre-tx check), soldCount `updateMany` guard, empty-string → null normalization on all optional attendee fields (photo, tags, dietaryReqs, customFields, bio, etc.) as last line of defense for direct-to-service callers, paymentStatus defaulting (UNASSIGNED for paid / COMPLIMENTARY for free or no-ticket), and the Phase 0 confirmation-email gate (paid + `finalPaymentStatus ∈ {UNASSIGNED, UNPAID, PENDING}`) — the specific drift bug that motivated the entire refactor is now structurally prevented since MCP has NO direct `sendRegistrationConfirmation` import, the email fan-out is service-owned end-to-end. Route reduced ~290 → ~45 lines; MCP executor ~265 → ~85 lines (rename to `createRegistrationTool` avoids shadowing). 34 new unit tests covering all 9 error codes, SOLD_OUT race, email-normalization parity between dup-check + attendee create, 5 confirmation-email gating cases, audit-source variants (rest with ip / mcp without), admin-message variants (actor name / organizer fallback / via MCP), side-effect isolation. Phase 0 parity tests at [__tests__/lib/agent-mcp-parity.test.ts](__tests__/lib/agent-mcp-parity.test.ts) got tx-proxy gain of `registration.findFirst` (duplicate check moved inside tx) and `registration.create` mock fixture expanded to include the full `{ attendee, ticketType }` relations the service's `include` returns. Backward compat: REST 201 body unchanged (same include tree), all status codes per error preserved, MCP response shape preserved via explicit reshape, auto-pivot hints preserved, audit log payload aligned to slim MCP-style `{ source, ticketTypeId, paymentStatus, status, ip? }` per Phase 1/2a/2b convention. Commit `aac0381`. Verification: tsc + lint clean, 1000/1000 tests (was 963), independent review-agent SAFE TO PROCEED with 45/45 checklist items verified. e2e note: existing `e2e/manual-registration.spec.ts` has a pre-existing login regression (verified identical on HEAD~, not introduced by Phase 2c); filed separately. Phase 2 is now complete; Phase 3 (external public REST API) is the next forcing function.

- **Invoice auto-generation + confirmation-number UX polish (April 22, 2026)** — Multi-part production-bug sweep after paid-registration testing. **(1) Receipt PDF attachment email now fires** — [src/lib/invoice-service.ts](src/lib/invoice-service.ts) `createInvoice` / `createReceipt` / `createCreditNote` used to throw `"Event code is required"` when `event.code` was null, which got swallowed by the Stripe webhook's fire-and-forget catch → no Invoice row was ever written → `sendInvoiceEmail` never ran → registrants only received Stripe's own receipt email, never ours with the PDF attached. Fix: new `resolveEventCode(event, ctx)` helper prefers `event.code`, falls back to the **shared** `deriveEventCode()` in [src/lib/utils.ts](src/lib/utils.ts) — the same deterministic helper that `POST /api/events` + MCP `create_event` already use to auto-populate `event.code` on new events. Fire-and-forget backfill writes the derived code to `event.code` on first use (`updateMany where code IS NULL`) so subsequent invoices read the stable prefix. Idempotent under webhook retries. **(2) "Invoice" button relabeled** — [src/components/invoices/invoice-download-buttons.tsx](src/components/invoices/invoice-download-buttons.tsx) when no Invoice/Receipt row exists, the fallback now says "Download Quote" instead of the misleading "Invoice" label (which was also the root cause of users getting `quote.json` downloaded when /quote served a JSON error). **(3) Confirmation-number terminology** — three registrant-facing emails (`registration-confirmation`, `payment-confirmation`, `refund-confirmation`) no longer all say "Confirmation Number" with different values (short serial vs full cuid). Now all say **"Registration #"** with the same padded serialId (e.g. `002`) across registration → payment → refund. Payment-confirmation email adds a distinct **"Payment Reference"** row with the Stripe PaymentIntent id for reconciliation. Stripe webhook threads `serialId` + `paymentIntentId` into `sendPaymentConfirmationEmail`; refund route threads `serialId` too. **(4) Quote PDF right-side box widened** — [src/lib/pdf/document-layout.ts](src/lib/pdf/document-layout.ts) `drawInfoBoxes` from 38% → 48% of page width (label col 45% → 38%, value col 50% → 60% of the right box), `lineBreak: false` on values. Fix applies to **all four PDF types** (Quote, Invoice, Receipt, Credit Note) because they share the layout helpers — billing emails like `vivek@meetingmindsdubai.com` no longer wrap + collide with the phone row below. Commits: `bb1dad0` (labels + PDF widening) and `ced1a18` (invoice auto-gen fix + UI relabel).

- **Services layer — Phase 2a + 2b shipped; Phase 2c deferred to external API (April 22, 2026)** — Phase 2 of the services refactor continued from the April 22 morning's Phase 1 landing. **Phase 2a (`761ec7a`)** extracted [src/services/abstract-service.ts](src/services/abstract-service.ts) with `changeAbstractStatus()`. Scope: status transitions only (UNDER_REVIEW / ACCEPTED / REJECTED / REVISION_REQUESTED / WITHDRAWN) — field updates on an abstract stay in the REST PUT handler since they aren't called from MCP and have no drift risk. Centralizes the `requiredReviewCount` gate (with `forceStatus` admin bypass logged as `source: "chair-override"`), WITHDRAWN terminal-state guard (intentional tightening of the REST path — previously only MCP enforced this), DB update with `reviewedAt` bookkeeping, fire-and-forget audit log, `refreshEventStats`, and awaited `notifyAbstractStatusChange` with isolated try/catch so callers receive `notificationStatus: "sent" | "failed" | "skipped"`. Reuses the existing `abstract-review.ts` + `abstract-notifications.ts` helpers.
