REST PUT reduced by splitting the review+WITHDRAWN branch (delegates to service) from the DRAFT→SUBMITTED + field-only branch (inline). 24 unit tests covering all 5 error codes, WITHDRAWN idempotent no-op, chair-override bypass, UNDER_REVIEW / REVISION_REQUESTED not gated, no-op ACCEPTED→ACCEPTED skips notification, notification failure isolation, `action: "UPDATE"` (not "REVIEW") on WITHDRAWN. **Phase 2b (`7381b65`)** extracted [src/services/speaker-service.ts](src/services/speaker-service.ts) with `createSpeaker()`. Both REST POST `/api/events/[eventId]/speakers` and MCP `create_speaker` delegate. Scope: single-create only — bulk paths (`MCP create_speakers_bulk`, `/import-registrations`) use different mechanics and aren't a fit for a shared single-create service. Service normalizes empty-string optional fields to null as a safety net for future direct-to-service callers. 18 unit tests covering all 3 error codes (EVENT_NOT_FOUND, SPEAKER_ALREADY_EXISTS, UNKNOWN), P2002 race path, email trim+lowercase normalization, source-tagged audit variants, admin-message difference (rest vs mcp), side-effect isolation, audit/notify non-blocking, empty-string normalization. **Phase 2c (`registration-service.ts`) is intentionally deferred.** Phase 0's in-place patches already eliminated the confirmed drift bugs for create_registration; the extraction is better done **alongside the upcoming external public REST API** when that spec is concrete, so the service shape is informed by the third caller's real requirements (not guessed). That lands as Phase 3 of the refactor. Review-agent checkpoints passed **SAFE TO PROCEED** on both 2a and 2b with minor follow-ups all applied. Full test suite 963/963 as of the April 22 close; services layer now at **3 services** covering the operations that had real drift risk.

- **Services layer — Phase 0 bug fixes + Phase 1 extraction (April 22, 2026)** — The MCP write tools had been implementing the same operations as the REST admin-create routes separately, and the two paths had drifted. Most critical: paid registrations created via MCP silently skipped the confirmation email + quote PDF because the single-create executor didn't call `sendRegistrationConfirmation()`. That and related drift (admin notifications, audit logs, contact sync, atomic `soldCount` guard, `qrCode` generation, sales-window enforcement, default `paymentStatus`) are all real bugs, not theoretical. **Phase 0 (`989c5fd`)** patched the confirmed drift directly in the MCP tools — no architectural change — so bug fixes could ship without waiting for the refactor. [src/lib/agent/tools/registrations.ts](src/lib/agent/tools/registrations.ts) `create_registration` + `create_registrations_bulk` and [src/lib/agent/tools/speakers.ts](src/lib/agent/tools/speakers.ts) `create_speaker` + `create_speakers_bulk` now fire the same side-effect fan-out as REST. 18 new parity tests in [__tests__/lib/agent-mcp-parity.test.ts](__tests__/lib/agent-mcp-parity.test.ts) assert email gate (sent for outstanding paid, skipped for PAID/COMPLIMENTARY/free), paymentStatus defaults (UNASSIGNED for paid, COMPLIMENTARY for free), `requiresApproval` → PENDING, atomic `soldCount` with SOLD_OUT race, `qrCode` persisted, side-effect fan-out (`syncToContact` + audit + `notifyEventAdmins` + `refreshEventStats`), sales-window validation, and CANCELLED exclusion in duplicate check. **Phase 1 (`5c6ff8e`)** created a new top-level `src/services/` directory and extracted the first service: [src/services/accommodation-service.ts](src/services/accommodation-service.ts). Both [src/app/api/events/[eventId]/accommodations/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/accommodations/route.ts) POST and [src/lib/agent/tools/accommodations.ts](src/lib/agent/tools/accommodations.ts) `create_accommodation` migrated to call the service, which centralizes the atomic overbooking guard that was previously duplicated. Route handler trimmed from ~210 → ~70 lines; MCP tool from ~153 → ~80 lines. **Conventions locked in** via [src/services/README.md](src/services/README.md): (a) errors-as-values result shape `{ ok: true, <domain-key>, ...derived } | { ok: false, code, message, meta? }` so the TS compiler forces callers to narrow on `result.ok`; (b) already-typed input — service takes `Date`, callers parse at their boundary; (c) caller identity via `source: "rest" | "mcp" | "api"` written into `AuditLog.changes.source`; (d) service owns the transaction + all side effects (email/audit/sync/notify), callers only handle auth, Zod, rate limits, HTTP/MCP response shaping; (e) services never import `next/server` — if they knew about HTTP, non-HTTP callers (cron, future external APIs) couldn't use them. 20 new unit tests in [__tests__/services/accommodation-service.test.ts](__tests__/services/accommodation-service.test.ts) cover all 11 error codes + audit-log source tagging + non-blocking audit failure. Verified clean: `tsc`, `lint`, 920/920 tests, independent review-agent checkpoint. **Phase 2 (next)** will extract `registration-service.ts` (3 callers, biggest win), `speaker-service.ts` (3 callers), `abstract-service.ts` (partial — notifications + review aggregates already extracted). **Phase 3** is driven by the external API surface when it ships. **Phase 4** is opportunistic — extract only when touching a route for a feature reason. The architecture rationale is in [docs/HANDOVER.md](docs/HANDOVER.md) §2.5 and [docs/ARCHITECTURE.md](docs/ARCHITECTURE.md) "Services Layer — In Progress"; full changelog in [CHANGELOG.md](CHANGELOG.md). One subtle design note: the Phase 1 extraction also tightened two behaviors — (i) the REST accommodation POST previously had a redundant pre-transaction `bookedRooms >= totalRooms` check that's gone now (the in-tx re-check is strictly safer, no stale-read race window), and (ii) `AuditLog.changes` for accommodation creates is now the slim MCP-style summary `{ source, registrationId, speakerId, roomTypeId, nights, ip? }` instead of the full accommodation JSON (aligns both callers on one shape; the entity is still retrievable via `entityId`).

- **Payment status UNASSIGNED + per-person email history + admin-create quote email (April 2026)** — Multi-strand round delivered together. **(1) `PaymentStatus.UNASSIGNED`** added to the Prisma enum for admin-created registrations where payment is intentionally pending (distinct from `UNPAID`, which implies the registrant self-registered and owes via Stripe). Migration `20260421000000_add_unassigned_payment_status`, with idempotent corrective migration `20260421120000_reapply_unassigned_and_email_log` to re-apply it + `EmailLog` (some prod deploys reported "No pending migrations" without running the SQL — corrective uses `ADD VALUE IF NOT EXISTS` + `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS` + `DO $$...$$` guards around FKs). **(2) Admin-settable Payment Status dropdown** exposed on both the Add Registration dialog and the full-page `/events/[eventId]/registrations/new`, with the dropdown sitting next to Registration Type in a 2-column grid. Manual subset: `UNASSIGNED` / `UNPAID` / `PAID` / `COMPLIMENTARY`; Stripe-driven states (`PENDING` / `REFUNDED` / `FAILED`) excluded — webhook owns those. Default: `UNASSIGNED` for paid tickets, `COMPLIMENTARY` for free. **(3) Enum-driven registration enums consolidation** — new [src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/registrations/registration-enums.ts](src/app/(dashboard)/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/registration-enums.ts) is the single source of truth for both PaymentStatus and RegistrationStatus dropdowns: imports Prisma's generated enum (compile-time static, zero DB cost) and exports exhaustive `Record<PaymentStatus, string>` label + colour maps (TS fails the build if a new enum value lacks a label/colour), plus `DISPLAY_ORDER` arrays guarded by a module-init `assertCovers()` runtime check. Detail-sheet edit dropdowns, list filter, Add Registration dialog, and full-page create all map over the enum — no more hardcoded `<SelectItem>` drift. `Registration.status` / `paymentStatus` typed as Prisma enum (were `string`). Four stale Zod schemas (PATCH route + three MCP tools in `register-mcp-tools.ts`) flipped to `z.nativeEnum(PaymentStatus)` / `z.nativeEnum(RegistrationStatus)` — before, the detail-sheet "Unassigned" save silently failed Zod server-side. **(4) Events list click-to-sort** — Event and Date column headers cycle `name ↕ startDate ↕ createdAt` with asc/desc toggles reflected in `?sort=&order=` query params. Zod-validated parser in `src/lib/event-sort.ts`. **(5) Preflight "already registered" check on signup Step 1** — new `POST /api/public/events/[slug]/check-email` (20/hr/IP), non-enumerable `{ exists, reason }` response. Step-1 "Continue" on both `/e/[slug]/register/[category]` and `/e/[slug]/abstract/register` blocks advancement with an inline "Already registered — Sign in instead" banner; server-side duplicate check at final POST remains the race-safety net. **(6) Per-person email history** — new `EmailLog` Prisma model (fields: `to`, `cc`, `bcc`, `subject`, `templateSlug`, `provider`, `providerMessageId`, `status` `SENT`/`FAILED`, `errorMessage`, `entityType` `REGISTRATION`/`SPEAKER`/`CONTACT`/`USER`/`OTHER`, `entityId`, `organizationId`, `eventId`, `triggeredByUserId`, `createdAt`, indexes on `[entityType, entityId]` + `organizationId` + `eventId` + `to` + `createdAt`) written by a wrapper around `sendEmail()`. Read via `GET /api/email-logs?entityType=&entityId=` (admin-only via `denyReviewer`). Email History card renders at the bottom of the registration detail sheet, speaker detail sheet, and contact detail sheet. Migration `20260421000100_add_email_log`. **(7) Every `sendEmail()` call site now passes `logContext`** so each send produces a row linked to its entity: abstract confirmation → `SPEAKER`; submitter welcome → `SPEAKER` with post-txn id lookup; password reset / org invite / reviewer invite → `USER`; webinar panelist invite → `SPEAKER` if matched by `(eventId, email)` lookup, `OTHER` otherwise; MCP agent bulk email → per-recipient `SPEAKER`/`REGISTRATION`; public + admin confirmation emails → `REGISTRATION`. `sendEmail()` itself emits `apiLogger.warn("sendEmail called without logContext")` if a future caller forgets — the warning surfaces in stdout + `logs/app.log` + `docker logs`. Four silent `.catch(() => {})` swallows on notification + push-cleanup paths also converted to `apiLogger.warn`. **(8) Auto-send confirmation + quote PDF when admin manually creates an outstanding-payment registration** ([src/app/api/events/[eventId]/registrations/route.ts](src/app/api/events/%5BeventId%5D/registrations/route.ts)) — reproducer was "admin adds a registration with UNASSIGNED / UNPAID, registrant never gets a quote email". Public path already called `sendRegistrationConfirmation()` (which attaches the quote PDF when `price > 0 && organizationName`); admin path never did. Fix: after the transaction, if `paymentStatus ∈ {UNASSIGNED, UNPAID, PENDING}` AND `ticketType.price > 0`, fire-and-forget `sendRegistrationConfirmation(...)` with the full payload. Event `select` widened to carry the organization company block + tax/bank fields the PDF renderer needs. Skipped for `PAID` / `COMPLIMENTARY` (admin settled) and for `REFUNDED` / `FAILED` (admin can re-send manually from detail sheet). **(9) E2E coverage** — new [e2e/manual-registration.spec.ts](e2e/manual-registration.spec.ts) drives the full-page create flow end-to-end and verifies the `UNASSIGNED` badge lands on the list row. Fixed two pre-existing spec failures where `pickSelect(page, "Title", "Dr")` broke after `TitleSelect` labels gained trailing periods — both specs updated to `Dr.`. Full 7-spec suite green in ~20s.

- **Sprint B Tranche 2: bulk creates + update_contact + update_event MCP tools (April 2026)** — Four new MCP tools filling write-side gaps identified in the audit. **`create_speakers_bulk`** + **`create_registrations_bulk`** (event-scoped, writeTools) — take an array of up to 100 rows, pre-dedup by email within the payload, validate each row against the same rules as their single-create counterparts (email format, title enum, ticketTypeId belongs to event, manual-status whitelist), run per-row inside a try/catch, and return `{ createdCount, failedCount, created: [{index, id, ...}], errors: [{index, email, error, code}] }`. One bad row can't kill the batch. Single audit log row per bulk call (`entityId: "bulk:{createdCount}"`, `changes.bulk: true`) rather than N rows — the per-row detail stays in the response for the caller to act on. Error codes: `MISSING_FIELDS`, `INVALID_EMAIL`, `DUPLICATE_IN_BATCH`, `INVALID_TITLE`, `INVALID_TICKET_TYPE`, `INVALID_STATUS`, `ALREADY_EXISTS`, `ROW_FAILED`, `TOO_MANY_ROWS`. **`update_contact`** (org-level inline tool, mirrors `create_event` shape) — org-scoped via `ctx.organizationId`, accepts contactId + any subset of title/names/organization/jobTitle/bio/specialty/phone/photo/city/state/zipCode/country/notes/tags. Email is **intentionally immutable** (returns `EMAIL_IMMUTABLE`) because changing it would collide with the `(organizationId, email)` unique index and needs the dashboard merge flow to handle duplicates. Audit log entry is org-wide (no `eventId` — contacts aren't event-scoped). **`update_event`** (org-level inline tool, takes `eventId` as input) — safe-fields whitelist: `name`, `description`, `venue`, `address`, `city`, `country`, `tag`, `specialty`, `taxRate` (0-100), `taxLabel`, `bankDetails`, `badgeVerticalOffset` (−500 to 500). **Explicitly rejects** `slug`, `startDate`, `endDate`, `eventType`, `timezone`, `organizationId`, `id` with `FIELD_NOT_ALLOWED` and an error message explaining the cascade (public URLs / scheduled emails / Zoom provisioning / timezone math). Unknown fields get `UNKNOWN_FIELD`. The rejection is explicit-not-silent so the caller sees the exact field name and gets routed to the dashboard Settings page for those. Files: `src/lib/agent/event-tools.ts` (+4 executors, +~400 LOC around the bottom before TOOL_EXECUTOR_MAP), `src/lib/agent/mcp-server-builder.ts` (+2 event-scoped writeTools entries, +2 org-level inline `server.tool` registrations). Package bumped 0.3.0 → 0.3.1 (serverInfo.version cache-invalidation hint). No schema changes. No new deps. Stdio `src/mcp/server.ts` deliberately untouched — Tranche 3 will consolidate it.
- **Sprint B: per-reviewer abstract scoring + reviewer assignment (April 2026)** — Closed the last major audit item (April 15) by refactoring abstract review from a single row on `Abstract` to proper per-reviewer submissions. **Schema (no backfill — pre-prod)**: dropped `Abstract.reviewScore|reviewNotes|criteriaScores|recommendedFormat`; added `AbstractReviewer` (per-abstract assignment metadata — role PRIMARY/SECONDARY/CONSULTING, conflictFlag, assignedBy) and `AbstractReviewSubmission` (upserts on `(abstractId, reviewerUserId)` — criteriaScores JSON, overallScore 0-100, reviewNotes, recommendedFormat enum ORAL/POSTER/NEITHER, confidence 1-5). `AbstractReviewSubmission.abstractReviewerId` is nullable with SET NULL cascade so unassigning a reviewer preserves their submission. Migration `20260417000000_add_abstract_reviewers_and_scores`. **Per-event required review count**: new `event.settings.requiredReviewCount` (default 1) gates ACCEPTED/REJECTED transitions — error code `INSUFFICIENT_REVIEWS` surfaces `currentCount` + `required`. Admin `forceStatus: true` bypass is logged with `changes.source: "chair-override"`. **Shared aggregation helper** at `src/lib/abstract-review.ts`: `computeSubmissionAggregates(abstractId, tx?)` returns per-criterion + overall mean/min/max/count; `computeWeightedOverallScore(scores)` for auto-computing overall from criteria via event weights; `consolidateReviewNotes(submissions)` joins multi-reviewer notes for the speaker email; `readRequiredReviewCount(settings)`. **REST routes**: `POST /abstracts/[id]/reviewers` (idempotent — returns `alreadyAssigned` on dup), `DELETE /abstracts/[id]/reviewers/[userId]` (preserves submission), `GET+POST /abstracts/[id]/submissions` (POST upserts current user's submission, auth = reviewer pool OR explicit assignment OR admin). Existing `PUT /abstracts/[id]` now routes all review field updates to the submissions endpoint — status transitions only here, with the requiredReviewCount gate. **Speaker email** uses aggregated reviewer notes (`consolidateReviewNotes`) and mean overall score, not the old single-row fields. **MCP tools**: 4 new — `assign_reviewer_to_abstract`, `unassign_reviewer_from_abstract`, `submit_abstract_review`, `get_abstract_scores` — plus `update_abstract_status` rewritten to drop reviewNotes/reviewScore params and add `force` bool (chair-override). All executors in [src/lib/agent/event-tools.ts](src/lib/agent/event-tools.ts), registered in [src/lib/agent/mcp-server-builder.ts](src/lib/agent/mcp-server-builder.ts). `submit_abstract_review` reuses the same reviewer-pool-or-assignment auth check as the REST route. **Reviewer portal** at `/my-reviews` ([src/app/(dashboard)/my-reviews/page.tsx](src/app/(dashboard)/my-reviews/page.tsx)): lists all abstracts across every event where the current user is a reviewer (union of event-pool + explicit per-abstract assignments), groups by event, shows submission status badge (PENDING / NEEDS_UPDATE / SUBMITTED) — NEEDS_UPDATE fires when the abstract was updated after the reviewer's last submission. Backed by [src/app/api/my-reviews/route.ts](src/app/api/my-reviews/route.ts). Sidebar gets a "My Reviews" link for REVIEWER role only. **Dashboard UI**: abstract list card now shows `meanOverallScore` + `reviewCount` instead of single score. Abstract edit page fetches `/submissions` to render the reviewer-feedback card with joined notes + mean score. The review dialog lost all the per-criterion scoring inputs — reviewers now score from `/my-reviews → abstract page`, and admins from the dialog get a status picker + admin-only "force status" checkbox + an info panel explaining the new flow. **Failure handling**: every new route + executor has structured `try/catch` with `apiLogger.error`, error codes (INSUFFICIENT_REVIEWS, NOT_A_REVIEWER, ASSIGNMENT_NOT_FOUND, INVALID_CRITERION_ID…), fire-and-forget audit log `.catch()`, and isolated notification failure pattern (Sprint A A1 — email failure never masks DB success). Logging taxonomy: `abstract-reviewer:assigned|unassigned`, `abstract-submission:created|updated`, `abstract-status:insufficient-reviews|changed|chair-override`, `abstract-status:notification-failed`. **Tests**: `__tests__/lib/rbac.test.ts` + `__tests__/lib/abstract-lifecycle.test.ts` updated to reflect the new PUT schema (no review fields), new submission schema, new auth matrix (ORGANIZER + REVIEWER can set review statuses via PUT; force override is admin-only). 160/160 passing. No new deps. Stdio `src/mcp/server.ts` is intentionally NOT updated in this tranche — follow-up will consolidate stdio + HTTP tool registration into a shared `src/lib/agent/mcp-tool-registrations.ts`.
- **MCP tool expansion: create_event + orchestration + actions + recently-shipped features (April 2026)** — The MCP server grew from 35 → 57 tools across 4 tranches to close the gap between "what claude.ai can ask for" and "what EA-SYS can do". Motivation: with OAuth fixed (previous feature) claude.ai web finally connects, but then hits a wall — the tool surface was heavily biased toward read + create, missing the most common natural-language asks. **Tranche 0 (1 tool): `create_event`** — long-missing top-level CRUD. Org-scoped via API-key/OAuth `ctx.organizationId`, auto-generates unique slug with -1/-2/-3 collision retries (fails cleanly after 10 attempts rather than silently appending `Date.now()` like the old POST route), seeds `DEFAULT_REGISTRATION_TERMS_HTML` + `DEFAULT_SPEAKER_AGREEMENT_HTML`, fires `provisionWebinar()` fire-and-forget on `eventType === "WEBINAR"` for auto-provisioning anchor session + Zoom webinar + email sequence. Writes audit log with `source: "mcp"`. **Tranche A (5 tools) — orchestration reads**: `get_event_dashboard` (single call returning registration counts by status + payment, speaker counts + agreement signed/unsigned, session counts including upcoming/live now/past, check-in rate, recent 5 registrations, next upcoming session — replaces ~5-call sequences); `list_unpaid_registrations` (filters `paymentStatus IN (UNPAID, PENDING, FAILED)` AND `status != CANCELLED`, optional `daysPending` cutoff on age, sorted oldest-first with computed `daysSinceRegistration`); `list_speaker_agreements(filter: signed|unsigned|all)` (reads existing `Speaker.agreementAcceptedAt`); `list_live_sessions_now(withinMinutes?)` (sessions where now ∈ [startTime, endTime], optional lookahead window, includes linked Zoom join URL + passcode); `search_event(query, domains?)` (case-insensitive substring search across registrations/speakers/abstracts/contacts, returns grouped results with `{ domain, id, label, status }`). **Tranche B (4 tools) — state-change actions plugging read/create/write asymmetry**: `update_registration` (full shape mirror of REST PATCH — status, paymentStatus, ticketTypeId, attendee fields; auto-adjusts `TicketType.soldCount` on type change inside a transaction; post-update `syncToContact()`; `paymentStatus=REFUNDED` flips DB flag only, does NOT trigger Stripe refund); `update_speaker` (status + title/names/bio/org/jobTitle/phone/city/country/specialty/website/photo/tags; post-update `syncToContact()`); `update_session` (name/description/startTime/endTime/location/capacity/trackId/status, validates times fall within parent event's date range, rejects trackId from a different event); `bulk_update_registration_status(registrationIds: string[] max 200, { status?, paymentStatus? })` (single `updateMany` transaction scoped by `event.organizationId`). All write tools write audit logs with `source: "mcp"`. **Tranche C (12 tools) — recently-shipped features**: webinar reads (`get_webinar_info` — settings + anchor session + ZoomMeeting; `list_webinar_attendance` — KPIs + top-N rows with registered/attended/rate/avg watch time computed; `list_webinar_engagement` — polls + Q&A). Sponsors (`list_sponsors` grouped by tier; `upsert_sponsors` — replace-all semantics matching the existing PUT route, validates URL schemes rejecting `javascript:`/`data:`, server re-assigns `sortOrder` from array index). Speaker agreement template (`get_speaker_agreement_template` read-only — uploads stay dashboard-only because file uploads don't fit MCP's JSON-RPC transport). Promo codes full CRUD (`list_promo_codes`, `create_promo_code` with discountType PERCENTAGE/FIXED_AMOUNT, `update_promo_code`, `delete_promo_code` — **soft delete via `isActive: false`**, usage history preserved). Scheduled emails (`list_scheduled_emails`, `cancel_scheduled_email` — PENDING → CANCELLED flip; create tool deliberately omitted because recipient+filter+template shape doesn't fit a flat MCP signature cleanly). **Architecture**: all 22 executors live in [src/lib/agent/event-tools.ts](src/lib/agent/event-tools.ts) (shared with the in-app AI Agent at `/events/[id]/agent`), registered in `TOOL_EXECUTOR_MAP`. MCP HTTP registrations added to [src/lib/agent/mcp-server-builder.ts](src/lib/agent/mcp-server-builder.ts) — event-level tools go into the `readTools`/`writeTools` arrays (auto-injects `eventId` param and runs `getOrgIdSecure()` for cross-tenant safety); `create_event` registered as top-level inline tool like `list_events` (no `eventId` because we're creating one). Existing org-scoping pattern: every executor either accepts `ctx.eventId` already verified by `getOrgIdSecure()`, or does its own `findFirst({ where: { id, event: { organizationId } } })` check before any write. Stdio transport at `src/mcp/server.ts` intentionally NOT updated — it's a separate 600-line registration layer that will be consolidated or deprecated in a follow-up PR (adding 22 more registrations there would double the drift problem). No schema changes. No new deps. Files: `src/lib/agent/event-tools.ts` (+22 executors), `src/lib/agent/mcp-server-builder.ts` (+22 registrations). Verified: `npx tsc --noEmit` + `npm run lint` clean.
- **MCP OAuth 2.1 + DCR for claude.ai web (April 2026)** — Claude Desktop connects fine via `mcp-remote` (Node subprocess sets `x-api-key` header), but claude.ai web **could not connect at all** because browser-based MCP clients fundamentally require OAuth 2.1 with Dynamic Client Registration per the MCP spec — there is no UI in claude.ai to paste a raw API key. Root-cause investigation found three problems: (1) `GET /api/mcp` on 401 returned no `WWW-Authenticate` header so claude.ai couldn't discover the OAuth server, (2) `/.well-known/oauth-protected-resource` and `/.well-known/oauth-authorization-server` both 404'd, and (3) `OPTIONS /api/mcp` with `Origin: https://claude.ai` returned 204 with zero CORS headers so every browser preflight got blocked. Implemented full RFC 7591 DCR + RFC 8414 Authorization Server Metadata + RFC 9728 Protected Resource Metadata + RFC 6749 authorization code flow with **mandatory PKCE S256** (plain PKCE disallowed). **Schema**: three new Prisma models — `McpOAuthClient` (DCR registrations with `redirectUris: String[]`, `grantTypes`, `tokenEndpointAuthMethod` default `"none"` for public clients), `McpOAuthAuthCode` (hashed one-time-use codes with 10-min TTL + `codeChallenge` + `codeChallengeMethod`), `McpOAuthAccessToken` (hashed Bearer tokens with 30-day access TTL + 90-day refresh TTL + `lastUsedAt` + `revokedAt`). All lookups via SHA-256 hash — raw tokens never stored or logged, only first 10-12 chars of the token ever appear in logs. **Service lib** at `src/lib/mcp-oauth.ts` owns: `hashToken()`, `verifyPkce()` (timing-safe compare), `validateOAuthAccessToken()` (hot path, fire-and-forget `lastUsedAt` update), `issueAuthCode()`, `exchangeAuthCode()` (verifies PKCE + redirect_uri match + client_id match + expiry, deletes code row inside transaction), `exchangeRefreshToken()` (mints new access, rotates refresh inside transaction, revokes old row), `revokeToken()`, `registerClient()`, `getClient()`, `verifyClientSecret()`. **CORS helper** at `src/lib/mcp-cors.ts` exposes `handlePreflight()` and `withCors()` — allowed origins: `https://claude.ai`, `https://*.claude.ai`, `https://*.anthropic.com`, `https://console.anthropic.com`, plus `http://localhost:3000` in dev. **Routes**: `/.well-known/oauth-protected-resource` (resource metadata), `/.well-known/oauth-authorization-server` (endpoint discovery — points `authorization_endpoint` at `/mcp-authorize` page, not an API route), `/api/mcp/oauth/register` (DCR, 10/hr/IP rate limit, accepts any valid DCR request, defaults to public client with `token_endpoint_auth_method: "none"`), `/api/mcp/oauth/token` (accepts both `application/x-www-form-urlencoded` and JSON for Zod-compliant clients, handles `authorization_code` + `refresh_token` grants, returns RFC 6749 token response shape), `/api/mcp/oauth/authorize/decision` (POST from the consent form, re-validates server-side, issues code, 302s to registered `redirect_uri`), `/api/mcp/oauth/revoke` (RFC 7009, always 200 per spec). **Consent UI** at `/mcp-authorize` is a Next.js server-component page (outside the `(dashboard)` route group so no sidebar clutter) that validates OAuth params, checks NextAuth session, redirects to `/login?callbackUrl=...` if not authenticated, and enforces **RBAC**: only `ADMIN` / `SUPER_ADMIN` / `ORGANIZER` roles can grant MCP access — reviewers / submitters / registrants are blocked with a clear error page. Shows the client name + user's org name + scope, with Approve/Deny buttons that POST to the decision route. **Backward compatibility**: the existing `x-api-key` header path in `/api/mcp/route.ts` is untouched. The `authenticate()` function now tries `validateApiKey()` first (fast, pre-existing) and falls back to `validateOAuthAccessToken()` — both paths return the same `{ organizationId, keyPrefix }` shape so downstream MCP tools don't care which auth method was used. Claude Desktop + `mcp-remote` + n8n all continue to work unchanged. **Wire-up**: the `/api/mcp/route.ts` 401 response now includes `WWW-Authenticate: Bearer realm="mcp", resource_metadata="${base}/.well-known/oauth-protected-resource"` so spec-compliant clients bootstrap the OAuth flow automatically. Added an `OPTIONS` handler that delegates to `handlePreflight()`. Every 200/401/429/response wrapped with `withCors()`. **Middleware bypass**: `src/middleware.ts` previously intercepted all `OPTIONS /api/*` and returned 204 with a mobile-only CORS allowlist that didn't include claude.ai — broke everything. Added an early `if (pathname.startsWith("/api/mcp")) return NextResponse.next()` short-circuit so MCP routes handle their own CORS via route-level `OPTIONS` exports. **Cleanup cron** at `/api/cron/mcp-oauth-cleanup` (Bearer `$CRON_SECRET`, hourly) deletes expired auth codes and tokens past a 7-day grace period. Migration: `20260416000000_add_mcp_oauth_tables`. Files: `prisma/schema.prisma` (+3 models + 2 User relations), `src/lib/mcp-oauth.ts` (new), `src/lib/mcp-cors.ts` (new), `src/app/.well-known/oauth-protected-resource/route.ts` (new), `src/app/.well-known/oauth-authorization-server/route.ts` (new), `src/app/api/mcp/oauth/register/route.ts` (new), `src/app/api/mcp/oauth/token/route.ts` (new), `src/app/api/mcp/oauth/revoke/route.ts` (new), `src/app/api/mcp/oauth/authorize/decision/route.ts` (new), `src/app/mcp-authorize/page.tsx` (new), `src/app/api/cron/mcp-oauth-cleanup/route.ts` (new), `src/app/api/mcp/route.ts`, `src/middleware.ts`. EC2 crontab addition: `0 * * * * curl -s -X POST -H "Authorization: Bearer $CRON_SECRET" https://events.meetingmindsgroup.com/api/cron/mcp-oauth-cleanup`.
- **Speaker / Faculty communications upgrade (April 2026)** — Four-part overhaul of speaker outreach so faculty get professionally personalized invitations and agreements. **(1) Title prefix everywhere.** `Speaker.title` already existed but was silently dropped on every public surface and every speaker email. The dashboard speaker sheet/list/detail page already used `formatPersonName()` correctly; the gap was on `/e/[slug]/agenda`, `/e/[slug]/session/[sessionId]` (Session Details speakers list + speakers grid), the registration-page featured-speakers card, and the `speaker-invitation`/`speaker-agreement` email templates which only interpolated `{{firstName}}`/`{{lastName}}`. All public surfaces now call `formatPersonName(speaker.title, speaker.firstName, speaker.lastName)`, and the upstream public APIs (`/api/public/events/[slug]/agenda`, `/api/public/events/[slug]/sessions/[sessionId]/detail`) were extended to `select` the `title` field. **(2) Presentation details in speaker emails.** Speaker emails previously sent only a comma-joined list of session names with no topic title, no date/time, no track, no role. New helper `buildSpeakerEmailContext(eventId, speakerId)` in `src/lib/speaker-agreement.ts` queries `Speaker → SessionSpeaker → EventSession (with track)` AND `Speaker → TopicSpeaker → SessionTopic` in a single `Promise.all`, builds a pre-rendered HTML table block (Session / Topic / Date & Time / Track / Role) plus a plain-text variant, and surfaces them as `{{presentationDetails}}` / `{{presentationDetailsText}}` template vars. Same context object also drives merge fields for the .docx generator below — single source of truth so email greeting and document never disagree. **(3) Per-user organizer email signature.** New `User.emailSignature` field (Text, HTML). Edited from the existing `/profile` page via TiptapEditor (lazy-loaded). New `GET/PATCH /api/profile` endpoint scoped to `session.user.id` only — every authenticated user can edit their own signature regardless of role, no `denyReviewer` because it's a self-edit. The signature is loaded by both single-send (`/api/events/[eventId]/speakers/[speakerId]/email`) and bulk-send (`/api/events/[eventId]/emails/bulk`) routes from the triggering user, threaded through `executeBulkEmail` via new optional `BulkEmailInput.organizerSignature` field, and rendered into the email body via `{{organizerSignature}}` (passed in `rawHtmlKeys` so it isn't escaped). The cron worker (`/api/cron/scheduled-emails`) was extended to load `emailSignature` in its batch organizer fetch so scheduled sends carry the same signature as the original user's identity. **(4) Personalized speaker-agreement DOCX attachment.** New `Event.speakerAgreementTemplate Json?` field stores `{ url, filename, uploadedAt, uploadedBy }` pointer to an uploaded .docx template. Upload UI is a `SpeakerAgreementTemplateCard` panel under Event Settings → Email Branding tab, backed by `POST/GET/DELETE /api/events/[eventId]/speaker-agreement-template` (DOCX MIME validation + zip magic byte check `PK\x03\x04` + 2MB cap + 10/hr rate limit + path-traversal-guarded `public/uploads/agreements/{eventId}/{uuid}.docx` storage). New `generateSpeakerAgreementDocx({ eventId, speakerId })` in `src/lib/speaker-agreement.ts` uses `docxtemplater` v3 + `pizzip` (new deps, both pure JS, work on EC2 + Vercel) with `delimiters: { start: "{", end: "}" }` so single-brace `{token}` syntax doesn't collide with the email renderer's `\{\{(\w+)\}\}` regex. Mail-merge tokens: `{title}`, `{firstName}`, `{lastName}`, `{speakerName}`, `{speakerEmail}`, `{eventName}`, `{eventStartDate}`, `{eventEndDate}`, `{eventVenue}`, `{eventAddress}`, `{organizationName}`, `{sessionTitles}`, `{topicTitles}`, `{sessionDateTime}`, `{trackNames}`, `{role}`. Returns `null` when no template configured (caller surfaces 400 with helpful "upload a template first" message), throws on render errors. **Per-recipient bulk attachments.** `executeBulkEmail` previously sent the same static attachments to every recipient. Extended with a pre-flight guard (fail fast with 400 if `emailType === "agreement" && recipientType === "speakers"` and no template configured — before resolving recipients, so we don't half-process and stress rate limits), then in the per-recipient send loop calls `generateSpeakerAgreementDocx({ eventId, speakerId: recipient.id })` and merges with any static `attachments` before the `sendEmail()` call. Per-recipient errors are captured in `result.errors[]` so one bad speaker can't kill the batch. The same code path covers immediate sends (`/api/events/[eventId]/emails/bulk`) AND scheduled sends (`/api/cron/scheduled-emails`) — scheduled .docx are generated at fire time, not at scheduling time, so they always reflect the latest speaker/session data. The bulk audit log now reports `hasAttachments: true` for agreement bulk sends even when the static `attachments` array is empty. **Default email templates updated** (`src/lib/email.ts` lines 306-370): `speaker-invitation` and `speaker-agreement` now greet with `{{speakerName}}` (formatted prefix), embed `{{presentationDetails}}` block above `{{personalMessage}}`, and append `{{organizerSignature}}` above the branded footer. Agreement template body now includes "Please find the personalized agreement attached to this email" line above the existing `agreementLink` button. The single-send agreement route generates and attaches the .docx synchronously and returns 400 if no template uploaded — atomic, no half-sent state. Migration: `20260415000000_add_email_signature_and_agreement_template`. New deps: `docxtemplater@3.68.4`, `pizzip@3.2.0`. Files: `src/lib/speaker-agreement.ts` (new), `src/app/api/events/[eventId]/speaker-agreement-template/route.ts` (new), `src/components/events/speaker-agreement-template-card.tsx` (new), `src/app/api/profile/route.ts` (new), `src/app/(dashboard)/profile/page.tsx` (extended with signature card), `src/app/api/events/[eventId]/speakers/[speakerId]/email/route.ts`, `src/lib/bulk-email.ts`, `src/app/api/events/[eventId]/emails/bulk/route.ts`, `src/app/api/cron/scheduled-emails/route.ts`, `src/lib/email.ts`, `src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/settings/page.tsx`, `src/app/e/[slug]/agenda/page.tsx`, `src/app/e/[slug]/session/[sessionId]/page.tsx`, `src/components/public/speakers-agenda-preview.tsx`, `src/app/api/public/events/[slug]/agenda/route.ts`, `src/app/api/public/events/[slug]/sessions/[sessionId]/detail/route.ts`. No new tests yet — verification is manual (upload template, send single + bulk + scheduled agreement, confirm per-recipient .docx attachment with merged values).
- **Abstracts flow audit fixes (April 2026)** — End-to-end audit surfaced and fixed four issues. **(1)** Regression from the prior public-registration tightening: a second public form at `/e/[slug]/submitAbstract` (distinct from the canonical `/e/[slug]/abstract/register`) still used the old permissive schema and broke every submission with 400 after the server schema was tightened. Brought it to parity — added `TitleSelect`/`RoleSelect`/`customSpecialty`, flipped org/jobTitle/phone/city/country to required, added the `customSpecialty`-when-"Others" `.refine()`, updated `STEP_FIELDS.details`, wired up the POST payload. **(2)** IDOR: `GET /api/events/[eventId]/abstracts/[abstractId]` did not enforce the SUBMITTER ownership check the PUT handler already had. A submitter with a speaker record in an event could fetch any abstract ID in that event including reviewNotes/reviewScore. GET now returns 404 (not 403 — avoids existence leak) when `session.user.role === "SUBMITTER"` and `abstract.speaker?.userId !== session.user.id`. **(3)** Agent tool gap: `update_abstract_status` in `src/lib/agent/event-tools.ts` updated status + reviewedAt but never sent the `abstract-status-update` email, never wrote an audit log, and never called `notifyEventAdmins()` — so organizers using the agent ("accept all abstracts from track X") were invisible to speakers. **(4)** XSS/phishing risk: `reviewNotes` was interpolated into the speaker email HTML without escaping; a reviewer could inject `<a href="https://evil">click</a>`. Extracted the dashboard PUT handler's ~45-line notification block into a new shared helper `src/lib/abstract-notifications.ts` (`notifyAbstractStatusChange({ eventId, eventName, eventSlug, abstractId, abstractTitle, previousStatus, newStatus, reviewNotes, reviewScore, speaker, feedbackOnly? })`) that owns: branded speaker email with `escapeHtml()`-sanitized reviewNotes, admin notification via `notifyEventAdmins`, `feedbackOnly` branch for the "notes/score changed without status transition" case. Both the dashboard PUT route and the agent tool call the helper — identical side effects from both entry points. Agent tool also now writes an audit log row with `changes.source: "agent"` so agent-initiated reviews show up in the audit trail. No schema changes. Files: `src/lib/abstract-notifications.ts` (new), `src/app/api/events/[eventId]/abstracts/[abstractId]/route.ts`, `src/lib/agent/event-tools.ts`, `src/app/e/[slug]/submitAbstract/page.tsx`. Deferred to a future pass: pagination cap on `GET /api/events/[eventId]/abstracts` list (AI agent's `list_abstracts` already caps at 200; dashboard-facing API doesn't).
- **Public registration required fields (April 2026)** — Tightened client + server Zod schemas on the three public entry points (`/e/[slug]/register/[category]`, `/e/[slug]/abstract/register`, `/e/[slug]/complete-registration`) so public registrants must supply `jobTitle`, `organization`, `city`, and `phone` in addition to the already-required `title`/`firstName`/`lastName`/`email`/`country`/`specialty`/`role`. Added a `.refine()` on all three schemas making `customSpecialty` required when `specialty === "Others"`. The admin `createRegistrationSchema`, CSV import (no Zod), and registrant self-service PUT intentionally keep their permissive rules — public forms use separate schemas so the change has zero blast radius on admin/bulk flows. The completion form also gained editable `RoleSelect` + `SpecialtySelect` fields (previously only read-only-if-pre-filled, leaving no way to supply them when CSV lacked them). Fixed pre-existing bugs in the submitter route where `customSpecialty` was validated but never persisted to `Speaker` / `Contact`, and in the completion route where `sendRegistrationConfirmation` and `syncToContact` used stale `attendee.*` snapshots instead of the newly-submitted values. All labels got red `*` asterisks. Files touched: `src/app/e/[slug]/register/[category]/page.tsx`, `src/app/api/public/events/[slug]/register/route.ts`, `src/app/e/[slug]/abstract/register/page.tsx`, `src/app/api/public/events/[slug]/submitter/route.ts`, `src/app/e/[slug]/complete-registration/page.tsx`, `src/app/api/public/events/[slug]/complete-registration/route.ts`. No schema migration.
- **Public session page rebuild: in-page Zoom embed + tabs + sponsors (April 2026)** — The public session page at `/e/[slug]/session/[sessionId]` was rebuilt into a sticky-CTA + 3-tab layout that keeps attendees on our domain. **Three parts.** **(A) Sponsors data layer** — new `SponsorEntry[]` stored on `Event.settings.sponsors` JSON (no Prisma table, six tiers: platinum/gold/silver/bronze/partner/exhibitor), `readSponsors(settings)` helper in `src/lib/webinar.ts`, `GET/PUT /api/events/[eventId]/sponsors` route (Zod-validated with URL scheme whitelisting — `logoUrl` accepts `http(s)://` or `/`, `websiteUrl` requires absolute `http(s)://`, rejects `javascript:`/`data:`), server reassigns `sortOrder` from array index so client reorder history doesn't matter. Admin editor at `/events/[id]/sponsors` with draft-based editing, add/edit dialog (logo upload via `PhotoUpload`), up/down arrows for reorder, Save/Discard gated on `isDirty`. **(B) Zoom SDK v6 Component View embed** — upgraded `@zoom/meetingsdk` from `^5.1.4` to `^6.0.0`. New `ZoomWebEmbed` component at `src/components/zoom/zoom-web-embed.tsx` dynamic-imports `@zoom/meetingsdk/embedded` (the UMD Component View entry, not the React-coupled Client View). The `/embedded` entry dynamic-imports the UMD Component View. **[⚠️ CORRECTED June 23 2026 — see the "Zoom embed React-19 crash fixed via CDN loader" entry above: this claim that the UMD "ships its own React 18 internally, isolated from React 19" is FALSE for v6.0.0; the UMD externalizes React and crashes on `ReactCurrentOwner` under React 19. The embed now loads the SDK + React 18 from Zoom's CDN. The original (wrong) text follows as historical record.]** The `/embedded` entry ships its own React 18 + ReactDOM + Redux internally but they live inside the UMD closure and never touch our React 19 fiber tree — that's why Component View works where Client View doesn't (the earlier memory note was correct about Client View but not the embedded entry). Lifecycle: `createClient → init → client.on("connection-change") → join → leaveMeeting → destroyClient`. **Three race guards**: (1) module-level `pendingDestroy: Promise<void> | null` serializes destroy-then-mount across React 19 StrictMode double-invoke; (2) `connection-change` subscription with `state === "Closed"` fires `onLeave()` so when the user clicks Zoom's in-meeting Leave button the parent unmounts cleanly (no black box); (3) `onLeave` stored in a ref so the mount-once effect always reads the latest parent callback without re-mounting. The iframe fallback at `src/components/zoom/zoom-embed.tsx` is preserved but NOT imported by default. **(C) Public session page refactor** — deleted the old right sidebar and replaced the page with: event banner + back link, session title/metadata, **sticky CTA card** (`position: sticky; top: 0; z-10` with gradient-blur background) that shows context-aware action (`Join Webinar` live/upcoming, `Watch Replay` ended+recording, "session ended" muted banner, "joinable at X" for upcoming). **Three tabs**: Live Video (HLS `LivePlayer` + `ZoomWebEmbed` that mounts only when the user clicks Join → keeps the ~3 MB SDK bundle off first paint + the ~50 MB of WASM/AV assets off users who just want to read details), Session Details (description + numbered topics with per-topic speakers + speakers grid with bios — topics and bios are new in the public detail API), Sponsors (grouped by tier, clickable cards with logo + name + optional description). `/api/public/events/[slug]/sessions/[sessionId]/detail` route now returns `session.topics[]` with `TopicSpeaker` join, `session.speakers[].bio`, and `sponsors[]` from the new settings field. Signature generation unchanged: `generateZoomSignatureForOrg()` already returned the shape Component View's `join()` expects; we just weren't consuming it. Memory file updated. No schema migration. Files: `src/lib/webinar.ts` (sponsor types + `readSponsors`), `src/app/api/events/[eventId]/sponsors/route.ts` (new), `src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/sponsors/page.tsx` (new), `src/components/zoom/zoom-web-embed.tsx` (new), `src/app/api/public/events/[slug]/sessions/[sessionId]/detail/route.ts` (extended), `src/app/e/[slug]/session/[sessionId]/page.tsx` (refactored), `src/components/layout/sidebar.tsx` (Sponsors link), `src/hooks/use-api.ts` (`useSponsors`, `useUpdateSponsors`). Docs at `docs/WEBINAR_EVENTS.md` / `.html`.
- **Webinar Console UX refresh (April 2026)** — Console at `/events/[eventId]/webinar` reorganized from a 10-card vertical stack (~3000px scroll) into a workflow-aware layout: (1) **Sticky status bar** (`WebinarStatusBar`) always visible above the fold — color-coded by status (blue/red-pulsing/gray), inline join URL + copy + passcode badge, context-aware primary action (`Start as Host` when Scheduled/Live, `Watch Replay` when Ended with recording ready, `Refetch recording` when Ended without recording); collapses to "Configure Zoom" banner when `!hasZoom`. (2) **Tabs: Setup / Analytics / Settings** — default tab is status-driven (Scheduled/Live → Setup, Ended → Analytics); Setup groups Overview + Panelists + Email Sequence, Analytics groups Recording + Attendance + Polls + Q&A, Settings holds the config form. (3) **`OverviewCard`** merges the old Anchor Session + Zoom Meeting cards into one. (4) **`GlobalRefreshButton`** next to Re-run provisioner — parallel-fires recording + attendance + engagement syncs via `Promise.allSettled` with a single summary toast; disabled until session ends. (5) **`CardLoading` + `CardEmpty`** primitives replace ad-hoc loading/empty markup across all 6+ cards for consistent scanning. **Import from Speakers** (new `POST /api/events/[eventId]/webinar/panelists/sync-speakers`): one-click pulls all anchor-session speakers with emails, parallel-fetches existing Zoom panelists, dedups by lowercased email (no 409 Conflict on re-import), batches via `addWebinarPanelists`. Response surfaces `skippedAlreadyPanelist` + `skippedNoEmail` counts. Shared 30/hr rate limit bucket with single-add. Panelists route now `export`s `resolveAnchorZoomMeeting()` so the sibling sync-speakers route reuses the 4-step precondition lookup (event access → anchor session → zoom meeting → webinar meetingType). **Optimistic UI** on panelist add/remove: `useAddWebinarPanelist.onMutate` inserts a row with id prefixed `optimistic:` (exported `OPTIMISTIC_PANELIST_PREFIX`), `onError` rolls back to previous query data, `onSettled` invalidates for the canonical refetch. PanelistsCard detects the prefix and renders rows greyed out + italic + spinner + disabled remove. The add form clears immediately on submit but restores its values on error so the user doesn't retype. No schema changes. Hook: `useSyncSpeakersToPanelists`.

- **Webinar events as first-class (April 2026, Phases 1–6)** — `eventType === 'WEBINAR'` now auto-provisions a ready-to-join webinar end-to-end. Creating a WEBINAR event triggers `provisionWebinar()` (fire-and-forget from `POST /api/events`) which creates an anchor `EventSession`, calls `createZoomWebinar()` if the org has Zoom configured, persists a `settings.webinar` JSON block, and enqueues a 5-phase email sequence (`webinar-confirmation` immediate + `reminder-24h`, `reminder-1h`, `live-now`, `thank-you` via existing `ScheduledEmail` cron). Sidebar is filtered via `webinarModuleFilter()` in `src/lib/webinar.ts` to hide Accommodation/Check-In/Promo Codes/Abstracts/Reviewers for webinar events and surface a new **Webinar Console** at `/events/[eventId]/webinar` with stacked cards: Overview (anchor session + Zoom join URL), Recording, Attendance, Panelists, Polls, Q&A, Email Sequence, Webinar Settings — now wrapped in Setup/Analytics/Settings tabs (see "Webinar Console UX refresh" bullet above). Public register route branches on `eventType` — webinar registrations get `sendWebinarConfirmationForRegistration()` (immediate direct send, no cron latency) instead of the generic `sendRegistrationConfirmation`. After the webinar ends, two cron workers poll Zoom: **`/api/cron/webinar-recordings`** (every 5 min) fetches cloud recording via `GET /meetings/{id}/recordings` and persists `recordingUrl`/`recordingPassword`/`recordingStatus` on `ZoomMeeting` (states: `NOT_REQUESTED`→`PENDING`→`AVAILABLE`, flips to `EXPIRED` after 7 days); **`/api/cron/webinar-attendance`** (every 10 min) fetches the participant report via `GET /report/webinars/{id}/participants` with `next_page_token` pagination and upserts per-segment rows into new `ZoomAttendance` table (unique key `(zoomMeetingId, zoomParticipantId, joinTime)` preserves rejoin history; registrationId best-effort matched via case-insensitive email lookup); attendance tick also chains `syncWebinarEngagement()` for polls + Q&A from `/report/webinars/{id}/polls` and `/report/webinars/{id}/qa` into new `WebinarPoll` + `WebinarPollResponse` + `WebinarQuestion` tables. Attendance re-sync is restricted to 24h post-end to avoid wasting Zoom API calls on old webinars. Public session page shows emerald "Watch Replay" card (replacing Join CTA) when recording is `AVAILABLE`, amber "Recording processing" spinner when `PENDING`. Thank-you email's `{{recordingBlock}}` renders real Watch Replay button when available. Webinar Console `AttendanceCard` shows KPIs (registered/attended/rate/avg watch time/peak concurrent computed via edge-event sweep) + attendee table with CSV export (`?export=csv`). Polls card renders per-poll horizontal bar-chart distributions; Q&A card is a searchable list with answer blocks. Polls sync uses a DB transaction (nullable composite unique on `WebinarPoll.zoomPollId` doesn't enforce NULL in Postgres, so two concurrent syncs could otherwise create duplicate logical polls); Q&A rows with missing `create_time` are skipped and logged to avoid uniqueness collisions from `Date.now()` fallback. Panelist management is accessible from the Webinar Console (see UX refresh bullet above); the existing session-level `/sessions/[sessionId]/zoom/panelists` route is reused in places. All cron workers: Bearer `CRON_SECRET`, serial processing with 500ms delay between rows (batches >3) to respect Zoom's 30 req/s rate limit, per-row try/catch so one bad row can't kill the tick, structured logging with `durationMs` on every state transition. Bulk-email also gained a sender-branding fix: `executeBulkEmail` now fetches `emailFromAddress`/`emailFromName`/`emailHeaderImage`/`emailFooterHtml` so `brandingFrom()` resolves to the per-event sender instead of provider defaults. Migration files: `20260413000000_add_webinar_recording_fields`, `20260413010000_add_zoom_attendance`, `20260414000000_add_webinar_engagement`. EC2 crontab additions: `*/5 * * * *` for webinar-recordings, `*/10 * * * *` for webinar-attendance (chains engagement). Decouplability: all code lives under `src/lib/webinar*`, `src/app/api/events/[eventId]/webinar/*`, `src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/webinar/*`, `src/app/api/cron/webinar-*`, `src/lib/zoom/{recordings,reports,polls-qa}.ts` — one-way imports from core. Full docs at `docs/WEBINAR_EVENTS.md` / `.html`.
- **Scheduled communications** — Organizers can queue bulk emails for future delivery from `/events/[eventId]/communications`. `BulkEmailDialog` has a "Send now / Schedule for later" toggle with a datetime picker (min lead time = 5 minutes); scheduled rows are stored in the new `ScheduledEmail` model with `recipientType + filters` (recipients are re-evaluated dynamically when the cron fires, so a "remind unpaid" send naturally excludes anyone who paid in the meantime). Cron worker at `/api/cron/scheduled-emails` (Bearer `CRON_SECRET`, accepts GET/POST) processes up to 10 due rows per tick using an atomic `PENDING → PROCESSING` claim to prevent double-send. Shared `executeBulkEmail()` helper in `src/lib/bulk-email.ts` is reused by both the immediate-send route (`/api/events/[eventId]/emails/bulk`) and the cron worker. Management UI: `ScheduledEmailsList` table at the bottom of the Communications page lets organizers list/edit/cancel pending rows and retry failed rows; status badges (PENDING/PROCESSING/SENT/FAILED/CANCELLED) with success/failure counts shown via tooltip. Schedule create/edit/cancel/retry routes all use `denyReviewer()`; schedule create shares the existing 20/hr/event rate limit bucket so users can't bypass it. EC2 crontab entry: `* * * * * curl -s -X POST -H "Authorization: Bearer $CRON_SECRET" https://events.meetingmindsgroup.com/api/cron/scheduled-emails`. Migration: `20260410000000_add_scheduled_emails`.
- **Email template WYSIWYG editor and branding** - Replaced raw HTML textarea with Tiptap v2 WYSIWYG editor (`src/components/ui/tiptap-editor.tsx`) with toolbar (bold, italic, underline, headings, lists, alignment, link, image, color, undo/redo) and source toggle; email preview opens in popup dialog (`src/components/email-preview-dialog.tsx`) with desktop (600px) / mobile (375px) toggle; added `emailHeaderImage` and `emailFooterHtml` fields to Event model for consistent email branding; `wrapWithBranding()` in `src/lib/email.ts` wraps all outgoing emails with table-based header image + footer layout; `inlineCss()` uses `juice` for email-client-safe inline styles; `renderAndWrap()` combines variable substitution + branding + CSS inlining; `stripDocumentWrapper()` in `src/lib/email-utils.ts` (client-safe) extracts body from legacy full-document templates; all 6+ email send routes updated to use `renderAndWrap()`; templates now stored as body fragments (no DOCTYPE/html/body), branding applied at render time; email template list inlined directly in Settings → Email Templates tab (no extra "Manage" click); Tiptap lazy-loaded with `next/dynamic` to avoid bloating other pages; **note:** Tiptap v2 is used (not v3) because v3 ships source-only without compiled dist
- **Database-backed logging for Vercel** - `SystemLog` Prisma model stores log entries in PostgreSQL; Pino writes to a custom `Writable` stream that buffers and batch-inserts; `/api/logs` route supports `source=database` (default on Vercel); log viewer UI at `/logs` with database/file/docker source selector; comprehensive logging coverage across all API routes, middleware, auth, uploads, and server pages
- **EventsAir import error handling** - Import dialog now shows error state UI with actual error message, Retry button, and Settings link; `listEvents()` throws on null API response; `useEventsAirEvents` hook uses `retry: false`; events API route returns actual error details in 500 response
- **Title and Registration Type fields** - Added `Title` enum (MR, MS, MRS, DR, PROF, OTHER) and `registrationType String?` to Attendee, Speaker, and Contact models; `TitleSelect` dropdown component; `RegistrationTypeSelect` component (fetches TicketType names with event context, falls back to text input); shared `titleEnum` Zod schema in `src/lib/schemas.ts`; `formatPersonName()` and `getTitleLabel()` helpers in utils; updated all 9+ API routes, all person forms, and all display views to show title prefix with names; CSV export includes title and registrationType columns
- **Sentry client instrumentation** - Replaced root-level `sentry.client.config.ts` with `src/instrumentation-client.ts` (Next.js 15+ convention); DSN from `NEXT_PUBLIC_SENTRY_DSN` env var with replay integration (10% session sample, 100% on error)
- **Uploaded photo serving** - Next.js `output: "standalone"` does not serve `public/` directory files automatically; added `src/app/uploads/[...path]/route.ts` catch-all handler that reads from `public/uploads/` and streams files with correct `Content-Type` and long-lived `Cache-Control` headers; includes path-traversal protection
- **Docker deploy fix** - Replaced `docker compose up -d --no-deps` with `docker compose down --remove-orphans && docker compose up -d` in `.github/workflows/deploy.yml` to prevent container naming conflicts from prior failed deployments
- **Specialty field on Abstract** - Added `specialty` to abstract create/edit Zod schemas, DB writes, and UI (SpecialtySelect in submit and edit dialogs); SUBMITTER role can set specialty on own abstracts
- **Tag input component** - `TagInput` chip-based multi-tag input replacing comma-string inputs; Enter or comma adds a tag, × removes individual chips, Backspace on empty removes last tag; used in registration forms, registration detail edit panel, and contacts form; contacts form state changed from string to string[]
- **Photo upload system** - File upload functionality for attendee/speaker/contact photos with validation (max 500KB, JPEG/PNG/WebP formats); `PhotoUpload` component with preview and progress indicator; stored in `/public/uploads/photos/YYYY/MM/` with UUID-based filenames; replaces URL-based photo fields across all forms; **note:** photo Zod schemas use `z.string().optional()` (not `.url()`) since upload returns relative paths like `/uploads/photos/...`
- **City and country fields** - Added to Attendee, Speaker, and Contact models; `CountrySelect` component with searchable dropdown (ISO 3166-1 standard, 249 countries); integrated into registration, speaker, and contact forms with display in list views and detail sheets
- **Event classification fields** - Added `eventType` (enum: CONFERENCE/WEBINAR/HYBRID), `tag`, and `specialty` fields to Event model; integrated into event creation and settings forms for better event categorization
- **Authenticated abstract submission (SUBMITTER role)** - Speakers create an account at `/e/[slug]/register`, then log in to submit/edit abstracts via dashboard; SUBMITTER role mirrors REVIEWER pattern (org-independent, abstracts-only access, scoped by `Speaker.userId`)
- **Submitter registration** - Public form at `/e/[slug]/register` creates User (role=SUBMITTER) + Speaker record linked to event (including specialty field); redirects to login on success; `/e/[slug]` server-redirects to `/e/[slug]/register`
- **Abstract submission URL widget** - Abstracts page shows a copyable URL card (visible to organizers/admins only) with the public submission link (`/e/[slug]/register`) and a short description to share with speakers
- **Abstract status notification emails** - Automatic email to speaker on status change (UNDER_REVIEW, ACCEPTED, REJECTED, REVISION_REQUESTED) with status-specific messaging, reviewer notes, and login link
- **Org-independent reviewers** - Reviewers decoupled from organizations (`User.organizationId = null`); one reviewer can review across multiple orgs; scoped only by `event.settings.reviewerUserIds`
- **Reviewers module** - Per-event reviewer management page with dual add mode (from speakers or by email); auto-invitation; API routes for add/remove; React Query hooks
- **Restricted role access hardening** - 3-layer RBAC enforcement (API guards on 29+ handlers, middleware redirects, UI write-action hiding) restricting REVIEWER and SUBMITTER to abstracts-only
- **Event scoping for reviewers** - `buildEventAccessWhere` removes org filter for reviewers; reviewers see only assigned events across all orgs
- **Server page query optimization** - Parallelized `params`/`auth()`/DB queries on speakers and event detail pages; switched to Prisma `select` for minimal data transfer
- **Composite database indexes** - Added `[eventId, status]` and `[eventId, ticketTypeId]` on Registration for faster filtered queries
- **Middleware scope narrowing** - Matcher targets only dashboard routes; reviewers redirected from non-abstract event routes
- **Barcode import system** - CSV import route (`/api/events/[eventId]/import/barcodes`) maps DTCM barcodes to registrations by ID or email; `barcode` field on Registration (`@unique`); import dialog UI with results summary
- **Badge PDF generation** - Server-side PDF generation with `pdfkit` + `bwip-js` (Code128 barcodes); one badge per A4 page, horizontally centered; badge layout: name, country, barcode, badge type (large), registration number (italic); all black text, no branding; `badgeVerticalOffset` on Event for print positioning; prints via `window.print()` (not download)
- **Check-in scanner page** - Mobile-optimized page at `/events/[eventId]/check-in`; camera mode via `html5-qrcode`; manual/hardware scanner mode with auto-focused input; check-in API searches both `qrCode` and `barcode` fields; live attendance counter, recent scans log, Web Audio API sound feedback, 2s debounce
- **API query optimization (March 2026)** - `select: { id: true }` on event existence checks across 25+ route files; parallelized independent queries in speaker/abstract detail routes; reduced over-fetching in registration list
- **WYSIWYG footer editor** - Event footer HTML now edited via TiptapEditor in settings (replaced textarea)
- **Registration detail edit** - Slide-out panel with full CRUD for registration details; registration type editable via dropdown
- **Import speakers from registrations** - Replaced "Import from Contacts" on the speakers page with "Import from Registrations"; dialog (`src/components/speakers/import-registrations-dialog.tsx`) lists the event's own registrations (excluding cancelled) with search, multi-select, name/email/org/type/status columns; API route (`src/app/api/events/[eventId]/speakers/import-registrations/route.ts`) maps attendee data to speaker records, deduplicates by email, skips existing speakers; React Query hook `useImportRegistrationsToSpeakers` in `use-api.ts`
- **Stripe payment integration** - Stripe Checkout for paid event registrations; checkout route at `/api/public/events/[slug]/checkout` creates Stripe sessions with rate limiting (3/60s per IP); webhook at `/api/webhooks/stripe` handles `checkout.session.completed` with signature verification, idempotent processing (interactive transaction to prevent duplicate Payment records), receipt URL fetching, and payment confirmation email; payment status polling endpoint at `/api/public/events/[slug]/payment-status/[registrationId]`; confirmation page (`/e/[slug]/confirmation`) shows Pay Now button for paid tickets, polls for webhook completion, displays payment status from server (not URL params); `src/lib/stripe.ts` provides lazy-init Stripe SDK singleton and zero-decimal currency helpers (`isZeroDecimalCurrency`, `toStripeAmount`, `fromStripeAmount`) for correct handling of JPY, KRW, etc.; `Payment` model stores amount, currency, stripePaymentId, receiptUrl; env vars: `STRIPE_SECRET_KEY`, `STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_STRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY`
- **React Query caching** for instant page navigation (registration types, registrations, schedule, abstracts, reviewers)
- Public event registration at `/e/[slug]` (no auth required)
- User invitation system with email tokens
- Cerulean Blue theme with gradients
- Bulk email sending via Brevo
- Session calendar view
- File-based logging (`logs/app.log`, `logs/error.log`)
- **REGISTRANT role and self-service portal** - New org-independent role for event attendees with account creation during public registration (email + password); `/my-registration` dashboard page shows all user's registrations with event headers, payment status (confirmed/complimentary/pay now), inline edit of attendee fields; self-edit API at `/api/registrant/registrations` with ownership verification; REGISTRANT redirected to portal from all dashboard routes (middleware); sidebar hidden, header shows "Registration Portal"
- **2-step public registration form** - Step 1: email + password (account creation) with organizer-customizable welcome HTML content; Step 2: personal details + category selection + terms & conditions; `registrationWelcomeHtml` and `registrationTermsHtml` fields on Event model, both editable via TiptapEditor on registration types settings page; default terms auto-seeded on event creation. All public entry points (main register, abstract submitter register, token-based complete-registration) enforce a strict required-field set: `title`, `firstName`, `lastName`, `jobTitle`, `organization`, `city`, `phone`, `country`, `email`, `role`, `specialty`, and `customSpecialty` when `specialty === "Others"`. Admin dashboard, CSV import, and registrant self-service schemas are **not** affected — they use separate Zod schemas and remain permissive.
- **Bulk registration type update** - PATCH at `/api/events/[eventId]/registrations/bulk-type`; bulk select registrations → change type via dialog; atomically adjusts soldCounts (decrement old types, increment new) and syncs `attendee.registrationType`; "Change Type" button in bulk selection toolbar on registrations page
- **Single source of truth for registration type** - `ticketTypeId` is the canonical reference for registration type; `attendee.registrationType` text field auto-synced from `ticketType.name` on create and type change; removed `registrationType` from registration edit forms and Zod schemas; CSV export uses `ticketType.name`; speakers/contacts retain `registrationType` as independent field (no `ticketTypeId` on those models)
- **Event-scoped login** - `/e/[slug]/login` page with event branding (banner, name, dates); `redirect` param routes to registration portal or abstracts after login; "Don't have an account?" links to register/abstract forms; reviewer invitation emails link to event-scoped login after accepting invitation
- **Event-scoped my-registration** - `/e/[slug]/my-registration` shows registration for specific event with event branding; global `/my-registration` shows all events; registration form sign-in links to event-scoped portal
- **PresentationType on abstracts** - `PresentationType` enum (ORAL/POSTER/VIDEO/WORKSHOP) added to Abstract model; dropdown in submit/edit dialogs and full-page forms (options + status colours centralized in `src/app/(dashboard)/events/[eventId]/abstracts/abstract-enums.ts`); badge displayed on abstract cards
- **Full-page abstract submission** - Submitters use `/events/[eventId]/abstracts/new` (2-column layout: content + sidebar) instead of dialog; edit at `/events/[eventId]/abstracts/[id]/edit` with reviewer feedback display, draft/submit actions; plain Textarea for content (not WYSIWYG — cleaner for academic text)
- **Abstract register page** - `/e/[slug]/abstract/register` with 2-step flow (account → details), separate `abstractWelcomeHtml` field; REGISTRANT→SUBMITTER role upgrade supported
- **Reviewer portal improvements** - Reviewers can now review, score (0-100), accept/reject abstracts; review dialog and buttons enabled for REVIEWER role; header permissions corrected; event list links go directly to `/abstracts`
- **PDF quote/proforma** - Generated with pdfkit; includes event details, line items, tax calculation (taxRate + taxLabel), bank transfer details, branded layout; attached to confirmation email for paid registrations; downloadable from registrant portal and admin detail sheet
- **Tax & payment** - `taxRate` (Decimal), `taxLabel`, `bankDetails` on Event model; tax config in Settings → Registration tab; registration form shows price + VAT breakdown; checkout sends base + tax as separate Stripe line items; Stripe `automatic_tax` removed; PDF quote, confirmation page, and registrant portals all show tax breakdown
- **Abstract notification improvements** - Email sent when reviewer adds notes/score without status change (not just on status change); login link in notification uses event-scoped URL
- **Bulk email for abstract submitters** - Select abstracts → send email; email types: Abstract Accepted, Rejected, Revision Requested, Submission Reminder, Custom; `abstract-reminder` template added to defaults; deduplicates by speaker email
- **Smart /e/[slug]/register redirect** - Auto-redirects to first active tier (Early Bird → Standard → Onsite); skips Presenter (shared separately by organizer); shows "Registration Closed" if no active tiers
- **Settings: branding split** - Branding (banner + footer) and Email Branding (header image + footer) separated into distinct tabs
- **UI polish** - Public form widths increased to `max-w-5xl`; font sizes increased to 16px base; all select dropdowns use `w-full`; Tiptap source mode formats HTML with indentation; Tailwind safelist for DB-stored HTML classes; footer/welcome/terms rendered with `prose` + `[&>*]:mb-4`; sheet width fix (removed hardcoded 540px)
- **SendGrid integration** - Added `@sendgrid/mail` as alternative email provider to Brevo; auto-selected via `SENDGRID_API_KEY` env var; both providers coexist in `src/lib/email.ts` with a unified `sendEmail()` interface; set `EMAIL_PROVIDER` to force a specific provider or omit to auto-detect from available API keys
- **Attendee cleanup on registration delete** - Deleting a registration now also deletes its attendee record; public registration route reuses orphaned attendees (same email, no active registrations) instead of creating duplicates; P2002 unique constraint error handled gracefully
- **COMPLIMENTARY payment status** - Added `COMPLIMENTARY` to `PaymentStatus` enum; admins can set any registration as complimentary from the detail sheet; complimentary registrations can check in without payment, are included in badge generation, and show "no payment required" in registrant portal; cyan badge color
- **Detail sheet redesign (registration, contact, speaker)** - Gradient header with photo (112px, editable on hover with pencil overlay and "Remove" link below), 2-column info grid in view mode, status badges, action buttons in header; `SheetDescription` uses `asChild` + `<span>` to avoid `<p>` > `<div>` hydration errors; 700px sheet width, 32px right padding
- **Speaker detail page** - Full page (not sheet) with gradient header, photo upload, 2-column info grid, inline edit, sessions/abstracts lists, social links, email dialog (invitation/agreement/custom); speakers list uses table layout (matching registrations)
- **Session topics system** - `SessionTopic` model for topics within sessions (title, sortOrder, duration, optional abstract); `TopicSpeaker` join table for per-topic speakers; `SessionRole` enum (SPEAKER, MODERATOR, CHAIRPERSON, PANELIST) replaces free-text role on `SessionSpeaker`; session form has "Session Roles" section (role + speaker dropdowns) and "Topics" section (repeatable sub-form with title, duration, speaker checkboxes); topics are optional — sessions work with just session-level roles; legacy `speakerIds` array still supported
- **Session date validation** - Session start/end times must fall within event dates; validated in both POST and PUT; datetime-local inputs have `min`/`max` set to event dates; "Add Session" pre-fills with current calendar date (9:00–10:00)
- **Badge print (not download)** - Badge button opens PDF in new browser tab and triggers `window.print()` instead of downloading; one badge per page, horizontally centered; `badgeVerticalOffset` field on Event model for organizer-adjustable vertical positioning (Settings → Registration tab); badge layout: name, country, barcode, badge type, registration number — all black text, no branding/colors
- **pdfkit Turbopack fix** - Added `pdfkit` to `serverExternalPackages` in next.config.ts to preserve `__dirname` for Helvetica.afm font resolution; `bwip-js` barcode rendering uses async `toBuffer()` with pre-rendered buffers (not `toBufferSync`)
- **Email template cleanup** - Removed gradient header divs from default email templates; `wrapWithBranding()` body cell has `padding: 24px 30px`; registration confirmation template uses clean text header; `titleEnum` accepts empty string `""` and transforms to `undefined`
- **Tiptap layout blocks** - Layout dropdown in editor toolbar: 2-column (50/50), 3-column, sidebar+main (30/70), content box (gray), info box (blue), highlight box (amber), CTA button, divider, spacer; all use inline styles (email-safe)
- **Photo delete fix** - Photo Zod schemas accept `.nullable()` on speaker and registration update routes; `photo: editData.photo ?? null` in save logic (not `|| undefined`); validation failure logging added (`apiLogger.warn`) on speaker and registration update routes
- **Signup notifications** - `SIGNUP` notification type; admins notified when: new registrant account created, new submitter account created, team member accepts invitation
- **Log viewer enhancements** - "Download All" button exports all logs; "Clear Logs" button (database source only) deletes logs by timeframe with confirmation; DELETE endpoint on `/api/logs`
- **Global settings redesign** - Gradient header banner; stats cards with colored left borders and icon badges; section cards with colored icon badges (cerulean, violet, emerald, sky, amber)
- **Organization primary color** - `primaryColor` field on Organization model; dynamic theme provider applies org color via CSS variables; auth session includes primaryColor
- **Title enum sorted alphabetically** - DR, MR, MRS, MS, PROF in schema, Zod, UI dropdown, and display labels
- **State and zip code fields** - Added `state` and `zipCode` to Attendee, Speaker, and Contact models; `billingState` and `billingZipCode` on Registration for invoice purposes; integrated into all person forms, CSV import/export, and contact sync
- **Terms accepted timestamp** - `termsAcceptedAt` (DateTime) on Registration records the moment a registrant accepted T&C; set on both public registration submit and completion form submit
- **Conditional member/student fields** - Registration types containing "member" in the name require `memberId`; types containing "student" require `studentId` and `studentIdExpiry`; enforced client-side and server-side in the completion form and public registration API; info box shown to registrant explaining ID verification at event
- **CSV import → registration completion flow** - Admins upload a CSV (required: email, firstName, lastName; optional: state, zipCode, registrationType, memberId, studentId, etc.) at `/events/[eventId]/registrations` → CSV import dialog; records are created, then "Send Registration Forms" triggers bulk completion emails; completion email contains a 7-day token link to `/e/[slug]/complete-registration?token=...`; public page pre-fills read-only fields (name, email) and collects editable details + optional account creation; API at `GET/POST /api/public/events/[slug]/complete-registration`; rate limited (20 GET / 15 min per IP, 5 POST / 15 min per IP); send-emails route limited to 5 sends / 1 hour per org; one-time-use token deleted after successful submission; `contact-sync.ts` fires after completion
- **Media library** - Organization-level media management; JPEG/PNG/WebP files up to 2MB with magic byte validation; stored in `/uploads/media/{YYYY}/{MM}/`; `MediaFile` Prisma model; API routes at `/api/media` (GET paginated list, POST upload, DELETE by id); usable in TiptapEditor for email template images; `STORAGE_PROVIDER` env var switches between local filesystem and Supabase Storage
- **Contact auto-sync** - `syncToContact()` in `src/lib/contact-sync.ts` upserts attendee/speaker data to Contact store after CSV import, speaker import, and registration completion; appends eventId to contact.eventIds (no duplicates); non-blocking (failures logged, never thrown)
- **Centralized Communications page** - `/events/[eventId]/communications` page consolidates all event email sending in one place (replaces scattered send-email buttons on individual pages)
- **Standalone Content page** - `/events/[eventId]/content` provides dedicated TiptapEditor panels for registration welcome HTML and abstract welcome HTML, outside of settings tabs
- **AI Agent** - `/events/[eventId]/agent` page lets organizers type natural language commands to autonomously manage their event; powered by `@anthropic-ai/sdk` with Anthropic tool-use API in an agentic loop; tools: `list_event_info`, `list_tracks`, `create_track`, `list_speakers`, `create_speaker`, `list_registrations`, `list_sessions`, `create_session`, `list_ticket_types`, `send_bulk_email`; streams progress to browser via SSE (`Content-Type: text/event-stream`); tool executors in `src/lib/agent/event-tools.ts`, system prompt builder in `src/lib/agent/system-prompt.ts`, SSE route at `src/app/api/events/[eventId]/agent/execute/route.ts`; rate limited (20 req/hr per user, 10 bulk emails/hr per event); read-only + create only (no deletes); restricted to ADMIN/ORGANIZER roles; `X-Accel-Buffering: no` header disables nginx buffering for EC2 production
- **Event-scoped media library** - Each event has its own media page at `/events/[eventId]/media`; `MediaFile.eventId` (optional FK) scopes uploads per event; API routes at `/api/events/[eventId]/media` (GET paginated list, POST upload with magic byte validation and 20/hr rate limit, DELETE by id); React Query hooks `useEventMedia`, `useUploadEventMedia`, `useDeleteEventMedia`; drag-and-drop upload zone, image grid with copy URL and delete; sidebar "Media" link under event Tools section
- **Accommodation assignment UI** - "Assign Room" button on Bookings tab of accommodation page opens `AssignAccommodationDialog` (`src/components/accommodation/assign-accommodation-dialog.tsx`); dialog has Registration/Speaker tab toggle, searchable person picker (filters to those without existing accommodation), room type `Select` grouped by hotel with availability counts, date pickers, guest count, special requests; POSTs to existing `/api/events/[eventId]/accommodations`
- **Speaker accommodation support** - `Accommodation.speakerId` (optional `@unique` FK to Speaker) added alongside `registrationId` (now optional); API POST accepts either `registrationId` or `speakerId` (Zod refine ensures at least one); GET/PUT responses include `speaker` select; speakers API (`/api/events/[eventId]/speakers`) now returns `accommodation: { id }` for filtering; booking cards show "Speaker" badge for speaker-linked bookings
- **Accommodation status management** - Booking cards on Bookings tab now have inline status action buttons: PENDING → Confirm/Cancel, CONFIRMED → Check In/Cancel, CHECKED_IN → Check Out, CANCELLED → Reinstate (→ PENDING); calls PUT `/api/events/[eventId]/accommodations/[id]` with `{ status }` and refreshes both bookings and hotel room counts
- **Accommodation API optimization** - GET list uses `select` instead of `include` for attendee (only firstName/lastName/email) and roomType (only name + hotel.name); detail route parallelizes `params + auth()` and `event + accommodation` lookups via `Promise.all`; PUT parallelizes `event + accommodation + body` parsing; audit logs changed from blocking `await` to fire-and-forget `.catch()`; added `apiLogger.warn` on Zod validation failures; added missing `nights <= 0` check on room type change path
